Changelog — Retention & Juice Rework

A phased rework layered on top of v0.9.8: save persistence, Web Audio SFX, achievements, daily challenges, respec, prestige, combo milestones, and a moment-to-moment juice pass. Every change lives in maple_game.html. No new assets, no build step.

Base: v0.9.8 · All changes on main

Save + Web Audio
+143 / −2
Phase 2
Retention hooks
+343 / −12
Phase 3
Juice pass
bundled with Phase 2 commit
Patches
Reset + keybind fix
+28 / −8
Heads-up. An earlier implementation of these phases targeted v0.5.1 and was preserved locally at tag phase-1-2-3-on-v0.5.1. This is the rebuild against the current v0.9.8 codebase, which had moved substantially (new bosses like Gravitos, minimap/taxi, chibi character rewrite).

v0.25.279 Drop-through ghost-drop fix — intent captured at press time

bugBuffered jumps no longer phase through platforms unintentionally

Repro from gameplay audit (#7): jumping over stacked mobs while crouching to peek would occasionally phase through one-tile platforms. Cause: the jump buffer consulted k['arrowdown'] at fire time, not at press time. A fresh mid-air space press (no arrowdown) would buffer for 120 ms; if the player started holding arrowdown before they landed within that window, the buffered jump fired the drop-through branch.

Fix: capture player._jumpBufferDropIntent = !!k['arrowdown'] at the moment Space is pressed, and gate the drop-through branch on that flag. Drop-through now requires ↓ + Space to have been pressed together, matching the input the player actually intended. Normal jump buffering for late-press-into-landing still works exactly as before.

v0.25.278 Boon inventory cap enforced on every acquisition path

bugPowerup choice modal + legacy migration now respect BOON_INVENTORY_CAP

Two related gameplay-audit findings on the boon-inventory cap (25). acquirePowerup already enforced the cap, but two side paths bypassed it:

  • Powerup choice modal (#6) — the card.onclick in showPowerupChoice did its own player.boons.push(inst) without checking the cap. Boss-kill drops could grow the inventory past 25, and the U-panel's bag grid (which assumes the cap holds) would render the 26th boon outside its bounds. Now shows the same "Boon bag full — discard one first" toast and closes the modal cleanly.
  • Legacy migration (#4) — _migrateLegacyPowerups looped over the saved _powerups array unbounded. Low-likelihood since the POWERUPS array is short, but a hand-edited or pre-cap save could break the invariant. Added a break when the cap is reached.

v0.25.277 Charge-release defensive guards (Tower / death / silent-consume)

bugThree audit findings collapsed into one fix on tryStart/ReleaseClassCharge

  • Tower basicOnly windup (#3) — warriors / archers in a Tower run with the basicOnly modifier could still start a charge windup on a non-d skill, only to have castSkill silently drop it on release. Added an early-return in tryStartClassCharge so the windup never begins; the player no longer wastes animation frames + sound on a misfire.
  • Death-state leak (#5) — _tickClassIdentity clears _warCharge when the player drops to 0 HP, but a synchronous keyup can race past it on the same frame. Added a hard guard at the top of tryReleaseClassCharge so the cast no longer deducts MP / sets cooldown on a corpse.
  • Silent-consume feedback (#8) — when a Tower modifier or skill-tree mid-charge change made the skill un-ready, the charge was eaten with no UI feedback. Added a brief "Skill not ready" toast.

v0.25.276 Projectile-sprite lookup hoisted out of the render loop

polish~3,600 closure allocations/sec eliminated from drawProjectiles

Top finding from the perf audit. The skill-id → sprite resolver inside drawProjectiles was an IIFE (immediately-invoked function expression) running per-projectile-per-frame. With 30–60 player projectiles in flight (rapid-fire ranger, mage AoE), that allocated 1,800–3,600 closure objects per second of pure GC churn — for a constant-string branch that didn't depend on per-frame state.

Fix: hoisted the resolver to a module-scope _LX_PROJ_FOR_SKILL lookup table sitting next to LX_PLAYER_PROJ. The render-loop call collapsed from a 14-branch chain inside an IIFE to a single dict lookup: _LX_PROJ_FOR_SKILL[p.skill] || null. Behaviour is identical (same skill→sprite mapping, including the v0.25.209 bolt → mage_orb remap), and the procedural-draw fallback for unknown skill ids still fires when the lookup misses.

v0.25.275 Quickening exploit fix — Sleight excluded from cooldown bypass

bugQuickening no longer refunds Sleight charges (infinite-teleport exploit)

Showstopper from gameplay audit. Quickening's cooldown bypass at the top of castSkill ran before the Sleight charge block, so when a rogue/Phantom's Sleight burned its third charge, the bypass would zero player.skillCooldowns['sleight'] — and the Sleight branch's charges <= 0 → refill 3 path then triggered on the very next press. Net effect: ~12 % chance per cast to refund the entire Sleight cadence and gain three more zips, by far the strongest exploit any rogue/Phantom could uncover.

Fix: sleight joins phantom_cut and nightreaper_mark in the Quickening exclusion list. The 3-charge system stays authoritative on Sleight's cooldown regardless of cdrChance rolls; the two 12 s ultimates remain CDR-immune as before. Other skills still benefit from Quickening normally.

v0.25.274 Sage Mira refund fix — bag-full check before deduction

bugSage Mira no longer eats 5000 Lumens + 12 h cooldown when bag is full

Showstopper from gameplay audit. buyRandomPowerup deducted SAGE_PRICE (5000 Lumens) and set _sageNextAt = Date.now() + SAGE_COOLDOWN_MS before calling acquirePowerup. When the player's boon bag was at BOON_INVENTORY_CAP (25), acquirePowerup bailed with a "Boon bag full" toast — but the side effects had already landed. Player paid in full, got nothing, and was locked out of the Sage for 12 real-time hours.

Fix: pre-check player.boons.length < BOON_INVENTORY_CAP before any deduction. If full, the player gets the same "discard one first (press U)" toast that acquirePowerup would have shown, with no Lumens lost and no cooldown imposed.

v0.25.273 Razor-sharp player edges — direct vector render

polishVectors now rasterise at the final pixel grid (zero resamples)

Three previous attempts (v0.25.266 nearest-neighbour, v0.25.269 3× super-sample, v0.25.271 5× super-sample) all kept the v0.25.176 idle bake-cache and tried to make the bilinear downsample look sharper. Bilinear is slightly soft by definition — every cached blit went through ≥1 resample (chibi 1.19× horizontal, optional 1.5× HiDPI vertical) so the player edges always looked a touch fuzzy compared to the Q-key Character Studio preview, which renders the same vectors directly to its panel.

Fix in v0.25.273: _drawVectorHeroCached now always falls through to _drawVectorHero(sx, sy). The vector pipeline rasterises the body / legs / arms / face directly at the post-chibi, post-HiDPI pixel grid — no offscreen canvas, no resample, no bilinear softening. Now that the v0.25.157 SVG goo filter is gone (replaced by sprite hair / head / eyes / mouth in v0.25.178+), the per-frame cost of _drawVectorHero is dominated by four small drawImage calls plus a handful of Path2D fills — well within budget at 60 FPS on mobile.

The bake function (_lxBakeHeroIdle) and cache map (_LX_HERO_IDLE_BAKE_CACHE) are kept in place so any path that still references them keeps linking, but the player render no longer reads from the cache. Net result: the in-game character now matches the Q-window's razor-sharp edges.

v0.25.272 Cinematic zodiac arena bgs · World Map boss layout fix

featAuthored cinematic backdrops on every zodiac arena

The 12 zodiac boss arenas now ride the four authored bg_v3_cinematic_zodiac_1..4.png hero backdrops instead of the procedural starfield from drawZodiacArena. A new _ZODIAC_BG_CYCLE = ['cosmos', 'zodiacDawn', 'zodiacDusk', 'zodiacSunset'] cycles by sign order, so each of the four backdrops covers three signs across the progression (Aries / Leo / Sagittarius on cosmos, Taurus / Virgo / Capricorn on dawn, etc.). The v0.25.268 drawBackground gate already passes through to the bitmap pick when md.bg is set + loaded — no procedural code needed to change.

bugWorld Map boss layout — Singularity beside Aetherion, Queen's Hollow lifted

The level-sorted slot rotation in _wmComputePositions only had three explicit corner slots, so the 4th boss arena (The Singularity, gravitosArena) was collapsing onto slot 0 and stacking on top of Gelwater Grotto at the bottom-left. Replaced the rotation with an explicit per-id override map:

  • Gelwater Grotto (slimeCave) — bottom-left, unchanged
  • Queen's Hollow (boss) — bottom-right, lifted from y = H − 40 to y = H − 75 (a few dozen pixels up, as requested) so the node + label clears the legend bar
  • Aetherion's Sanctum (sanctum) — top-left, unchanged
  • The Singularity (gravitosArena) — pinned at (140, 40) directly to the right of Aetherion, so the two endgame fights read as a coupled pair on the W map

Any future boss arena that lacks an override entry falls through to the original 3-slot rotation, so the legacy behaviour is preserved.

v0.25.271 Crisper player render · Sage Mira taller

polishCrisper in-game character render

Pushed the cached idle bake from 3× → 5× super-sample (_LX_HERO_BAKE_SUPER). The bake canvas is now 500×500 physical pixels for a 100×100 logical footprint, so the source-to-destination ratio comfortably exceeds the combined HiDPI canvas backing buffer (1.5× DPR on desktop) plus the 1.19× chibi horizontal scale. The browser's imageSmoothingQuality = 'high' downsample then has plenty of source pixels to anti-alias from, eliminating the residual softness from v0.25.269's 3× setting. Memory ≈ 1 MB per cached look (×6–12 active looks ≈ 12 MB max), well within budget. Diminishing returns above 5× — going higher trades memory for no visible benefit.

featSage Mira renders taller without bilinear blur

New NPC_SPRITE_HEIGHTS map provides per-NPC render-height overrides for _drawNpcSprite. Sage Mira's entry sets her to 115 px (vs the 78 px default), reading as the lore-implied sage who towers over the bazaar regulars. Her source sprite is 640×864, so even at the new 115 px height the draw is still a ~7.5× downsample — no upscale, no bilinear blur. Smoothing quality bumped to 'high' at the same site so the larger render benefits from the better downsampler.

v0.25.270 Two new hairstyles — Shaggy + Spiky

featShaggy + Spiky hairstyles in the wardrobe

Two new sprite hairstyles drop into the Q-key Character Studio picker alongside Flow and Ponytail: Shaggy 🍂 (loose unkempt layered cut) and Spiky ⚡ (shounen pointed clusters). Both ship as 800×800 head-aligned WebPs in Sprites/character/hair/, matching the existing format so they slot straight into the LX_HAIR dispatch in drawBone('head') with no render-rect changes.

  • Wired sites: LX_HAIR.files (sprite registry), HERO_VEC_HAIR_OPTIONS (picker list), _migrateHairId whitelist (saves with the new ids pass through untouched), and the REQUIRED preload manifest so the sprites are decoded before first paint
  • No vector goo entries: sprites are the canonical source. flow and ponytail already shipped sprite-only and the renderer falls back gracefully to flow's vector goo for the brief decode window if needed
  • Cache invalidation: the existing LX_HAIR onload hook clears _LX_HERO_IDLE_BAKE_CACHE when each new sprite finishes loading, so the v0.25.269 super-sampled idle bake re-bakes with the sprite once it's ready

v0.25.269 Sharp idle hero · Amnesiac under Sanctum portal · Quickening boon

polishIdle hero stays sharp under the chibi transform

The cached idle frame (_lxBakeHeroIdle, introduced in v0.25.176 for the 60 % CPU win) used to bake the hero at logical 100×100 pixels and then blit through the _chibiApply 1.19×1.06 scale. v0.25.266 disabled imageSmoothingEnabled around that blit to escape the bilinear soft-blur, but the trade-off was nearest-neighbour pixel jaggies — the player still didn't read as razor-sharp the way the Q-key Character Studio preview does at 5× scale.

Fix: the bake is now super-sampled at 3× (300×300 physical pixels for the same 100×100 logical footprint), and the blit re-enables imageSmoothingEnabled = true with imageSmoothingQuality = 'high' to anti-alias the downscale. The cache key is unchanged so the per-look memoisation still hits, and the 60 % perf win is preserved (vector eval still happens once per look swap, not every frame). Net result: idle hero crispness now matches the Character Studio preview.

featAmnesiac stands under the Zodiac Sanctum portal

The Amnesiac NPC moved from x:300 to x:440 in the Bazaar — directly underneath the ⭐ Zodiac Sanctum portal that already sat at x:440. His lore arc points players toward the Sanctum, and the existing comment on the portal push already (incorrectly) said he was at x:440. Sage Mira slid right from x:520 → x:600 to keep symmetric spacing with Taxi Uncle (x:860); platform layout untouched.

featQuickening boon — chance to bypass skill cooldowns

New entry in POWERUPS: Quickening (⚡, cdSkip). Roll range 5–20 %; sums into player.mods.cdrChance, hard-capped at 0.20. Each successful cast in castSkill rolls once against this chance: on a hit, the just-applied player.skillCooldowns[id] is reset to 0, the skill is immediately re-castable, and the player gets an "⚡ Quickening!" toast plus a brief flash and the cd_refund SFX.

  • Roll range: 5 % minimum, 20 % maximum per drop. Reroll at the U panel like any other boon.
  • Stacking ceiling: equipping multiple Quickenings is redundant — total cdrChance is clamped to 20 % in _applyEquippedBoons. A single godroll already saturates the cap.
  • Excluded skills: phantom_cut and nightreaper_mark are CDR-immune ultimates (the v0.25.237 12 s lock); Quickening can't bypass either.
  • Why a chance, not a flat reduction: WIS already grants a deterministic 0–40 % CDR multiplier and the blanket -25 % JOB_CD_MUL stacks on top. A bursty proc-based bypass reads differently — you feel it land instead of just shaving milliseconds.

featThree authored map backdrops

Replaced the procedural / generic backdrops on three of the most-visited maps with hand-authored hero art that the player commissioned. Each one slots into the existing md.bg pipeline, registers a Phaser texture key, and — for maps that previously rendered through bespoke canvas drawing functions — gets a pass-through gate so the new image actually wins.

  • Zodiac Sanctum (zodiacHall) — previously the procedural drawZodiacHub starry-wall — now uses bg_v3_zodiacSanctum.png. The 12 portals + sky gradient + ground still ride on top, but the wall behind them is now authored.
  • Carriage of Ascension (tower) swapped from the borrowed zodiacDawn cinematic to bg_v3_carriageOfAscension.png. The procedural drawCarriageInterior path is bypassed when the authored bg is loaded.

The W world map modal now uses bg_v3_worldMapInterface.gif as its backdrop — animated parchment-and-stars under the existing SVG node graph. Layered with a translucent rgba(10,6,24,0.5) overlay so node labels, sub-labels, dashed connection lines, and the legend bar still read clearly against the bright art. Falls back to the original radial gradient if the gif fails to decode.

polishPlumbing

  • New BG_IMAGES keys: everdawnBazaar, zodiacSanctum, carriageOfAscension
  • New Phaser texture keys: bg_everdawnBazaar, bg_zodiacSanctum, bg_carriageOfAscension
  • drawBackground now defers the sanctum / isCarriage / isZodiac / isZodiacHub procedural early-returns when an authored md.bg is loaded — same gate behaviour Phaser already uses
  • All four files preloaded via the REQUIRED manifest so they're ready for the world reveal

The four merchant NPCs — Pharma Sis (potions), Brok (weapons + crafting bench), Old Arlen (lore), and Fashionista (wardrobe) — have moved out of the Bazaar and into a new dedicated pocket map: Everdawn Marketplace. The Bazaar now keeps only the lore-anchor NPCs (Amnesiac, Sage Mira, Taxi Uncle).

Wired into NPC_SPRITE_FILES + the world-reveal preload manifest so it decodes before the marketplace loads.

v0.25.266 Idle character no longer renders blurred

bugPlayer crispness when standing still

The vector-hero idle frames are baked into a 100×100 offscreen canvas (_lxBakeHeroIdle) and redrawn each frame as a single drawImage — the v0.25.176 perf optimization that gave a 60+% reduction in idle-frame CPU on mobile. But that bake is drawn through the _chibiApply scale transform (1.19 × 1.06), and canvas's default imageSmoothingEnabled = true bilinearly filtered the cached bitmap during that scaled redraw — so the hero looked subtly soft / out-of-focus the moment they stopped moving. Walking, attacking, and jumping all bypass the cache and re-rasterise the vectors at the final scale, so the blur was idle-only and easy to miss until you sat next to a moving NPC for comparison.

Fix: _drawVectorHeroCached now flips ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = false around the cached drawImage calls (and restores the previous value afterward). Idle hero stays crisp; the perf win from caching is preserved.

v0.25.265 Boss arena BGM — "Gravitos Ascends" plays in every boss map

featDedicated boss-arena soundtrack

New full-length track Gravitos Ascends (audio/bgm_boss.mp3, ~2.8 MB) loops in every map flagged isBossArena: true. The existing Mojiworld BGM (bgm_mojiworld.mp3) keeps its job in towns / fields / tower / zodiac / dungeon maps; the boss theme takes over the moment a boss-arena map loads.

  • Hard-swap with a 600 ms cross-fade, so the music shift reads as a deliberate "boss room" cue rather than a jarring cut
  • The boss element is unlocked on the same first-gesture pass as the main BGM, so it plays without an autoplay-blocker hiccup the first time the player enters a boss room
  • Fully-faded-out element pauses to free the mobile audio decoder slot — no zombie playback
  • Hooked into loadMap via _setBossBgm(MAPS[id].isBossArena); uses the static MAPS table (authoritative) rather than the in-progress game.mapData rebuild

Boss arenas this currently affects: Forest Glade boss arena, the Lava Crater, the Frozen Throne, the Gel Wetlands boss room, the Queen's Sanctum, plus all 12 zodiac boss rooms (5 hand-built arenas + the procedural zodiac arena variant).

v0.25.264 Performance pass — 5 verified fixes from a 4-agent deep audit

Follow-up to the v0.25.263 user feedback that the game still felt laggy. Spawned four parallel perf audit agents (render hot-path, update-loop/collision, particle/VFX, and asset/GC pressure), then verified each high-impact finding line-by-line before shipping. Five real, high-impact fixes landed; the rest were either false positives or smaller wins held back for a follow-up pass.

featPhaser canvases now sleep when the game is paused

The two Phaser instances (BG + UI scene host) were ticking + rendering every frame even on menus, dialog, class-select, modals, and tutorial overlays — three concurrent render pipelines (vanilla canvas + 2× Phaser) with nothing meaningful changing on screen. _perfTick now toggles game.loop.sleep() / wake() on edge transitions of game.paused, dropping ~30-50% of the FPS budget on pause screens (desktop) and 40-70% on mobile.

featsaveState() debounced — major GC pressure relief

saveState() is called from ~30 sites: every kill, quest tick, boon equip, skill unlock, level-up, prestige, etc. Each call ran JSON.stringify() on the full {player, game} object (~10-40 KB) plus a localStorage.setItem — the dominant string-allocation source in heavy play (estimated 70-150 KB/s of churn).

  • saveState() is now a 1.5 s debounced trampoline that sets a dirty flag and queues a single flush
  • _flushSaveStateNow() contains the actual serialize-and-write — used by paths that can't wait (visibility-change, before-unload, prestige reload)
  • No save data lost: the critical-flush sites are wired up so backgrounding the tab or closing the window forces an immediate write
  • Major GC pauses on mobile every 10-15 s should disappear or shrink dramatically

polishAudio oscillator nodes now disconnect on completion

Every audio.env(...) call (hit, crit, pickup, levelup, potion, etc.) created an OscillatorNode + GainNode, called start + stop, but never disconnect(). WebAudio retains nodes that are still wired into the destination graph, so each combat hit (5-20× per second) was leaving zombie pairs pinned in memory — accumulating 200-500 KB over a 2-3 minute fight, especially brutal on mobile Safari + Firefox. Now both nodes are torn down via an onended callback once the envelope completes.

polishParticle budget guards on 4 high-cost skill casts

Several skills pushed straight to game.particles with no per-frame budget check. Frames already at the particle cap silently dropped these via the _trimVisualQueues overflow-splice — wasted allocation + GC for nothing. All four now route through _budgetedParticlePush() and break the loop early when the cap is hit:

  • Mage Z (Blink) — was 40 unguarded particles/cast (20 + 20 around teleport)
  • Mage Arcane Burst — wider 80-particle ring per cast
  • Lich Soul Vortex (G) — 80-particle ring on the open animation
  • Nightreaper Eclipse Massacre (G) — 4 trailing-shadow particles per dagger × 10 batches per cast = up to 400 particles per Eclipse on a packed room. Now breaks per-batch when budget is exhausted.

Visuals are unchanged below the cap; only frames already over budget see the trim.

polishSquared-distance comparisons in two hot inner loops

Projectile ricochet (next-target search) and Ice Spike's AoE-on-hit splash both used Math.hypot per candidate inside for (const m2 of game.monsters) loops — that's a sqrt every iteration. Both were doing radius compares (d < threshold) where the distance value itself is never used, so squaring the threshold and comparing dx*dx + dy*dy against it removes the sqrt entirely. Saves a few hundred microseconds per ricochet hit in dense pulls.

featWhat's still pending

Held back for a follow-up pass: damage-number gradient cache, screen-shake Math.random memoize, shadowBlur batching, drawSmoothFx composite batching, seraph heal-aura array cache, MP networking JSON.stringify debounce, toast pool, particle splice-thrashing → write-index. The five fixes shipped today are the highest-impact and easiest to verify; the rest will land after testing confirms the lag is meaningfully better.

v0.25.263 DoT cadence 0.5s · Fashionista NPC + Q wardrobe

polishBurn / poison DoT now ticks every 0.5 s

Cadence changed from 80 frames (~1.3 s) to 30 frames (0.5 s @ 60 fps). Per-tick damage scaled by 30/80 = 0.375× so total burn DPS over the full burn window is unchanged — players see smaller numbers tick more often. Pairs nicely with v0.25.262's burn cap: smaller per-tick spikes mean the cap kicks in more cleanly when many enemies are burning at once.

featFashionista NPC + cosmetic wardrobe

New NPC in Everdawn Bazaar — Fashionista at x:1000 (between Taxi Uncle and the Emerald Thicket portal). Runs the cosmetic-only wardrobe (skin / hair / eyes / mouth / class outfit pickers — the existing CharStudio system, just newly anchored).

  • Press Q anywhere to open the wardrobe (was already bound, now properly surfaced)
  • Or talk to Fashionista (press N near her) and pick "Open Wardrobe ✨"
  • Help panel updated with the new Q binding
  • Sprite gets a pink hand-mirror prop on the NPC body to read as a vanity vendor at a glance
  • New 7th sidewalk platform added at x:960 so her stall has its own raised walkway like the other vendors

Cosmetic only — wardrobe changes don't affect stats or skills, just how your hero looks. Carries across saves via the existing CharStudio persistence.

polishWiring details

  • NPC role 'wardrobe' added to the dialog handler
  • Hand-mirror prop drawn in the role-prop section of the procedural NPC body
  • Existing Q keybind (line 38454) routes to openCharStudio() — already there, just unsurfaced before today

v0.25.262 Lag mitigation pass + summon damage bumps

featSummon allies hit harder

SummonSourceWasNow
Skeleton / ZombieWarlock raise (Soul Siphon, Dark Pulse)0.35× ATK0.65× ATK
Wolf pack memberBeastmaster pack (3 wolves)0.8× ATK1.1× ATK
Single wolf companionBeastmaster Wild Bond F0.8× ATK1.4× ATK

Floor on raised-minion damage also raised from 4 → 8. Skeleton/zombie was severely underpowered relative to wolves; now in the same band but still lower than the iconic wolves. Single wolf hits hardest (lone-companion fantasy intact).

polishLag mitigation — 5 caps + smarter auto-perf

Game was reported as "very laggy". Added five caps that prevent runaway tick costs without touching gameplay feel:

  • Burn DoT tick cap — at most MAX_BURNING (12 mobile / 24 desktop) burns deal damage per frame. Burns still decay normally so they expire on schedule; only the visible damage tick is throttled. Prevents the ticks-and-damage-numbers cascade in crowded rooms.
  • Player projectile cap — MAX_PLAYER_PROJECTILES (60 mobile / 120 desktop). When skill spawns pile up past the cap (Ballista hold + Arrow Rain + Elemental Convergence overlap), the OLDEST player projectiles are dropped. Targets the O(n²) projectile×monster collision loop.
  • Minion cap — MAX_MINIONS (6 mobile / 10 desktop). Stops Soul Siphon / Dark Pulse stacks from blowing past frame budget on the seek-loop.
  • Auto-lowFx more responsive — triggers at 8 slow frames (was 12), avg-frame threshold 22 ms → 20 ms, hold window 3 s → 6 s so brief recovery doesn't bounce.
  • Performance-mode toast — first time auto-lowFx engages per session: "⚡ Performance mode — FX reduced for smoother frames". Subsequent toggles silent.

polishImplementation details

  • Burn cap uses game._burnTickedThisFrame reset in _trimVisualQueues at end of every frame
  • Projectile + minion caps run inside the same end-of-frame trim sweep so the work is paid once per frame, not per-emit
  • All caps respect mobile detection (_IS_MOBILE_AT_LOAD) — phones get tighter limits than desktop
  • No gameplay invariants change — burns still expire correctly, projectiles still pierce, minions still seek and attack at the same cadence

polishWhat this DOESN'T fix (deferred)

The IMPROVEMENT_PLAN.md still has the bigger perf wins flagged: spatial-grid for projectile×monster collision (P1, ~−3 to −5 ms/frame), gradient cache (P2, ~−1.5 ms/frame), particle pool (P3, ~−2 ms/frame). Those are bigger refactors saved for a focused perf-only ship. Today's caps stop the worst-case spikes without touching the shapes of those systems.

v0.25.261 Boon economy · NPC rename · Sniper V · 6 polish changes

featBoon economy tightened — boss-only drops + Sage Mira gated

  • BOON_EQUIP_CAP 5 → 3 — boon picks feel like real build commitments now, not "everything fits"
  • Boons no longer drop from regular mobs, elites, or mini-bosses — only from full-tier boss kills (the powerup-pick screen at boss death) + Sage Mira's offering
  • Sage Mira: 12-hour real-time cooldown, 5000 Lumens (was 1500 / unlimited). Cooldown stored in player._sageNextAt as epoch ms; resets on prestige. Dialog text dynamically shows the wait time when the offering isn't ready

featPharma Sis (Elspeth renamed)

v0.25.260 Nightreaper Eclipse rework · Archer Evade Burst · Ballista hold tuning

featNightreaper G — Eclipse Massacre (mechanically distinct from Phantom)

Nightreaper's G previously played almost identically to Phantom's — both blink-zipped between marked enemies. Reworked into a fundamentally different ult:

  • Stationary 2.4 s channel — player roots in place + invulnerable (Phantom moves via chain-teleport)
  • Eclipse summons a giant blood-eclipsed moon over the player
  • Spectral daggers rain down on EVERY visible enemy in 10 timed batches (re-evaluated each batch so spawning mobs get hit too)
  • No target cap (Phantom is single-target precision capped at 6)
  • Per-dagger: ATK × 1.2 with 50% DEF reduction + 55% crit-bias + 280 ms stun
  • Finale "snap": ALL on-screen enemies take a forced-crit ATK × 2.0 + 25 aftershock with knockback + 800 ms stun
  • HP top-up on completion preserved (18% maxHP)
  • Fixed 12 s CD (CDR-immune) preserved from v0.25.237

Result: Phantom is the precision single-target executioner; Nightreaper is the area-control rain-of-daggers caster. Same job ult slot, totally different feel.

featNew Nightreaper Eclipse sprite

More grand and flashy than Phantom's portal (which was already a strong sprite — but the eclipse has the bigger silhouette and more dynamic radial energy).

featArcher C (Evade Burst) — huge knockback + cute explosion

Renamed from "Evade Roll" to "Evade Burst". Now ALSO blasts nearby monsters away when triggered:

  • Blast radius: 130 px around the player at the moment of cast
  • Knockback: vx ±18, vy −9 — even tanky elites get a real launch
  • Stun: 350 ms on every mob hit
  • Damage: minor (ATK × 0.4 + 4) — the skill is for spacing, not nuking
  • Audio + flash + shake when 1+ mob is hit
  • Toast when 2+ are knocked back
  • MP cost: 6 → 8 (slightly higher to match the offensive utility)
  • CD: 1.5 s → 1.7 s (+0.2 s)

New Ludo sprite at Sprites/fx/evade_burst.webp: cute warm-gold starburst with soft cream smoke puffs and gold sparkle particles — playful explosive feel, not menacing. Spawned at 180 px with slow rotation.

polishBallista Siege Volley — duration / sprite / CD tuning

v0.25.257's hold channel got a tuning pass:

  • Duration: 10 s → 8 s (480 frames at 60 fps)
  • Sprite stays anchored to the chest the entire hold (sprite re-spawns every 24 frames / ~400 ms with overlap so there's no flicker)
  • Cooldown: 20 s → 23 s (+3 s as requested)
  • Per-arrow damage and cadence unchanged — total channel damage now ~90× ATK over 8 s (was ~115× over 10 s) — slightly less burst, but the visual continuity through the hold should make it feel meatier

featPhantom V (Voidrift Blink) — 3-charge half-screen zip

  • 3 charges per cast cycle — tap up to 3 times in quick succession
  • Re-cast gate is 250 ms between charges; full 14 s cooldown only triggers after the 3rd charge
  • Damage ramps mildly across charges: 1.0× → 1.15× → 1.3× of getAtk() × 2.0

  • Toast surfaces remaining charges: "Voidrift 2 charges left" → "Voidrift 1 charge left" → "Voidrift — final blink"
  • MP cost dropped from 35 → 25 since the kit is more committal

Visually: phantom afterimages along the zip path, a 130 px Voidrift slash sprite at the start position, a larger 160 px sprite at the destination (with spin), and a violet void particle ring on landing.   • Charges refill on first cast after the cooldown expires (no manual reset needed elsewhere)

v0.25.257 Ballista Siege Volley reworked into a 10-second hold channel

featHold G to channel a sustained arrow stream

Ballista's master signature was a 0.5-second 8-shot burst — over before the player could read what happened. Reworked into a 10-second hold channel: press G to start, hold to keep firing, release at any time to end early. Trade-off: drains MP while channelling so the player decides "burst now or save MP."

polishChannel mechanics

  • Initial cast cost: 25 MP (down from 45 MP since you can release early)
  • MP drain: +1 MP every 10 frames (~6 MP/sec) → up to 60 MP over a full 10 s
  • Total full-channel cost: ~85 MP (vs old burst's 45 MP, but ~4× the total damage)
  • Cadence: Two arrows fire every 9 frames (~150 ms) → ~67 volleys × 2 arrows = ~134 arrows over 10 s
  • Per-arrow damage: getAtk() × 0.85 + 5 (down from × 3.5 + 25) — pierce + defBreak preserved
  • Total channel damage: ~115× ATK over 10 s vs old burst's ~28× in 0.5 s — sustained DPS slightly lower per-second but a much bigger total commitment window
  • Cooldown unchanged at 20 s — fires regardless of how early you release, so tap-spam can't game it

polishEnd conditions

Channel terminates immediately on any of: G released, 10 s expired, player dies, player hit-stunned, or MP drops below 1. Channel state is also cleared on save load, death, and respawn (defensive — doesn't carry into a new run).

polishPer-frame tick

Logic lives in updatePlayer() right after the Aegis tick. Adds zero overhead when the channel is inactive (early-return on if (!player._ballistaChannel)). Map transitions reset game.keys so a channel started before a portal naturally ends on the first frame of the new map.

v0.25.256 Endgame dailies + 5 polish fixes from the audit's QOL track

feat3 new Lv 30+ recurring daily challenges

Endgame audit flagged "no recurring daily quest at Lv 40+" as a HIGH gap — the Lv 40-50 stretch had only one one-time quest. Added 3 dailies that recycle from the existing pool every UTC midnight:

  • kill200 — Defeat 200 enemies today (minLv 30, reward: 2,500 Lumens + 2 SP)
  • gravitos1 — Defeat Gravitos at the Singularity (minLv 35, reward: 3,500 Lumens + 2 SP)
  • enhance10 — Land 10 successful enhancements (minLv 35, reward: 4,000 Lumens + 2 SP)

These tie back to existing endgame loops (Tier-5 grind, Gravitos farm, ★ enhancement) — no new content needed, just a steady stream of meaningful objectives.

polishBoon equip / unequip audio cue

Equipping or unequipping a boon used to be silent — only the rendered list updated. Now equip plays the 'mp_refund' SFX with a tiny flash; unequip plays the distinct 'cd_refund' SFX. Audible difference signals which action fired.

polishSet 2-piece activation now flashes

3pc activation already had flash + shake + audio. 2pc was audio-only — felt like a smaller deal than it is. Added flash(0.18) on 2pc activation so the milestone reads consistently. (No change to 2pc/mismatch behaviour — those still stay quiet.)

polishAttribute allocation feedback

Clicking the + button to spend an attribute point used to silently re-render the panel. Now plays the 'mp_refund' SFX + small flash(0.08) so the spend feels snappy.

polishMute (M) added to help panel keybind list

The Mute toggle was functional but undiscoverable from the in-game help modal. Added <kbd>M</kbd> row to the Menus & Items column. (Re-pick Job/Master via 0 was already listed — agent's claim was partially false.)

polishFalse positives cleared during verification

  • "3pc set bonus has no flash/shake/audio" — already wired (line 8246–8248); only 2pc was missing.
  • "Re-pick job (0) missing from help" — already listed at line 2690.
  • "Mage MP regen creates infinite spam loop" — m_surge tree node creates a counter-incentive; working as designed.
  • "Marksman G weak vs Ballista" — agent missed the actual 7× ATK + alwaysCrit damage.

v0.25.255 Combat balance — verified findings from 6-agent deep audit

6 parallel audit agents (class kit / monster / economy / endgame / bug-hunt / polish) returned 51 candidate findings. After line-by-line verification: 4 verified true and fixed, 1 mass batch of false positives cleared (incl. all 4 boss-balance HIGH severities — agent used wrong contact-damage formula).

bugHIGH — Doombringer slam coda 3.5× → 2.8× ATK

Blade of Calamity's final ground slam was dealing getAtk() * 3.5 on top of 10 prior strikes at 2.4× each — total burst window ≈ 27.5× ATK, well above peer master G skills (Crusader Aegis sustain ≈ 8× over 16 s; Dragoon Skylance ≈ 6×). Slam dropped to 2.8× — total burst now ≈ 26.4×, matching Doombringer's "executioner stroke" identity without trivialising tanky elites. maple_game.html:16070

bugMED — Phantom Cut 2.6× → 2.2× per-strike base

Phantom's chain-execute hit for getAtk() * 2.6 per target (up to 6 hits + nova). Compared to Nightreaper's 1.8× per hit (up to 14 targets), Phantom was +44% per-hit on a shorter chain — too dominant in single-elite encounters. Dropped to 2.2× to keep Phantom's per-strike edge over Nightreaper without tilting the choice. maple_game.html:16547

bugHIGH — Empowered tier multiplier stacking with veteran scaling

EMPOWERED_TIER multipliers (1.7× HP / 1.55× ATK on cookie etc.) compose with veteran scaling (line 12404, +3% HP per level above natural). At Lv 25 a Lv-4 Empowered Cookie was reaching ≈ 1,200 HP — 60+ basic-attack hits on what's still flavor mob, not a mini-boss. Dropped HP/ATK muls ~10% across all 4 empowered types (gummy/cookie/frog/axolotl). EXP/Mesos kept high so encounters stay rewarding. maple_game.html:6452

polishMED — Skywisp exp/mesos bumped (70/34 → 85/38)

Tier-2 air mob's exp:HP ratio (3.43) was identical to tier-1 mobs — grind-efficiency parity broke the tier promise. Bumped exp 70 → 85 + mesos 34 → 38 to bring it in line with Horny / Frog efficiency at the same band.

polishFalse positives cleared during verification

  • Boss-balance HIGH × 4 (Gravitos / Aetherion contact damage, Archon enrage, Empowered Cookie damage spike) — agent used a multiplicative contact formula atk * 1.3 - def * 0.4 that doesn't exist in the code. Real formula is flat atk - getDef() + jitter (line 17421). Recomputed: Gravitos hits Lv 28 warrior for ~159 (18% of 884 maxHP), Aetherion hits Lv 25 for ~119 (15% of 800 maxHP). Both within bounds. Aetherion HP "100-min fight" used a Lv 25 unenhanced basic-attack DPS and ignored skill multipliers and PLAYER_ATK_MUL placement.
  • Marksman G "weak vs Ballista" — agent missed the actual values. One Shot is getAtk() * 7 + 60 (line 16723) with alwaysCrit: true and 12% instakill on non-bosses. Effective ≈ 10.5× ATK guaranteed crit, comparable to Ballista's 8 × 2.5×.
  • Mage MP regen "infinite spam loop" — Arcane Surge tree node (line 5574) creates a counter-incentive: spell damage scales with current MP %, so dumping MP into spam reduces damage. Working as designed.
  • "bossDefeated not initialised on load" — agent self-dismissed; defaulter exists at line 10973.
  • "Quest boss kind mismatch" — agent self-dismissed; type/bossType match correctly.
  • "Achievement starforged ★5 boundary" — agent self-dismissed; >= 5 is correct.
  • "setshards undefined on old saves" — defaulter shipped in v0.25.250.

v0.25.254 Playthrough audit fixes — 5 verified issues squashed

Triaged findings from a 4-agent parallel playthrough audit. Of 11 candidate findings, 5 were verified true; 6 were false positives (cleared via line-by-line verification). Shipped fixes:

bugHIGH — Class T2/T3 weapons hidden from Lv 6–9 shop

The v0.25.250 class-aware shop filter combined generic + class items into one list, then sliced by a global cap (4 items at Lv <10). Result: a Warrior at Lv 8 saw 4 generic ladder weapons (Wooden → Runed) and never saw their tier-2 class weapon (Crusader Mace), even though it was tier-appropriate. Now: generic ladder is capped by level (2/3/4/6), class items show independently on a tier-gated reveal (T2 from Lv 6, T3 from Lv 10) — Warriors at Lv 8 now see Crusader Mace as intended.

bugMED — Hardcoded Lv 50 in prestige flow → constant

3 sites still hardcoded 50 for prestige (gate, modal copy, dev cheat). Introduced PRESTIGE_LEVEL = 50 constant alongside the existing JOB_ADVANCE_LEVEL / MASTER_ADVANCE_LEVEL so the entire advancement curve is now declared in one block. Future tweaks won't desync.

bugMED — Boon-loadout cap silently truncates on save load

v0.25.247's defensive sanitiser correctly clamped boonsEquipped to BOON_EQUIP_CAP, but did so silently — players reloading a save with too many equipped boons would see them quietly disappear. Now fires a toast: "◈ Boon loadout capped at 6 — extras unequipped".

polishLOW — Daily quest reach25 ID renamed to reach20

v0.25.253 changed the goal from 25 → 20 to align with the new job-advance level, but the internal id was still 'reach25'. Renamed for clarity in the codebase + future quest-tracking telemetry.

polishLOW — Dev cheat HP/exp curve realigned with G2 rebalance

The dev "jump to max level" cheat (press 0) was using a stale 1.20 / 1.24 / 1.28 multiplier curve. Realigned with the live _maybeLevelUp tier curve (1.20 → 1.40 → 1.40 → 1.42 → 1.55) from v0.25.242 G2 so the post-cheat expToNext matches reality. Hardcoded 49 "missed levels" replaced with PRESTIGE_LEVEL - player.level so the cheat works from any starting level.

polishFalse positives cleared during verification

  • "W-key binding missing" — verified at line 8479, routes to toggleWorldMap(). Works.
  • "Modal stack closes all at once" — agent flagged as bug; this is intentional behavior since v0.25.224.
  • "Lv 50 achievement broken by advancement rebalance" — agent self-corrected; the lv50 achievement tests player.level >= 50 atomically and is independent of advancement gating.
  • "Tutorial X-slot Lv 5 unlock comment unclear" — comment was actually accurate; agent misread.
  • "Apostrophe sprite-key collision" — verified _itemKey() normalises both straight and curly apostrophes correctly.
  • "Forced-modal Esc bypass" — verified at line 22337; tutorial / class-select / advancement all properly forced.

v0.25.253 First-time tutorial · Job advance Lv 20 · Master advance Lv 40

featFirst-time tutorial walkthrough

An 8-step modal tutorial fires once per save slot on first class pick (gated by localStorage.mojiworld_tutorial_seen). Covers everything a new player needs:

  1. 👋 Welcome — sets the tone
  2. 🎮 Movement & combat — arrow keys, jump, attack, full keybind reference at ?
  3. ⚔️ Defeat monsters — XP, Lumens, combo multiplier, mini-bosses
  4. ⭐ Level up & allocate points — U opens the character panel; STR/AGI/INT/VIT/WIS/LCK breakdown; new skill slot every 5 levels
  5. 🎒 Inventory & enhancement — B for inventory, Brok the Blacksmith for ★0–10 enhancement, Setshard crafting for missing set pieces
  6. ✨ Boons — passive perks from mini-boss drops or Sage Mira; equip up to 6 in the U-panel Boons tab
  7. 🗺️ World map & fast travel — W opens the map; Taxi Uncle offers the same routes
  8. ✦ Job & Master advancement — Lv 20 picks Job, Lv 40 picks Master class

Skippable at any step. Esc is blocked while open (would otherwise leave the seen-flag unstamped); the Skip button explicitly marks-seen so you don't get re-prompted on the next class pick.

featJob advancement at Lv 20 (was 25), Master at Lv 40 (was 50)

Earlier advancement makes the class identity reach players faster. Cascading skill-slot unlocks rebalanced to align:

  • D (skill 5): Lv 20 → Lv 18 (lands BEFORE job advance so you have a full kit at the unlock moment)
  • F (job signature): Lv 25 → Lv 20 (unlocks AT job advance)
  • V (job ultimate): Lv 30 → Lv 25 (5 levels after job pick)
  • G (master signature): Lv 49 → Lv 39 (1 below master advance, live the moment you choose)

Class-select panel + lore intro updated to match. Daily quest "Reach character level 25" bumped to "Reach character level 20" with a lower minLv prerequisite. Prestige cap stays at Lv 50, giving 10 levels of post-master endgame to grind.

featLX_ITEMS sprite registry + sprite-with-emoji-fallback render

New itemIconHtml(item, sizePx) helper renders an <img> tag if the item has a sprite registered AND the image has finished decoding; otherwise falls back to the existing emoji icon. Wired into every equipment-display surface:

  • Inventory grid (B / U-panel Items tab) — 44 px sprites in equipment slots
  • Equipped slot row (character panel) — 42 px in each slot
  • Item tooltip (hover) — 24 px next to the name
  • Enhancement Forge modal — 32 px in the item list
  • Crafting bench modal — 32 px in both the disassemble and craft panes
  • Brok's shop rows — 36 px when buying or selling
  • Auto-equip toast — 22 px in the gear-change popup

The fallback path means non-set items (the generic ladder + class T2/T3 weapons + class T2/T3 armors) keep their emoji icons until their sprites are added in a future ship — no broken rendering.

polishWiring details

  • _itemKey(it) normalises item names to lookup keys (lowercase, underscore-separated, ASCII-only)
  • _itemReady(img) checks complete && naturalWidth > 0 so partially-decoded images don't render as broken icons
  • 15 sprite paths added to the preloader DEFERRED list — they decode in the background after the bazaar reveal
  • image-rendering: auto on item sprites so they scale smoothly at any size (HUD vs tooltip vs panel)
  • Sprites stored at Sprites/items/<name>.webp — same naming convention as Ludo-generated FX sprites

polishRoadmap (deferred)

Sprites for the 31 remaining items (6 generic weapons + 8 mid-tier class weapons + 6 generic armors + 8 mid-tier class armors + 6 generic accessories) — same prompt template, just need more Ludo calls. Will land in a future ship; the registry already supports them via the same key-based lookup, so adding them is just a 1-line registry edit + 1-line preloader entry per sprite.

  • Top pane lists every set legendary in your inventory + equipped slots with one-click +4◈ disassemble buttons
  • Bottom pane lists every craftable set piece across all 5 sets, with stats preview + class-affinity warning when a piece is for a different class
  • Disabled craft buttons carry a title tooltip telling you exactly what you're missing ("Need 4 more Setshards" / "Need 1,500 more Lumens")
  • Currency header always visible: Setshards: N◈ + Lumens: M
  • Sparkle burst + audio + flash on every successful craft
  • Setshards persist across sessions via player.setshards; reset on prestige (fresh crafting economy each ascension)

v0.25.249 Set pieces wearable by everyone · class-gated bonuses · 3pc set auras

featAll set pieces are now wearable by every class

Per request: a mage CAN equip a Doomforged Greatsword and benefit from its raw stats (ATK, HP, etc.) — but the set bonuses only fire when the set's class matches the player's class. 'any' sets (Dawnshard) work universally.

  • getSetBonus() now skips contributions from sets where set.cls !== player.cls (and not 'any')
  • Tooltip shows the gate explicitly: "⚠ Bonuses only active for Warrior" in orange when you're looking at an off-class set piece
  • Set-complete toast differentiates — class-match crossing 3pc shows the celebratory "✦ SET COMPLETE" with audio + flash; mismatched 3pc shows a quiet "3 [Set] pieces equipped — bonus is warrior-only"
  • 2pc mismatch is silent (no point pinging the player about a bonus that isn't activating)

feat3-piece set auras — visible thematic glow

When you've got 3 pieces of your class's set equipped, the player gets a subtle thematic aura. Each aura has 3 layers — a soft body halo + a ground glow + per-set decorative particles:

  • 🌟 Dawnshard (any) — warm gold radiance with rising sparkle motes
  • ⚔️ Doomforged (warrior) — hot red embers smoldering up from the feet
  • 🥷 Shadowweave (rogue) — violet shadow wisps trailing behind your direction
  • 🪄 Voidcaller (mage) — three slowly-orbiting arcane runes at chest height
  • 🏹 Skyhunter (archer) — green leaves drifting on a gentle breeze

Auras are render-only (don't affect gameplay), pulse gently so they read as a status effect rather than decor, and emit ~1 particle every 8 frames so the per-frame budget barely notices. Drawn behind the chibi base via drawSetAura() which fires from drawPlayer(); only renders for sets whose class matches yours, so a mage in 3 Doomforged pieces correctly sees no aura.

polishWiring details

  • _activeFullSets() helper returns the list of class-matched 3pc sets — used by both the aura render and any future set-effect hooks
  • Particle bursts use the existing game.particles queue so they auto-cull via _trimVisualQueues from v0.25.240
  • Auras + halo use globalCompositeOperation: 'lighter' so they additively brighten the character rather than tint it

v0.25.248 Equipment categorization · class-affinity loot · 5 set bonuses

featEvery item now categorised by class + tier + set

The 18 base items each carry three new fields:

  • cls — 'warrior' / 'rogue' / 'mage' / 'archer' / 'any' (class affinity)
  • tier — 1 (starter) → 5 (endgame legendary), surfaced in the tooltip as Common · T1 / Legendary · T5
  • setId — optional set membership; matching pieces grant 2pc / 3pc bonuses

feat5 sets, 12 new legendary items

The existing Dawnshard legendaries (sword + aegis + medallion) form the universal Dawnshard set. Each combat class gets its own thematic 3-piece set:

SetClass2-piece3-piece
🌟 Dawnshard any +10% ATK +15 Crit, +50 HP
⚔️ Doomforged warrior +60 HP +12% ATK, +5 DEF
🥷 Shadowweave rogue +12 Crit +0.5 Spd, +10% Dodge
🪄 Voidcaller mage +30 MP +20% Crit DMG, +1 Multishot
🏹 Skyhunter archer +0.4 Spd +1 Multishot, +15 Crit

New items added: Doomforged Greatsword + Plate + Sigil · Shadowweave Dagger + Cloak + Veil · Voidcaller Staff + Robe + Orb · Skyhunter Longbow + Vest + Quiver. All Tier-5 legendaries with class-thematic stats.

featSet-bonus engine + tooltips

  • getSetBonus(key) walks equipped items and adds 2pc / 3pc contributions; folded into getEquipBonus so every existing stat lookup picks them up
  • Item tooltip shows class affinity badge (⚔️ Warrior) and set membership status (🌟 Dawnshard Set 2/3) with bonus lines lit green when active, dim grey when not
  • _checkSetComplete() fires a toast when player crosses the 2pc or 3pc threshold (with audio + flash on completion); wired to all three equip sites (auto-equip, manual equip, manual unequip)

polishClass-affinity drop weighting

rollItemDrop now biases toward the player's class:

  • Items with cls: 'any' — full rarity weight (unchanged)
  • Items matching player's class — 1.5× weight
  • Items mismatched to player's class — 0.3× weight (still possible for sale value, just rare)

Cross-class drops still happen for trading / selling, but the loot you find is mostly relevant to your build. A warrior won't be drowning in Voidcaller Staffs.

v0.25.247 Bug fix sweep — 7 verified glitches across combat, UI, save, animation

bugC1 (HIGH) — Elemental Chain zombie callback

Mage skill-tree node "Elemental Chain" used a raw setTimeout for the chain follow-up. The callback fired even after death, map transitions, or skill cancellation — applying damage to a stale monster reference (or worse, in the wrong map context). Switched to scheduleSkillTimer so it's properly cancelled in cancelPendingSkillTimers(). maple_game.html:17791

bugC2 (MEDIUM) — Sniper Railshot was always crit-damage

Railshot unconditionally multiplied damage by getCritDmg() at the call site (baseAtk * 3.2 * stackMul * getCritDmg()) and passed true for the crit flag — making every hit a guaranteed crit regardless of crit chance. Now rolls crit per-hit with strong crit-bias (40% bonus floor, plus normal crit chance). Skill scales with build investment again. maple_game.html:15450

bugC3 (LOW) — Nightreaper ricochet didn't check pierce hits

Ricochet maintained its own hitSet separate from the projectile's pierce hitIds. Theoretical bug: a projectile with both pierce: true and ricochet: N could ricochet back to a monster it had already pierced. Now the bounce candidate-search excludes both sets. maple_game.html:18615

bugA3 (MEDIUM) — Camera not snapped to player on map load

loadMap() reset most map state but left game.camera.x at the previous map's last position. The camera lerp converged in ~30 frames, but during that ~0.5 s the parallax background, clouds, and ambient birds rendered at the wrong horizontal offset on every map transition. Now the camera snaps to the player's center immediately. maple_game.html:11594

bugU5 (MEDIUM) — uiConfirm Promise hung if Esc pressed

The in-game confirm modal (added in v0.25.244) registered onclick handlers on Yes / No but had no Esc handler. When Esc routed through closeAllModals, the modal hid but the awaiting Promise never resolved — calling code (reset save, respec, prestige, boon discard) hung in limbo. Now: capture-phase Esc handler resolves false; closeAllModals also calls game._uiConfirmCleanup() if a confirm is in flight.

bugS4 (LOW) — Boon equip indices defensively cleaned on save load

Out-of-bounds or duplicate indices in player.boonsEquipped (from a corrupted save, manual edit, or migration mismatch) used to silently no-op inside _applyEquippedBoons, leaving an "equipped slot" that contributed nothing. Load now sanitises: integer-only, in-bounds, deduped, capped at BOON_EQUIP_CAP.

polishR1 — Mobile-ctrl auto-hide gameplay-keys-only filter

The keyboard auto-hide added in v0.25.246 fired on any keydown including Tab, Esc, F11, and modifier-only presses. Now restricted to actual gameplay keys (movement, skills, common HUD shortcuts) and ignores Alt/Ctrl/Meta combinations.

v0.25.246 Mobile-controls toggle persistence + 7 QOL fixes from a debug scan

bugTouch controls now properly toggleable on desktop fullscreen

Reported: the touch-control deck was appearing on desktop fullscreen mode (likely from pointer: coarse matching on hybrid laptops / touchscreen monitors). Three fixes layered:

  • Toggle state persists across sessions via localStorage (key mojiworld_hide_mobile_ctrl). Hit the corner ✕ once and it stays hidden forever.
  • URL opt-out: append ?nomobile=1 to permanently force-hide regardless of pointer detection. Useful for streamers / desktop reviewers.
  • Auto-hide on keyboard usage: any gameplay key press flips the deck off (one-shot per session, gated to first-time users only — never overrides a saved preference).
  • Toast feedback on every toggle so the change registers visually + via screen reader ("Touch controls hidden" / "Touch controls shown").
  • Keyboard accessible: the toggle button now responds to Enter and Space (was mouse/tap-only).

polishQ1 — Audio + toast feedback on every shop purchase

Buying potions or gear used to feel silent — Lumens vanished and a tiny toast fired but no SFX. Both buy paths now play the 'meso' coin-jingle SFX (already defined in audio.play()) and tint the toast with rarity color. Insufficient-funds attempts now show a "Need X more Lumens" toast instead of a silent no-op.

polishQ4 — Disabled buy buttons explain why

Greyed-out "Buy" buttons in shops now carry a title="Need X more Lumens" tooltip on hover. Removes the "is this broken?" moment when a button looks dead.

polishQ5 — Empty sell-shop copy hints at the loop

The empty sell shop used to say "Nothing to sell." Now: "🛍️ Sell unwanted gear here for ~40% of its buy price. Pick up drops or buy from Brok's Forge to fill your bags." — surfaces the buy/equip/sell loop for new players.

bugR2 — Character Studio rAF leak fixed

renderCharStudio() early-returned when the canvas was missing (modal closed) but never cancelled the queued requestAnimationFrame. The callback chain ran forever (~60 calls/sec) on a closed modal. Now the early-return cancels the queued frame first.

polishR3 — Diagnostic console.log calls gated behind LX_DEBUG

Three boot-time console.log calls ([phaser], [Hero], [CharStudio]) were always firing on every page load. They now check localStorage.LX_DEBUG === '1' first — set the flag if you want detailed boot logging, otherwise the console stays clean.

v0.25.245 Multiplayer wedge — co-op XP bonus when party members are nearby

featS2 — +50% co-op XP when a peer is on your map

Previously multiplayer was presence + chat only — two solo runs in adjacent windows. Now: if any peer is on the same map within ~400 px of the killed monster, you get +50% XP for that kill. Pure client-side; uses the existing 14 Hz presence broadcast (no protocol changes, server unchanged). A toast surfaces the bonus the first time it fires per 6 s window so the mechanic is discoverable.

  • Helper: _coopXpMul(monster) walks net.peers, returns 1.5 if any peer is on the same map within range, else 1
  • Multiplied into the standard player.exp calculation in killMonster alongside combo / prestige / curve mults
  • Multiplayer modal copy updated with the new co-op bonus tagline

Why the wedge: server-authoritative combat (the README's stated next milestone) is a heavy lift — server has to own monster state, damage events, and loot. This change unlocks 80% of the "we're farming together" experience for ~30 lines of client code, and the multiplayer loop becomes worth running today instead of waiting on the bigger refactor.

v0.25.244 In-game confirm modal + skill-slot unlock toast

featX4 — Browser confirm() replaced with styled in-game modal

Reset save / respec / prestige / boon-discard all used native confirm() popups that broke the visual world (and on mobile look identical to phishing prompts). New uiConfirm({ title, body, yesLabel, noLabel, danger }) Promise helper renders a polished modal that matches the rest of the UI:

  • Reset save: was a double-confirm; now a single in-game modal with red "Erase everything" button
  • Respec: in-game confirm shows the cost
  • Prestige: ascend modal with full bonus breakdown rendered inline
  • Boon discard: red "Discard" button when destructive

The modal is registered in closeAllModals() so Esc dismisses it (defaults to "No"). Falls back to native confirm() only if the markup is somehow missing.

featX5 — New skill slot triggers an unlock toast

Hitting a level threshold (5 / 10 / 15 / 20 / 25 / 30 / 49) now fires a dedicated toast: "🔓 X-slot unlocked: [Skill Name] — [first sentence of desc]". Pulls from SLOT_LEVEL_REQ + the current class kit so the toast names whatever skill became available. No more silently expanded skill bars.

v0.25.243 UX & accessibility pass — 6 first-session wins

polishX1 — Death screen names the killer

Death overlay used to say "Returning to Everdawn Village..." with no context. Now: "💀 Defeated by [enemy name] · Returning to Everdawn Village...". Tracks player._lastDamageSource in the contact-damage and projectile-damage paths so the most recent hit is named.

polishX2 — Skill unlock toast carries effect description

Tree-node unlock toast went from "✦ Unlocked: Berserker Mastery" to "✦ Unlocked: Berserker Mastery — +50% ATK while raging". Pulls the first sentence of node.desc; falls back to bare name if desc is missing.

polishX3 — NPC dialog auto-dismisses on walk-away

Walking > 110 px from the active NPC now auto-closes the dialog. Tracks game._activeNpc in openNPC; per-frame distance check in updatePlayer; cleared in closeDialog. Removes the friction of "click to open shop, glance at prices, hit Esc to leave" — you can just walk.

polishX6 — First-session tip toast for the hotkey panel

After class pick, surface a one-time localStorage-gated toast: "💡 Tip: the hotkey panel (top-left) shows your skills. Press ? for full controls." Backed by a generic _firstTimeTip(key, txt) helper.

polishX8 — Toast region is now screen-reader accessible

Every toast now carries role="status" + aria-live="polite", so VoiceOver / NVDA / TalkBack announce drops, level-ups, deaths, and tutorial tips without interrupting other UI announcements.

featS3 — World Map discoverability at Lv 5

Hitting Lv 5 fires a one-time toast: "🗺️ Press W to open the world map — fast-travel between unlocked areas." The world map (and Taxi Uncle) is currently hidden behind two layers of discoverability; many new players never find it. Same one-shot pattern as X6.

v0.25.242 Balance pass — 6 tuning ratchets across enhancement / XP / assassin / mage

polishG1 — Star enhancement curve flattened, success floor raised

The ★4–7 cost shoulder was a wall most players bounced off. Old curve cumulative ~99,000 Lumens with a 5% success floor; new curve cumulative ~70,000 with a 15% floor. ★8–10 stay punishing but reachable. Costs shifted: ★4 800 → 1500, ★5 1500 → 1500, ★6 3000 → 1500, ★7 6000 → 2000, ★8 12000 → 8000, ★9 25000 → 20000, ★10 50000 → 35000.

polishG2 — Lv 25–39 XP grind softened

The mid-grind was the longest dead-zone in the curve (~8–12 hours). Cut multipliers: 20–24 1.45 → 1.40, 25–29 1.45 → 1.40, 30–39 1.50 → 1.42. Endgame (40+) curve unchanged so the ascend-to-50 ceremony still feels earned.

polishG3 — Phantom + Nightreaper G now respect DEF

Both ultimates wrote damage directly to target.currentHp with guaranteed crit, bypassing DEF entirely — tanky elites melted regardless of build investment. Reworked:

  • Nightreaper Mark: ATK ×2.2 (always crit) → ATK ×1.8 with 50% DEF reduction and 60% crit-bias
  • Phantom Cut: ATK ×3.2 (always crit) → ATK ×2.6 with 40% DEF reduction and 70% crit-bias

Net DPS on squishy mobs is similar; tanky bosses now actually trade with the skill instead of dissolving.

polishG4 — Assassin CDR refund cap

Assassin job's cdRefundOnKill was 30% with no internal cooldown — chain kills in AoE clears reset every cooldown, locking a power ceiling above other rogue subs. Now 15% with a 2 s gate so a single multi-hit doesn't refund off every mob.

polishG5 — Tier-5 zone level requirements raised

v0.25.225 rebalanced map level reqs but didn't adjust monster ATK to match. Two zones now match the new XP curve:

  • levelReq 24 → 26 (gives players two extra gear levels before the wraith / skeleton wall)
  • levelReq 28 → 30 (tier-5 boss prep)

polishG6 — Mage Chain Cast 1.5 s internal cooldown

Chain Cast (1.5× damage on alternating skills within 1 s) had no internal cooldown. With multishot affixes, every chain triggered 6 empowered hits — broke single-class power curve. Trigger now fires at most once per 1.5 s.

v0.25.241 Performance pass — Y-cull + tighter particle bounds + frame budget

polishP4 — full off-screen cull on monster draw

drawMonster() only checked the X-axis off-screen, so aura draws + particle emissions still fired for mobs above/below the viewport on tall maps. Added a Y-axis cull (sy + m.h < -30 || sy > H + 30) right after the existing X check. Estimated saving: −0.6 to −1 ms/frame on tall maps.

polishP5 — tighter particle cull margin + first-pass life skip

drawParticles() uses two passes (halo + crisp core). The halo pass kept emitting for old particles whose alpha curve had already faded the glow below visibility. Tightened cull margin from ±30 to ±10, and added a p.life > 250 skip for the halo pass. Estimated saving: −0.8 to −1.2 ms/frame in dense particle scenes.

polishP7 — per-frame "extras" particle budget

Burst-spike frames (Nightreaper ricochet + ice AoE + multishot stacked) could dump 200+ particles in one frame, causing stutter even after the queue cap. New _budgetedParticlePush(p) helper that decorative emitters can route through; first 120 (desktop) / 60 (mobile) particles per frame go through, the rest are skipped. Counter resets in _trimVisualQueues. Load-bearing skill FX still fire unconditionally.

v0.25.240 Bug-fix sweep: 5 plan items (B1–B5)

bugB1 — dead string-vs-object comparison removed (HIGH)

Line 17935's if (game.currentMap === game.mapData ...) compared a string id to an object — always false, the early-return never fired. The bug was masked by the next guard's !mapD.isTown check, but the dead expression was a footgun for future edits. Removed.

bugB2 — closeAllModals null-guards forced-modal lookups

closeAllModals() read cs.style.display and av.style.display on un-guarded getElementById results. If either modal hadn't been injected yet (or got removed), the throw broke Esc + X across every overlay. Now both forced-modal lookups + the dialog close are null-guarded.

bugB3 — defensive defaulters on save load

Object.assign(player, save.player) doesn't add missing fields. Older saves predating skillCooldowns, buffs, consumables, equipped, or inventory would crash on next access. Added explicit defaults at the load site so any save schema gap fills cleanly.

bugB4 — divide-by-zero clamps in damage scaling

player.hp / getMaxHp() and player.mp / getMaxMp() appear in 6 buff-scaling formulas (Berserker passive, Blood Rage, Berserker tree, Arcane Surge, Second Wind, etc.). If a (theoretical) boon ever drops max to 0 the result becomes NaN/Infinity. All call sites now divide by Math.max(1, getMaxHp()) / Math.max(1, getMaxMp()).

bugB5 — _trimVisualQueues now runs every frame

The trim helper existed (_trimVisualQueues() at line 18923) but had no caller. Particle / afterImage / damage-number arrays would grow unbounded on burst-spike frames (Nightreaper ricochet + AoE in one frame can dump 200 particles). Wired into the main RAF loop right after updateUI(); uses the existing mobile-aware _particleCap() / _afterImageCap() helpers.

v0.25.239 Enhancement Forge UI overhaul · star badges on equipment

featAnvil sprite + polished forge mood

The Enhancement Forge modal got a major visual upgrade. A custom Ludo-AI anvil sprite (Sprites/ui/anvil.webp — transparent background, glowing forge fire, golden sparks) now floats on the left of the panel and gently bobs idle. The whole modal background gets a warm radial forge-glow, the title is a gold-to-orange gradient, the preview card has a subtle amber border, and the Forge button has a continuous sheen sweep so it pulls the eye. Anvil hides itself on viewports under 540 px so mobile is unaffected.

featStar count badges on every equipment surface

Once an item has been enhanced, a tiny golden ★N chip floats on the upper-left of its slot — visible in the inventory grid (B and the Items tab in U), in the equipped slot row, and on the enhance modal's own list. Tier color shifts with star count:

  • ★1–4 — gold gradient
  • ★5–7 — orange gradient (mid-tier)
  • ★8–10 — magenta-violet gradient with white text (legendary)

The badge has a slow brightness shimmer so high-star gear catches the eye even in a packed inventory. aria-label="N stars enhanced" for screen readers.

polishForge feedback animations

  • Success: the anvil rocks + glows on each successful star (one quick hammer-stroke); a star-shaped spark burst erupts radially from the anvil with an expanding gold ring
  • Failure: the anvil still rocks once but the modal pulses red (fail-flash); no sparks
  • Selected card now slides 3 px right + gets a soft amber inner-glow so the active item is unambiguous

polishWiring details

  • Anvil added to BAZAAR + DEFERRED preloader sets (also fetchPriority=high on cold load)
  • _starBadgeHtml(it) helper used everywhere — single source of truth for the badge markup
  • _playForgeAnim('success' / 'fail') helper handles the reflow-and-replay pattern so the animations always retrigger even on rapid forging

featEleven Ludo-AI skill sprites shipped or upgraded

Big visual upgrade pass for under-served kit slots. Each sprite is a Cartoonish 2D platformer cel-shaded VFX, transparent background, sized for chibi side-scrolling combat:

  • Skill funcs use spawnSpriteBurst with appropriate size/life/spin parameters per skill aesthetic
  • elemental_link sprite spawns once per chain hop (up to 6 hops in Elemental Convergence); 80 px size, 22-frame life, fast spin

v0.25.237 Bazaar-priority loader · clone tuning · CDR-immune assassin ults

featThree-tier loader prioritises Everdawn Bazaar

The preloader now has a BAZAAR tier ahead of CRITICAL. Only the ~14 sprites the player sees the moment they spawn into Everdawn Bazaar (hero face/hair/eyes/mouth, the bazaar bg, the 6 bazaar NPCs, walkway tiles, portal) gate the world reveal. UI tabs + dialog box dropped to a second tier that loads with high priority right after reveal but no longer blocks the loading screen. Net effect: reveal gate shrunk from ~21 → ~14 sprites, and the bazaar paint isn't held up by UI assets the player isn't looking at yet. Hard fallback dropped 5 s → 4 s.

  • Loading status copy reworked to bazaar-flavored phrases: "Painting Everdawn Bazaar…", "Lighting the lanterns…", "Stocking Brok's anvil…"
  • BAZAAR sprites still get fetchPriority='high' + img.decode() like before
  • UI tier (dialog box, char_header, tab_*) now starts immediately after BAZAAR fires, parallel-loading while the player is already in town
  • DEFERRED tier behavior unchanged — still streams via requestIdleCallback with the corner-pill progress bar from v0.25.235

polishShadowlord G — long-range turret screen

Mirror Shadow tuned for sustained-control gameplay:

  • Lifetime: 4 s → 15 s
  • Cooldown: 20 s → 22 s — uptime sits at ~68%
  • Spawn fan distance: 130 px → 320 px per side. Clones now plant themselves far from the player, projecting their AOE rings across most of the visible width without overlapping
  • Toast updated to "✦ MIRROR SHADOW — 3 floating clones, 15s"

polishShadowlord V (Death Blossom) — fast cycle, 5-target cap

  • Cooldown: 20 s → 8 s for tight rotational play
  • Each of the 3 waves now strikes up to 5 closest enemies in radius (was unlimited). Pairs the faster cycle with a tighter target cap so it doesn't clear entire rooms by itself
  • Damage per hit unchanged (ATK × 1.15)

bugPhantom + Nightreaper G — CDR-immune at 12 s

Both assassin ultimates were drifting below 12 s with stacked WIS CDR + skill-tree CDR + the JOB_CD_MUL blanket modifier. The earlier v0.25.226 floor (Math.max(12000, computedCd)) only kicked in when CDR pushed below the floor, so the listed cooldown didn't match what players saw. Both skills now lock at exactly 12 s regardless of CDR. Skill table cooldowns updated from 30 s/28 s base to a flat 12 s, and the description tags "Fixed 12 s CD (CDR-immune)" so it's clear in tooltips.

v0.25.236 Shadowlord clones reworked into levitating AOE turrets

featFloating summons, fixed positions

The Shadowlord G ultimate (Mirror Shadow) used to orbit the player like escorts — they drifted along whenever you moved, which meant repositioning yanked your DPS with you and walls/ledges occasionally cut their swings short. The three clones now anchor to the world at the moment of cast and hover in place with a gentle bob animation. They behave like spirit turrets you drop, not pets that follow.

featCircular AOE strike (no more directional hitbox)

Each clone pulses an 110 px radius circular AOE every ~400 ms, hitting up to 5 monsters per pulse — anything inside the ring gets struck regardless of which direction the clone is facing. Damage rebalanced to ATK × 1.1 + 6 per hit (down from ×1.4) since you can now catch ringed-up packs of mobs much more reliably. Net DPS on a single target lands close to the old behavior; AOE clears are dramatically faster.

polishVisible AOE telegraph

  • Persistent faint violet ring drawn on the floor under each clone — you can see the strike radius at a glance
  • Ring brightens + thickens during each pulse so the strike timing is readable
  • 360° spinning sweep ring around the clone body replaces the old directional crescent slash
  • Drop-shadow puddle on the ground beneath each clone reinforces the "levitating" read
  • Clones spawn further apart (130 px fan, was 80 px) so their AOEs cover more territory without overlapping fully

v0.25.235 Persistent corner loader for deferred sprites

featIn-game asset-stream pill

Added #defer-loader — a tiny top-right pill that fades in after the world reveals, showing how many of the v0.25.234 DEFERRED sprites are still streaming. So if the player alt-tabs in or starts running around town immediately, they can see at a glance whether the boss bgs / master FX / biome tiles have finished decoding.

polishPill design

  • Tiny spinning ring icon + text "Loading 32/95" + 60 px progress bar
  • Backdrop blur, soft purple border, gold-and-violet bar gradient — matches the loading screen palette
  • pointer-events: none + user-select: none so it doesn't capture clicks or interrupt gameplay
  • Hides itself with a 400 ms fade once defLoaded === DEFERRED.length — gone the moment everything is decoded

v0.25.234 Tiered preloader + mobile warm-up — faster reveal, smoother first seconds

featTiered loading: critical first, defer the rest

The all-or-nothing v0.25.224 preloader blocked the world reveal until all ~120 sprites finished decoding — slow on mobile. Split into two phases:

  • CRITICAL (~21 sprites): town bg, town NPCs, hero base + face layers, first-biome tiles, dialog box + U-panel UI, portal. Loaded in parallel with fetchPriority='high' + img.decode() — guaranteed ready-to-paint before world reveal.
  • DEFERRED (~95 sprites): boss bgs, master-class FX, summons, all biome tiles + bgs, mob projectiles. Started via requestIdleCallback after critical finishes — streams in background while the player explores town.

Loading bar fills from CRITICAL only, so the percentage progresses much faster on screen. Hard fallback dropped 12 s → 5 s for the smaller critical bucket.

featDecode + fetchpriority hints

Each loader image now uses img.decoding = 'async' + img.fetchPriority = 'high' (critical only) + img.decode() on completion. The decode promise gives the browser a chance to pre-rasterise so the first frame on world reveal doesn't stall.

featMobile starts in low-FX warm-up

LX_PERF.lowFx now defaults to true on mobile (pointer: coarse OR max-width: 900px) for the first 8 seconds of play. The adaptive heuristic continues to run, so:

  • Mid-tier phones with consistently fast frames release the gate after the warm-up window expires.
  • Low-end phones never escape lowFx — the additive glow halo + extra particle counts stay disabled, keeping the framerate playable.
  • Desktop is unaffected — still starts at full effects and only drops to lowFx after 12 sustained slow frames.

v0.25.233 Archer F wolf sprite + Mojiworld BGM loop

bugWolf sprite now shows for archer F (Wild Bond)

Traced why LX_SUMMON.wolf never appeared on the F-skill summon: drawPet() only routed the BEASTMASTER pack array through drawWolf; the single player.pet spawned by wildBond was hand-rendered with procedural rect-art directly in drawPet, bypassing the sprite. Replaced the inlined draw with a single drawWolf(player.pet, null) call so it picks up LX_SUMMON.wolf (or wolf_alpha for beastmaster, wolf_sky for skyhunter).

featMojiworld main BGM

User-supplied BGM mojiworld.mp3.mpeg copied to audio/bgm_mojiworld.mp3 (3.3 MB). Wired as a looping background track that starts the moment the loading screen fades out. Browsers block autoplay before user interaction, so a one-shot pointerdown / keydown / touchstart listener retries the play on first input — guarantees the music kicks in by the time the player presses the arrow key to start moving. Volume sits at 0.55 to stay below SFX. The audio element loops indefinitely via loop = true.

v0.25.232 Aetherion + Gravitos bg fix + better arrow rain sprite

bugAuthored bgs now render in sanctum + singularity arenas

The boss-arena maps for Aetherion (sanctum) and Gravitos (gravitosArena) were configured with explicit bg: 'aetherion' / bg: 'gravitosArena' back in v0.25.213, but the bg renderer kept falling through to a procedural sky gradient. Traced the root cause:

  • Vanilla path _pickBGImage (line 21218): had an early-return at the top — if (md.sanctum || md.singularity || ...) return null; — which fired BEFORE the md.bg override check.
  • Phaser path pickBgKey (line 2934): same ordering bug.

Both render paths now check the explicit md.bg override FIRST. The early-return for "special backdrops without authored art" is preserved as a fallback for any map that genuinely doesn't want a bitmap. Boss arenas with their own bg keys (sanctum / gravitosArena) finally show the authored Ludo art.

featBetter arrow rain sprite

Regenerated fx/arrow_rain.webp with a denser, more iconic bundle of 15+ sharp golden arrows in a tight downward fan, steel arrowheads with flame trim, golden mist at the impact base. Replaces the earlier sprite which read more as a sparse diagonal scatter.

v0.25.226 Phantom + Nightreaper G — hard 12-second cooldown floor

balanceCooldown floor on assassin master G skills

Per user request, ensured phantom_cut and nightreaper_mark always recharge for at least 12 seconds. Both have generous base cooldowns (28 s and 30 s respectively), but stacked CDR (mage class 0.70× × WIS up-to-40% × blanket -25%) could collapse the effective cd well below 12 s. Added computedCd = Math.max(12000, computedCd) branch in the cooldown-apply path scoped to these two skill ids.

SkillBase cdBest-case CDR floor

nightreaper_mark (Blink Barrage)30 s≥ 12 s (was ~11.3 s w/ max stacks)

v0.25.223 World map redesigned as a clickable SVG diagram (W key + Taxi share it)

featDiagram-style world map

Replaced the prior bucket-grouped grid of cards with a single SVG diagram. Hub town sits at the centre with concentric tier rings around it: Beginner (Lv 1–4) → Intermediate (Lv 5–14) → Advanced (Lv 15–29) → Endgame (Lv 30+). Boss arenas pin to the bottom corners; the Tower of Ascension pins to the top-right. Subtle dashed connection edges link the hub to every ring node. Background gradient + sparkle stars give the map a celestial feel. Each node is a clickable disc with the biome's emoji icon, name, and sub-label (level requirement / fare / lock reason).

featShared by W key + Taxi NPC

New _renderWorldMapDiagram(host, opts) takes an isAccessible(id, m) predicate and an onPick(id, m) handler — letting the same SVG render power two different fast-travel modes:

  • W key (renderWorldMap): any map at or below player level is reachable; clicking warps via loadMap. Higher-level maps render dimmed with a 🔒 sub-label.
  • Taxi NPC (renderTaxi): only visited / taxiAccessible maps are reachable, boss arenas always blocked, fare gating (50💰) baked into the predicate. Clicking deducts the fare and warps.

polishModal containers widened

Both worldmap-modal and taxi-modal bumped to min-width:780px / max-width:880-900px to fit the 760-px-wide diagram cleanly. Removed the old grid-with-overflow scroll containers — the diagram is fixed-size + responsive via SVG preserveAspectRatio.

polishVisual affordances

  • Current map: gold halo + cream label + "▸ YOU ARE HERE" sub-label
  • Inaccessible map: dimmed disc + tier-coloured ring + reason text in muted red
  • Hover any disc to grow it from r=19 to r=22 (cursor: pointer)
  • Tier-colour legend strip along the bottom of the diagram
  • <title> tooltips on every node show full name + level + status

v0.25.219 Rogue / thief now uses a forward dagger thrust attack animation

featNew attack_rogue animation — committed forward dagger thrust

Per user request: the thief class now does a knife-stab thrust instead of inheriting the warrior's wide swing. Built two new bone-curve helpers:

  • _heroVecRogueFrontArm(t) — tiny windup pull to −0.70, then SNAP forward to +1.55 (just past horizontal so the dagger points forward), brief held tremor at full extension, smooth retract back to neutral.
  • _heroVecRogueBackArm(t) — off-hand drifts back slightly during the thrust for body balance, stays settled, then returns.

New entries added to:

  • HERO_VEC_ANIMS.attack_rogue — modest spine + head lean forward, light leg squat
  • HERO_VEC_DEFORM.attack_rogue — front arm stretches lengthwise on the thrust to sell the lunge reach; hand grows slightly at full extension
  • HERO_VEC_BOB.attack_rogue — sharp 2 px forward poke + 0.8 px recoil pull (less than the warrior's 5.5 px lurch since a dagger is small + quick)

polishDispatcher + time-norm wiring

_heroVecAnimFor now returns 'attack_rogue' when player.cls === 'rogue'. _heroVecTimeNorm recognises the new anim name so the shared attack timer drives it identically to warrior / archer / mage variants. Slash-arc trail visual stays gated to the warrior-style swings (a thrust doesn't have an arc).

Previously: airborne-only 6-strike V-slash combo. Now: classic Naruto-style flash-step.
