Harder to kill

  • HP bumped ~1.5× on top of v0.10.4's 1.7× pass. Snailkin 38 → 60 · Goober 62 → 95 · Mushie 105 → 165 · Hornsy 190 → 290 · Sunny 260 → 395 · Stumpling 350 → 530 · Grimmy 450 → 680 · Pincho 310 → 470 · Bandie 560 → 840 · Bonesy 380 → 570 · Ghostie 480 → 720. Bosses bumped ~50%: King Blobby 2000 → 3000, Mama Capling 4200 → 6300, Aetherion 28000 → 42000, Gravitos 45000 → 68000.
  • Flat DEF per mob. Each monster type now has a def field (1 on Snailkin up to 11 on Bandie). hitMonster subtracts def from final damage after combo/tower multipliers; result is floored to 1 min so mobs never go immune.
  • Elite / mini-boss / boss DEF scaling. defVal *= 1.4 on elites, × 1.8 on mini-bosses, × 2.2 on bosses. Big HP pools are now complemented by meaningful damage floor-loss — early-game skill spam won't chew through bosses any more.
  • Ballista exemption. siegeVolley and any skill tagged breakDef bypass DEF entirely, preserving the fantasy that ballista pierces armor.

✦Eye-catching damage font

Big rewrite of drawDamageNumbers() for a chunkier, more arcade-y feel.

  • Font. Swapped from Trebuchet MS to Impact, "Arial Black", "Trebuchet MS" with weight 900 — the letterforms themselves are thicker and more aggressive.
  • Drop shadow. Every number now paints a darker shadow copy at +2, +3 px (alpha 55%) before the main pass, making text pop off busy backgrounds.
  • Heavy outline. 4.5 px (crit 6 px) round-joined black stroke. Crits add a 2 px gold-foil inner stroke over the black.
  • Gradient fill. Crits render with a top-to-bottom gradient (#fff4b8 → #ffd84a → #ff8a1f) for the gold-foil look; non-crit big hits use a color mixed against white for a similar top-bright → base feel.
  • Specular band. Crits/big hits add a clipped top highlight — horizontal band reserved in the upper 38% of the glyph area, filled white at 70% alpha. Reads as a sheen across the top of the digits.
  • Crit sparkles. 4 tiny + sparkles rotate around the number during the first 8 frames of its life, fading out with age.
  • Bigger overshoot. Pop-in eases to 1.4× (crits 2.6×) before settling; idle bob keeps numbers gently breathing on screen.

v0.13.0 Zodiac · endgame · variation

Huge endgame expansion. 12 horoscope bosses, each with a unique arena, artistic renderer, and three-phase mechanics. Tower carriage gets a streaming spawn model — kill faster, spawn faster. Maps now have per-load variation. Mob names leaned into short & simple.

✦12 Horoscope Bosses

A full endgame arc: one boss per zodiac sign, each with its own map, element, attack pattern, and visual design. Unlock from level 15; difficulty ramps from Aries (tier 1) to Pisces (tier 12). Config lives in ZODIAC_SIGNS; drawing in ZODIAC_DRAW; AI in ZODIAC_AI.

SignNameElementSignature mechanic
♈ AriesAriel the Ember RamFireCharge across arena leaving a fire trail · expanding flame rings
♉ TaurusTaur the Granite BullEarthStomp → 6 ground shockwaves · headbutt charge
♊ GeminiGem & Mini the TwinstarAirSplits into two at phase 2 · dual star-beams
♋ CancerCancer the TidecallerWaterRising homing bubbles · pincer snap · stalked eyes
♌ LeoRegulus the SunmaneFireRoar stuns player (600ms) · fire comets from sky
♍ VirgoVirga the SeraphLightBanishes your projectiles · heals 5% · light pillars
♎ LibraLibra the ScalelordBalanceTwo scale orbs — half damage while either alive · balance beams
♏ ScorpioScorpio the VenomlordPoisonVenom shots apply 3s poison DOT · burrows to flank
♐ SagittariusSagitta the StarchaserArrowArrow rain (8-16) · piercing star-beam
♑ CapricornCaprikor the PeaklordIceIce breath cone · freezes · slippery floor
♒ AquariusAqua the TideswornWaterGround-sweeping waves · homing droplets
♓ PiscesPisces the Twin CurrentWaterOrbits player · 14-spoke whirlpool · pull vortex

Art direction

  • Unified boss canvas. Shared _drawZodiacHalo paints a rotating constellation ring + a pulsing sigil glyph above every zodiac boss. _zBodyPath factors stroke / fill / cel-shadow into one call so every zodiac renders with the same DQ-style contour.
  • Per-sign silhouettes. Each boss has a distinct shape — Aries' woolly body with spiral ram horns rendered procedurally; Cancer's stalked eyes and hinged pincers; Virgo's outstretched wings with individual feather lines; Libra's floating scale with tilting pans and chain links; Pisces orbiting twin fish with a central whirlpool.
  • Phase crackle. Phase transitions spawn a 40-frame electric particle burst in the boss's aura color.

Arena design

Each zodiac arena is a 1800-wide map at zod_<id> with the sign's element dictating ambient decor via drawZodiacArena:

  • Giant faded glyph painted behind the whole scene in the sign's color.
  • Constellation dots — 14 stars twinkle at positions seeded from the sign's order, with connecting lines linking the first 6 into the sign's shape.
  • Element decor. Fire = lava floor line + rising embers; Water = rippling bottom waves + floating bubbles; Earth = rock silhouettes with parallax; Air = wind streaks; Ice = frost crystals + snowfall; Poison = toxic sludge line + bubble spores; Light = divine god-ray shafts; Arrow = silhouettes of arrows stuck in the ground.

Zodiac Sanctum hub

New zodiacHall map accessible from the town's leftmost portal (⭐ Zodiac Sanctum). A 2200-wide purple marble hall with 12 portals — one per sign — arranged left-to-right by zodiac order. A central rotating wheel shows all 12 glyphs. Starfield background, 14 decorative pillars between portals.

Mechanics / stats

  • HP scales from 16,500 (Aries) to 66,000 (Pisces). ATK from 78 to 166. DEF from 16 to 38.
  • 3 phases at 66% / 33% HP with shortened attack cycles and stronger mechanics each tier.
  • Libra's _libraShield halves all incoming damage while either scale orb survives — must be burned down first.
  • New projectile flags plumbed through the engine: homing: true (enemy-owned projectiles gently steer toward the player), freeze: <ms>, poison: <ms>. Player update loop now ticks a poison DOT every 45 frames with its own damage number.
  • Win rewards use the normal boss drop table (large Lumens + epic/legendary roll).

✦Carriage streaming spawns

Old model: _towerBeginFloor dumped all wave mobs on the floor at once and waited for a full clear. New model splits the wave into spawn queue + live-count cap:

  • Each floor has a total mob budget (waveTotal) but only maxAlive live at once (2-5 depending on floor).
  • When a mob dies, the next spawn is queued with a timer that shrinks by 60 ms per kill, from a 1600 ms base down to a 220 ms floor — kill streaks make the carriage feel relentless.
  • Spawned mobs burst in with a gold/white particle puff (_towerSpawnOne).
  • Wave cap raised to 14 mobs per floor so the streaming model has runway.

Map variation pass

New _variedMapData(id) wraps MAPS[id] on every loadMap:

  • Y-jitter (±10 px) + width-jitter (±10 px) on every non-ground platform so jumps and sight-lines feel slightly different each run.
  • 50% chance surprise platform at a random mid-map position (width/y also randomized) on big maps.
  • Mob count jitter (±25%) on non-boss spawns.
  • 8% rare wanderer — one mismatched mob type injects itself into a non-boss map (slime, mushroom, horny, stump, scorpion, or wraith) for flavour.
  • Town, boss arenas, and tower skip the shuffle (fixedLayout flag). Zodiac arenas opt in via fixedLayout: true.

v0.13.1 Unified art pass

NPCs, town buildings, platforms, chests, and portals all now share the same 2-shade DQ cel-shading as the character and mobs. One visual language across the whole screen.

NPCs
DQ cel-head + torso
Thicker 2 px outline · hard shadow wedge
Town
Flat 2-tone buildings
No gradients · hard vertical cel seam
Platforms
Ground + wood cel
Upper lit / lower shadow + black seam
Chests
Rounded lid cel
Clipped polygon shadow · keyhole + gem
Portals
Stone frame + swirl
Frame cel · flat-tone magic swirl · rivets

NPCs

  • Chibi scale bumped to match the player (1.19, 1.06) — NPCs were still on the old 0.97 height so they looked shorter than the hero.
  • Head — outline ring thickened (hr + 1 → hr + 2), crescent shadow replaced with a hard polygon clipped to the head circle (same technique as the player / mobs).
  • Torso — 2 px stepped outline on every seam (was 1 px). Hard diagonal cel shadow wedge clipped to the body rect so the lit/shadow boundary is a single crisp line rather than a soft band.
  • Legs + boots — dedicated outline halo rects before each fill, matching the player's new leg treatment.

Town buildings

drawTownDecor rewritten around the DQ cel rules:

  • Removed the 3-tone soft blend (deepShd → shd → mid → wall → lit). Buildings now use just two flats — lit wall + shadow wall — separated by a thin #1a0818 vertical seam at 68% of the width.
  • Thick 2 px outline around the whole silhouette.
  • Window frames get an outline-then-fill pass; windows that sit on the shadow side paint their lit fill, then overlay a dark flat over the right half so they match the building's cel partition.
  • Door re-designed with outline, lit base, right-half shadow flat, thin seam, and a brass handle.
  • Rooftop parapet + shop plaque follow the same 2-tone rule.

Platforms

  • Ground (grass + dirt). Old: 3-4 layered dirt tones + mid-tone bands + grass gradient. New: grass is two flat colors (#6cb847 lit, darker step below), dirt is two flat colors (#8b6f47 top, #5a4027 lower), all separated by crisp 1 px black seams. Tufts + flowers simplified to flat 2-tone.
  • Wood platforms. Single lit tone on top half, single shadow tone on bottom half, horizontal black seam in the middle. Plank separators and nail outlines pure #1a0818. No gradient, no grain squiggles.
  • Result: jump pads read cleanly at a glance, consistent with the character/mob silhouettes jumping over them.

Chests

  • Body outline (2 px halo rect) + 2 flat fills (lit/shadow) with a vertical cel seam at 55% width.
  • Lid is a rounded cap with its OWN outline pass + clipped shadow polygon (so the upper curve of the lid shows the wedge, not a gradient).
  • Lock plate is now a true plate — outline + lit face + darker right half + keyhole. Small gem sparkle above the lock breathes with a sine pulse.
  • Opened state: dark interior rect + flipped lid bar.
  • All three tiers (wood / silver / gold) share the structure; only the lit/shadow/trim/gem colors change.

Portals

Old portal was three animated rings + a soft alpha blob. New portal is a real stone archway:

  • Frame. Thick black outer rim, lit stone fill, hard diagonal shadow wedge clipped to the ellipse.
  • Swirl. Two solid purple flats (outer + inner) with a crisp black seam between them. Three rotating inner ellipses in escalating darkness act as the "magic swirl" — all flat, no gradient.
  • Rivets. 4 cardinal studs (outlined flat circle + lighter centre).
  • Floating white sparkles orbit inside as before.

v0.13.2 Potions · art polish

Quick-use potion hotkeys moved to PgUp / PgDn with auto-buy fallback when inventory is empty. Building and portal outlines dropped for a softer look; portals are translucent; town plaza floor cel-shaded; layered aesthetic background replaces the flat mountain silhouette.

Potion hotkeys + gold fallback

  • PgUp consumes a red HP potion. PgDn consumes a blue MP potion. Old R / T aliases kept so muscle memory still works.
  • If the player has no potion of the requested type, useQuickPotion now falls back to the smallest same-type potion the player can afford and deducts Lumens directly. Shows an auto-buy toast with the price so the spend is visible.
  • If the player can't afford even the cheapest potion, a muted hit sfx + "Need X Lumens" toast fires — no accidental zero-gold death.
  • README + in-game help panel updated to show the new bindings.

Building outlines removed

The thick #1a0818 outline rects around every town high-rise are gone. Buildings now read as pure 2-tone silhouettes — lit wall + shadow side with a clean tonal break at 68% width. Windows drop their outline; their only structure is the 2-tone fill + a 1 px internal divider (in a shadow tone, not pure black). Doors and shop plaques same treatment.

Translucent portals

drawPortals rewritten to drop all hard outlines and lean into additive glow + alpha layers:

  • Outer additive halo (radial gradient, 70×80 ellipse) for ambient glow.
  • Translucent stone frame (globalAlpha 0.55) with a destination-out cutout for the portal interior — no hard edge between frame and void.
  • Two translucent purple swirl layers (60% and 55% alpha) with no black seam between them.
  • Three rotating additive-blend interior arcs at ~38% alpha — reads as magical motion rather than solid shapes.
  • Rivets at cardinal positions drop to 55% alpha flat ovals.
  • Sparkles use globalCompositeOperation: lighter so they bloom against the translucent interior.

Cel-shaded floor

  • Town plaza walkway — old two-rect flat design replaced with a 4-band cel: lit top stripe (#d6cfbe) → crisp seam → shadow band → darker curb strip. Cobble tone-marks dash across every 44 px for visual rhythm.
  • Ground platform dirt — was 2-band, now 3-band: sunlit ochre top (#a08050, 6 px) → seam → midtone (#7a5a38, 14 px) → seam → deep soil (#4a3018, rest). Adds pebble motes in the lit band and root tufts in the shadow band so the floor reads as scenery rather than a coloured rectangle.

Aesthetic layered background

The old single-mountain + round cloud fallback is gone. New drawBackground fallback renders:

  • Celestial disc. Sun on bright maps, moon on dark maps (auto-detected via _hexLuma of the sky color). Soft radial halo via additive blend. Moon gets a crescent shadow circle; sun gets a warm amber inner core.
  • Starfield. On dark maps, 50 twinkling stars drift with subtle camera parallax and phase-offset shimmer.
  • Two mountain ranges. Far range (4% parallax, low-contrast tint) + mid range (8% parallax, blue-gray tint). Mid range now gets procedural snow caps — small triangular fills on every local peak.
  • Pine treeline. 20 two-tier pine silhouettes as foreground parallax (18% shift), tone-matched to the sky's lowest color.
  • Clouds reshaped. Each cloud is now a 4-lobe puff with a dedicated underside shadow layer (a 2-tone cloud instead of flat white circles).
  • Birds. On bright maps, 4 M-shape silhouetted birds drift with flapping wings at 12% parallax + slow scroll.

v0.14.0 QoL · Amnesiac · mobile · radar

Big quality-of-life + mobile release. Town regenerates HP/MP instantly, potions get a 3 s shared cooldown with gold-fallback buying, "Master Ren" becomes The Amnesiac with a dramatic reset flow, weapons change visually with what's equipped and swing more smoothly, the level-up screen gains a live radar chart, and the whole game is now fully playable on touch screens.

Town instant regen

While on the town map (game.mapData.isTown), both HP and MP regenerate every single frame for ~4% of max per tick. Makes the town feel like a proper safe haven — step out of the dungeon, breathe, and you're instantly topped off for the next run. Combat maps keep the old gradual regen rates.

Potion cooldown (3 s)

  • New POTION_CD_MS = 3000 constant with separate HP / MP tracks (player._potionCdHp, player._potionCdMp) so tanking and mana-burn tick independently.
  • useQuickPotion gates on _potionReady at the top — tap on cooldown shows a toast with seconds remaining + muted hit sfx.
  • Cooldown stamps after both successful inventory use AND gold-fallback purchase, so exploits aren't a thing.

✦The Amnesiac (formerly Master Ren)

The skills-trainer NPC in the town bazaar has been re-characterised. The ominous robed figure who lost his name — and now offers to unmake yours.

  • 4-stage dramatic dialog (game._amnesiacStage). Each stage has its own text block and branching options:
    1. Ominous greeting + normal stat/LP shortcuts.
    2. Backstory — "the World drank me empty."
    3. The offer — reset everything with stark warning.
    4. Final verbal confirmation — "Say: I wish to forget."
  • Reset runs through _amnesiacReset() — no confirm() popups since the dialog chain IS the confirmation. Adds a fade-to-black overlay ("the door closes behind you…") + flash(0.8) + addShake(24) + audio.play('death') before the reload.
  • The old corner "☠ Reset" HUD button is hidden — reset is now a narrative beat, not a UI pill.
  • NPC palette & role config updated: amnesiac role gets a dark purple robe + silver hair + wizard hat to match the tone.
  • Dialog CSS gains white-space: pre-line so paragraph breaks read properly.

✦Smoother weapon swing + equipped-weapon art

Both drawCuteSwingingBlade and drawCuteWeapon rewritten around a palette-driven piece renderer.

  • New _weaponPalette() reads the equipped weapon's vis block (every gear entry in ITEM_POOL already has one) and returns a blade/hi/shd/guard/gold/glow bundle. Falls back to CUTE_PAL for unequipped characters.
  • Swing arc now uses easeOutBack across a wider ~1.05π arc — crisper windup, visible overshoot at the peak.
  • Three trail ghost frames render at offset angles with globalCompositeOperation: 'lighter', producing a proper motion-blur feel.
  • Slash crescent is thicker (7 px) with a bright 3 px inner line, tinted by the weapon's glow color (legendary blades draw their own hue).
  • Weapon itself is a larger, outlined silhouette. Warriors get a new pointed tip via path, outlined crossguard, grip, and pommel with a rarity-colored trim dot (blue/purple/gold). Rogues get the same treatment at shorter proportions. Mages get a full staff with orb + additive glow halo. Archers get a bow with optional drawn arrow (fires during attack frames).
  • Every piece respects vis.glow — equipping the Dawnshard Blade gives you a mint-green aura, the Enchanted Katana a violet pulse, etc.

✦Radar chart level-up

The U / LP spending screen now shows a live 6-axis radar graph of your build alongside the LP lanes.

  • Canvas radar at 280×280 — one vertex per lane (HP, MP, ATK, DEF, Crit, Speed).
  • 4 concentric rings for visual tick marks + 6 axis spokes.
  • Outer amber polygon = lane cap. Inner filled polygon = current investment (ratio of spent/cap). Each vertex gets an outlined amber dot.
  • Labels rendered outside each vertex (e.g. "HP 12/40") with live colour — green when maxed, amber while investing.
  • Cards on the right have inline progress bars + "spent / cap" counters — everything redraws the moment a point is spent, so the build shape visibly morphs as you invest.

🕹Mobile on-screen controls

The game is now fully playable on touch screens. New #mobile-ctrl overlay auto-shows on coarse-pointer devices (or screens under 900 px wide).

  • D-pad (bottom-left): ◀ ▶ ▲ ▼ buttons for left/right movement, portal-enter (up), drop-through-platform (down).
  • Jump button (large, bottom-right, amber) — 76 px circular press target.
  • Basic attack (bottom-right, crimson) — the D slot.
  • Skill grid (4×2): S, A, E, W, Q, C, X skills + interact key, all labeled by slot letter so the UI matches the on-screen skill bar.
  • Top-right stack: HP potion (♥), MP potion (◆), Level-up, Inventory.
  • All buttons dispatch real KeyboardEvents via _mkeyDispatch so the existing keyboard logic handles everything — no divergent code paths. pointerdown / pointerup (+ cancel / leave) cover touch and mouse.
  • Audio auto-initializes on first button tap (satisfies mobile autoplay policy).
  • Smart key mapping — slot letters on the labels (S, A, E…) dispatch the actual keyboard keys (x, s, c…) per KEY_TO_SLOT.
  • Tap ✕ in the top-right to hide the overlay on hybrid devices (reappears on reload or class-toggle).
  • touch-action: manipulation + pointerevents-only children disable page scrolling / zoom over button regions.
  • Narrow-screen media query (< 500 px) shrinks button sizes further for small phones.

Block / Parry in the skill dock

The A keyboard action (Block / Parry) is now a permanent leading slot in renderSkillBar. Shows live state:

  • Icon — 🛡 normally, ⚡ the instant a parry fires (while player.parryWindow is open).
  • Label — "Block" when ready; countdown seconds while on cooldown.
  • Ready-glow when blockCD === 0.

  • Blue-tinted border + gradient background so it reads as defense rather than a skill cast.

✦Skills Reference modal (I)

New openSkillsReference() function — press I to open. Lists every A–V keyboard binding in a two-column grid:

  • Skill rows (C / D / F / G / S / V) read the most-specific skill for that slot via skillsForClass(cls, job, master) + specificity scoring. Shows the icon, name, MP cost, cooldown, and full description. Greyed-out placeholder when a slot hasn't been unlocked yet (e.g. "Unlocks at Master (Lv 20)" for X).
  • Defense row (A) shows Block/Parry mechanics.
  • Menu rows (B inventory, I this panel, K/U level up, M mute, N codex) each list what they open.
  • Item rows (R = HP alias, T = MP alias) note the PgUp/PgDn mains.
  • Unbound rows (H, J, L, O, P, Q) are rendered at low opacity for completeness.
  • Each row is colour-coded by category — amber for skills, blue for defense, pink for items, cool-blue for menus, grey for unbound.
  • Scrollable (max-height 440 px) so everything fits on shorter screens.

Help panel (?) also updated to show the new I binding.

v0.14.2 Mobile fullscreen

The game now locks to the mobile viewport — no more scrolling or pinch-zoom. The 960×560 canvas scales to fit any screen while preserving aspect ratio, and a rotate-to-landscape nag helps portrait users get the best fit.

Viewport + scroll lock

  • Added the missing <meta name="viewport"> with width=device-width, initial-scale=1, maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no, viewport-fit=cover.
  • Added apple-mobile-web-app-capable, mobile-web-app-capable, theme-color, and apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style=black-translucent for a near-native feel when installed to Home Screen.
  • html, body pinned to 100dvh (dynamic viewport) so iOS Safari's retractable URL bar doesn't leave a dead strip.
  • body becomes position: fixed; inset: 0; overflow: hidden; overscroll-behavior: none; touch-action: manipulation — blocks the bounce-scroll.
  • Safe-area insets respected via env(safe-area-inset-*) so the iPhone notch / home indicator don't eat controls.
  • Global touchmove handler calls preventDefault() unless the target is inside a scrollable element (shop lists / inventory modals etc.) — stops rubber-banding without breaking menus.
  • gesturestart blocked to suppress iOS pinch-zoom.

Aspect-ratio fit

  • New _fitGameToViewport() runs on load, resize, and orientation change. Computes scale = min(availW / 960, availH / 560) and writes it to --game-scale.
  • .game-wrapper uses transform: scale(var(--game-scale, 1)) with transform-origin: center — every absolutely-positioned child (mobile controls, minimap, tower HUD, modals) scales with the wrapper so hit-testing stays pixel-accurate.
  • Border / radius / shadow removed on coarse-pointer or small screens — edge-to-edge immersive look on phones.

Rotate-to-landscape nag

  • On touch devices in portrait orientation < 768 px wide, a fullscreen overlay prompts the user to rotate with an animated 📱 icon.
  • Dismiss button ("Play in portrait anyway") sets body.dataset.nagDismissed = '1' so it doesn't flicker back on orientation changes.
  • Overlay auto-hides the moment the device goes landscape.

v0.14.3 Skill rework · shadow clones · 9-reset

Warrior Power Strike now sweeps 3 vertical lanes, every rogue skill hits 2–6 lines, Mirror Shadow summons three black silhouette clones that attack for 4 s, and 9 is a global reset shortcut.

High / mid / low sweep

QoL

Warrior — Power Strike (S) 3-lane cleave

  • Was a 2-hit combo. Now a 3-strike vertical sweep — high (-36 px), mid (0), low (+28). Each strike has ±28 px extended vertical reach so airborne and grounded foes both get hit.
  • Damage curve 1.5× / 1.8× / 2.2× ATK — the low finisher stuns 0.5 s.
  • New performMelee options tall and yShift let future skills extend their hitbox vertically or shift it up/down without rewriting the helper.
  • Slash crescent paints at each lane's height so the animation reads as three distinct swipes.

Rogue — every skill hits 2–6 lines

  • Backstab (S) — blink + 3-stab combo: quick / quick / heavy crit finisher. No target → fallback triple-thrust across high / mid / low lanes.
  • Throw Dagger (A) — 3-dagger fan became 5 daggers stacked on 5 vertical lanes (caps at 6 with multishot bonuses). 30° downward base so they stream like a waterfall.
  • Smoke Dash (E) — dash corridor widened from ±20 px to ±60 px vertical, hitting 3 effective lines. Mid-lane hits get +0.5× damage. Still drops the 3-tick smoke cloud.
  • Flurry (W) — already 6 strikes in the V-pattern; description updated to reflect.

✦Mirror Shadow (Shadowlord master)

Complete rewrite. Instead of a single clone that mimics your moves, you now summon three black silhouette clones that act autonomously for 4 seconds.

  • Each clone spawns at a triangle point around the player (fan angles ±2.2 rad), bobs with a sinusoidal orbit, and auto-targets the nearest enemy within 240 px.
  • Each swings every 400 ms (staggered phase offsets so you hear rapid-fire strikes), dealing ~140% ATK + 6 per hit with rollable crits.
  • Up to 3 enemies hit per swing per clone — ceiling at 9 hits per 400 ms cycle, theoretical ~70 hits over 4 seconds.
  • Visuals: pure-black #0a0010 chibi silhouette with a violet outline and purple under-glow that breathes with each swing. Violet bar eyes. Drops a purple-and-black crescent slash on each strike.
  • New drawShadowClones() renders them behind the player in the main pass. Fades over the last 400 ms of life.
  • Old single-clone mimic system retired — the action-queue code path at cast is now a no-op; clones don't copy skills, they just attack relentlessly.
  • Cast burst: 48-particle violet ring + 3 dark spawn puffs + crit sfx + 60 ms hit-stop.

Press 9 → reset save

  • Global hotkey 9 fires resetSave() — same double-confirm browser prompt as the Amnesiac's final stage.
  • Doesn't fire while paused (can't accidentally reset during a modal).
  • Added to the help panel and Skills Reference modal.
  • Existing Amnesiac dialog flow still works — the key is just a faster escape hatch for dev/testing.

v0.14.4 Potion CD fix · mobile deck

Fixes a 50-second potion cooldown that should have been 3 seconds, and extends the mobile controls beyond the game canvas so the D-pad / skills never cover gameplay.

Potion cooldown — real 3 seconds

  • Bug: POTION_CD_MS = 3000 was being added to game.time, which counts frames (+1 per frame at 60 fps), not milliseconds. Effective cooldown was ~50 s.
  • Fix: renamed to POTION_CD_FRAMES = 180 (= 3 s × 60 fps). Cooldown toast now divides by 60 (frames → seconds) instead of 1000.
  • Affects both HP (PgUp) and MP (PgDn) — each tracks its own CD so they don't compete.

✦Mobile control deck — outside the game

The D-pad and action buttons are now in a dedicated deck element rendered outside .game-wrapper, so they no longer overlap the canvas. The tiny HP/MP/menu cluster stays inside the game area as a compact top-right overlay.

  • Portrait orientation: body uses flex-direction: column — game canvas stretches across the top of the screen, control deck sits below it in its own bar.
  • Landscape orientation: body switches to flex-direction: row — canvas on the left (as large as height allows), vertical 260 px control strip on the right. D-pad above, actions below.
  • Canvas fills more of the screen: _fitGameToViewport now measures the deck's live width/height and subtracts it from the available viewport before scaling. The wrapper's transform-origin moved from center center to center top so the upward-growing wrapper snaps to the top of its flex cell.
  • Slight stretch: touch devices get an extra 4% scale bump on top of the aspect-preserving minimum, capped so it never overflows the available box.
  • Re-fit fires 4 times on orientation change (0 / 120 / 350 / 800 ms) to catch Android's delayed layout settle.
  • The control deck has its own touchmove preventDefault so swipes on the deck don't rubber-band the page.
  • hide-mobile-ctrl body class now hides the deck too, for hybrid laptops that prefer the keyboard.

v0.15.0 Crusader rework · perf pass · GBA controller

✦Crusader — Divine Aegis rework

Was: Heal 60% + short damage barrier. Now: heal + 5 hovering holy orbs that pendulum around the player, striking enemies they pass through. While active, the player takes half damage from all sources (melee contact AND enemy projectiles) for 8 seconds.

  • Orbs arranged at 5 fan angles, pendulum radius 30–110 px via sinusoidal phase, rotate around the player at ~60°/sec.
  • Each orb checks for monsters within 22 px, deals ~110% ATK + 6 with a 350 ms per-orb cooldown — prevents chain-stun but lets them reliably strike in combat.
  • Damage reduction hook added at both melee-contact and projectile-hit sites (if (player._aegis) dmg = Math.max(1, Math.floor(dmg * 0.5))).
  • New drawAegisOrbs() renders with additive blend — outer amber halo, warm yellow core, white-hot center, fades in last 600 ms.
  • Ambient sparkle trail per orb; consecration cast burst still fires on activation.

✦Performance pass

  • updateUI DOM cache — new _uiGetRefs caches every getElementById on first call; _uiSetText / _uiSetStyle write only when the value actually changes. Cuts ~19 lookups/frame to 0, eliminates redundant style writes that triggered repaints.
  • renderSkillBar rebuilt once — was bar.innerHTML = '' + 9 createElement per frame. Now _sbBuild() runs once per class/job/master change, _sbSlots[] caches the DOM refs, renderSkillBar() patches icon/MP/CD/ready state in place with per-slot dirty flags. Major churn removal.
  • Projectile frustum cull — drawProjectiles early-outs on projectiles outside the viewport (+60 px buffer). Saves draws during heavy arrow/rain skills.
  • Sky gradient cached — createLinearGradient was rebuilt every frame in drawBackground. Now cached via _skyGradCache with a colour-key invalidation; only rebuilds when the map's sky changes.
  • Dead code purged — 734 lines of unreachable legacy renderers removed:
    • 440 lines from drawTownDecor (old medieval town art, after return;).
    • 294 lines from drawPlayer (elaborate procedural character kept "for reference" behind if (false) { ... }).
  • File shrunk from ~19,150 → ~18,615 lines. Expected lag reduction on lower-end devices: ~30–40% on combat-heavy frames.

🕹GBA-style mobile controller

The flat-rectangle button deck becomes a proper plastic handheld. Purple/indigo shell with inset shadows, glossy button highlights, a power-LED indicator, and a "LEVELX" brand plate.

  • D-pad — single chunky cross (4 buttons inside a circular recessed plate), not 4 separate pills. Glossy purple plastic, rounded corner-matched directional badges.
  • Face buttons — 3×3 diamond: 
    [W] [Jump]  [C]
[A] [Basic] [S]
[X] [E]     [Q]
    Basic attack is the red "A button" at the center (54 px circle, red gradient). Jump is the orange "B button" at the top. 7 skill slots ring around them in purple circles.
  • Shoulder pills — Block (🛡, blue) and Dodge (💨, green) are long pill-shaped buttons floating at the top-left / top-right corners of the deck, like L/R bumpers.
  • Power LED — small red pulsing dot between the D-pad and the buttons, animating 2 s ease-in-out.
  • Brand plate — "LEVELX" etched in light purple between the controls.
  • Every button has inset highlight + drop shadow + active press-scale (0.9) for tactile feedback.
  • Landscape: deck switches to a vertical strip on the right (280 px wide) — D-pad above, face buttons below, shoulders on top row.

v0.15.1 Mobile controller fix

GBA controller now spreads properly in portrait and actually shows up in landscape — the previous build's nested media query and sizing-overflow issues hid the controls when the phone rotated.

Portrait — wider spread

  • Deck switches from a cramped 3-column grid to a flex-direction: row with justify-content: space-between — D-pad hugs the left edge, face buttons hug the right, lots of breathing room in between.
  • D-pad bumped 150 px → 170 px; directional buttons 42 px → 48 px; gap between directional buttons widened.
  • Face button cluster bumped 152 px → 172 px with 8 px gaps between buttons (was 4 px). Individual buttons 48 px → 52 px.
  • Basic attack at center of diamond grew to 60 px — the classic "A button" now properly dominates.
  • Shoulder pills repositioned with env(safe-area-inset-left / right) so they respect iPhone notch / home indicator area.
  • LEVELX brand plate + power LED moved to the top-centre of the deck (used to be a grid cell; now absolutely positioned so it doesn't fight for flex space).
  • Deck top-padding bumped 10 px → 50 px to make room for the shoulder pills + brand plate.

Landscape — controller actually appears now

  • Bug: the old CSS nested @media (orientation: landscape) inside an @media (pointer: coarse), (max-width: 900px) block. Older Safari/Chrome interpreted the nesting inconsistently, and the grid grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr fit a 150 px D-pad into a 140 px column (2×140 = 280). Result: controls overflowed off-screen or were hidden.
  • Fix: landscape styles no longer nest. They sit under two flat media queries ((pointer: coarse) and (orientation: landscape), and (max-width: 900px) and (orientation: landscape)) that toggle a body.mc-landscape class via JS — then the landscape rules apply off that class alone, immune to browser media-query edge cases.
  • JS in _fitGameToViewport computes isTouchOrNarrow + isLandscape every re-fit and toggles the class accordingly, so it's always in sync with the actual viewport even when CSS media queries flicker during orientation changes.
  • Landscape deck is a 220 px vertical strip on the right — shoulders top-corners, D-pad (150 px) mid, face cluster (152 px) bottom, LEVELX brand between them.
  • Buttons shrink to 42 / 48 px for vertical fit on ≤ 400 px tall landscape viewports.

v0.15.2 Landscape fix · button spacing · no shoulders

Root-cause fix for the missing landscape controls: the deck is now position: fixed on the right edge so the game-wrapper's 960 px authored layout width can't push it off-screen. Portrait buttons get much more breathing room. Shoulder pills removed.

Landscape — deck is now position:fixed

  • Root cause: the wrapper was authored at 960 × 560 px and only visually scaled via transform: scale(). Transforms don't shrink an element's layout box — so in landscape, flex-row body put a 960 px wrapper next to the 220 px deck, totalling 1180 px of layout. On a 844 px wide iPhone the deck ended up painted off-screen.
  • Fix: in landscape the deck uses position: fixed; top:0; right:0; bottom:0; width:240px. It sits OUTSIDE body flex flow, guaranteeing it's visible. Body gets padding-right: 240px so the wrapper's 960 px layout doesn't slide under the deck — the transform then scales the visual down into the reserved space.
  • JS stops double-subtracting the deck width (the body padding already handles it). The game canvas scales to min((vw - 240) / 960, vh / 560).
  • Tested at 844 × 390 (iPhone 14 landscape) and 667 × 375 (iPhone SE landscape): deck is a visible 240 px strip on the right, game fills the rest.

Portrait — bigger cells, no overlap

  • Face button cluster grew from 172 × 172 px → 192 × 192 px with 56 × 56 cells and 12 px gaps (was 52 × 52 with 8 px gaps).
  • Basic-attack "A button" downsized 60 → 56 px so it fits cleanly in its center cell (the 60 px button was overlapping neighbours at the 8 px gap spec).
  • Skill buttons bumped 52 → 56 px to match — easier to hit.
  • Jump button bumped 52 → 56 px too, font 22 → 24 px.
  • D-pad stable at 168 px; directional buttons 46 px with bigger central gap.
  • Top padding reduced 50 → 32 px since the shoulder pills are gone — the brand plate / LED now sit at top-6 / top-22 for a tighter header.

Shoulder pills removed

  • Block (🛡) and Dodge (💨) pills hidden via display: none. They were cluttering the deck and overlapping skill buttons.
  • Block/parry still works on the keyboard A key for desktop players; mobile users use the A-slot skill (left face button) for active skills.
  • Dodge (Shift) was rarely needed on mobile — the roll wasn't comfortable to time with thumbs anyway.

Horoscope bosses get a proper badge system with earn-flourish + hub-wall display, every zodiac arena gets a signature backdrop matching its theme, and the mobile controller splits across both screen edges in landscape.

v0.16.1 Translucent overlay controls + fullscreen game

Mobile controls become translucent-white frosted-glass overlays that float over the game. Canvas fills the whole viewport — no reserved deck. Portrait gets D-pad positioned above the face buttons for better thumb ergonomics; PgUp / PgDn potion buttons already render in the top-right stack.

Translucent white button styling

  • Every .mc-btn now uses a frosted-glass look: background: rgba(255,255,255,0.22), 2 px white-tinted border at 55% alpha, backdrop-filter: blur(10px), soft inset highlight, white text with 3 px shadow.
  • On press: background jumps to 42% white with inner-shadow for a tactile feel. No plastic colour — buttons let the game show through.
  • Accent-coloured buttons keep their tint but also become translucent: Basic attack (red) at 32% alpha, Jump (amber) at 32%, HP potion (pink), MP potion (blue). Skill circles stay neutral white.

Game canvas fills the whole viewport

  • Deck is now position: fixed; inset: 0; pointer-events: none — a transparent overlay that doesn't reserve any layout space.
  • _fitGameToViewport no longer subtracts deck height/width — scale = min(vw / 960, vh / 560) uses the full viewport.
  • Body landscape padding dropped (was 200 px on each side). Game wrapper centers in full viewport and scales uniformly.
  • Result: game view is noticeably bigger on phones since the D-pad + buttons no longer eat a bottom strip or side column.

Portrait — D-pad above face buttons

  • D-pad pinned to bottom-left but raised 240 px from the bottom edge — sits on the left side of the screen well above the lower-thumb zone.
  • Face buttons pinned to bottom-right, 20 px from the edge — the classic right-thumb rest position.
  • D-pad is now physically above the face buttons on screen, matching the ergonomic ask.
  • Potions + menu icons stacked vertically in the top-right corner (56 px down from the top to clear the HUD).

Landscape — unchanged split with translucent styling

  • D-pad bottom-left, face buttons bottom-right — both at 18 px from their edges.
  • Potions + menu stacked horizontally in the top-right.

PgUp / PgDn potion buttons

Already in the HTML as data-mkey="pageup" / data-mkey="pagedown". Now styled to stand out: pink HP button (♥), blue MP button (◆), both 50 px circles in the portrait top-right stack (or landscape top-right row). Tapping dispatches the PgUp / PgDn keyboard event which fires useQuickPotion() (same auto-buy fallback the keyboard binding uses).

Narrow-phone fallback

Screens < 380 px wide shrink the D-pad to 150 px, directional buttons to 44 px, face buttons to 50 px, potions to 44 px. Ensures every button fits comfortably on small phones.

v0.16.2 Max-screen landscape · portrait polish

Mobile landscape now stretches the game to fill every pixel of the viewport (slight aspect distortion accepted for maximum screen use). Portrait controls repositioned + sized for natural thumb travel.

Mobile landscape — stretch to fill

  • _fitGameToViewport now emits independent X / Y scales (--game-scale-x, --game-scale-y) in mobile landscape.
  • CSS reads both: transform: scale(var(--game-scale-x), var(--game-scale-y)) — lets the game-wrapper stretch non-uniformly to fill the full viewport.
  • Desktop + portrait keep uniform scaling (aspect-preserving).
  • Example: 844 × 390 iPhone landscape — was scale 0.696 (668 × 390 visual, 176 px of unused bars). Now scale x=0.88, y=0.70 → fills the full 844 × 390 with ~4% horizontal stretch. Characters remain recognisable, every pixel counts.
  • transform-origin: top left in mc-landscape so the stretched wrapper anchors to the viewport corner and doesn't drift off-canvas.

Portrait control polish

  • Diagonal thumb-rest layout: D-pad raised on the left (bottom 40 px), face buttons tucked in the bottom-right (bottom 16 px). Vertical offset avoids overlap on narrow phones.
  • Button sizes optimised — oversized buttons felt nice in theory but ate screen. Now:
    • D-pad 168 → 156 px, directional buttons 58 → 46 px
    • Face cluster 216 → 184 px, skills / jump 62 → 54 px
    • Basic-attack "A button" centres at 58 px so it still pops
    • Potions / menu 50 → 44 px
  • Potions + menu icons sit in a horizontal row at the top-right corner (was vertical stack) — thumb tilts up to reach them but they take less vertical real estate.
  • Result: controls visibly smaller but more game canvas visible, and all buttons remain comfortably tappable.

v0.16.3 Landscape un-stretch · perf pass

Reverts the squashed landscape aspect ratio and takes a heavy perf pass — removes the biggest mobile-lag source (backdrop-filter blur), caches zodiac-arena gradients, precomputes Sagittarius starfield, and trims aggressive particle spawn rates.

Landscape — aspect ratio fixed

  • Bug: v0.16.2's non-uniform X/Y scaling stretched the game wider than authored. Characters looked squashed / elongated depending on phone aspect.
  • Fix: reverted to uniform min(sx, sy) scaling. Phones with wider aspect than 1.71:1 get small letterbox bars, but the game's proportions stay correct. Mobile still gets a subtle 4% size bonus (capped so it never overflows).
  • Transform origin reset to center center in landscape so the wrapper stays centred.
  • Same --game-scale-x / --game-scale-y CSS vars remain wired in case we return to non-uniform later, but both always receive the same value now.

⚡Mobile perf pass

  • Killed backdrop-filter: blur(10px) on the touch buttons. This was the single biggest mobile lag source — every frame the browser re-blurred the underlying canvas for every visible button (~15 buttons × 60 fps = 900 blur composites/sec). Replaced with a simple rgba(40,30,60,0.55) translucent background + stronger border + drop shadow. Looks almost identical, costs essentially nothing.
  • Cached zodiac-arena gradients. ZODIAC_SIGNATURE_DECOR functions were calling createRadialGradient / createLinearGradient every single frame. New _zGrad(key, factory) cache populated on first use — Aries sun, Cancer moon halo, Scorpio red mist, Pisces abyssal gradient, and the arena vignette all now build their gradient ONCE and reuse it. Zero recurring cost across the rest of the fight.
  • Sagittarius starfield precomputed. Was 120 stars × 2 Math.sin/cos calls per frame = 240 trig ops/frame. Now positions are precomputed into a static array on first call; frame loop only touches the twinkle phase. Also dropped star count 120 → 90.
  • Particle spawn rates tamed:
    • Capricorn blizzard: every 2 frames (30/s) → every 5 frames (12/s).
    • Taurus dust: every 3 frames (20/s) → every 8 frames (8/s).
    • Capricorn life cut 200 → 140 frames so particles turn over faster.

Net effect: frame time during zodiac fights should drop significantly on mobile, especially on signs with moonlit halos / red mist / starfields (Cancer, Scorpio, Sagittarius, Pisces, Aries).

v0.17.0 Village · Bloodlust · Zodiac portal · cute floor

Zodiac portal above the Amnesiac

🩸Berserker — Bloodlust rework

Was a brief 6 s lifesteal + speed buff. Now a proper ultimate.

Town — humble village cottages

Old 6-storey high-rise town replaced with a proper storybook village. Each NPC now lives in a thatched cottage.

  • Half-timber beams — vertical posts at each edge, horizontal lintel, diagonal brace rendered as pixel-staircase for an authentic look.

  • Arched wooden door with 2-tone cel shading, plank lines, and a brass handle.

Cuter floor + cloud design

  • Ground dirt simplified from 3-band to 2-tone (honey-dirt top + deep-soil bottom) with a crisp black seam. Round pebbles replace flat dots — each pebble gets a drop shadow + body + highlight pixel for volume. Undersoil "roots" are now little curved squiggles via quadraticCurveTo rather than static vertical ticks.
  • Grass top gets a scalloped wavy edge — small arcs drawn atop the flat grass band for an uneven, natural lip. Two-tone deeper green band underneath.
  • Grass tufts doubled in density, drawn as 2-tone blades (bright lit + shadow side) instead of single pixels.
  • Chibi flowers every ~90 px — a 4-petal pink/yellow/purple plump flower with a yellow core AND a tiny cute face (2 eye dots) rendered on top. Matches the monster chibi vibe.
  • Clouds now have optional tiny faces on bright maps — little black dot eyes, pink blush cheeks, and a subtle smile arc. About half the clouds get faces (every even-sized cloud) to avoid feeling busy.

v0.25.137 Vector hero — head shading polish, dramatic attack swing, outlines +1 px

User feedback: "improve the shading of the head, improve the attacking vectors especially the weapon, outline increase by 1px."

Head shading

  • Light band enlarged from rx=10,ry=7 → rx=11,ry=8 (wider lit wash on upper-left).
  • New rim crescent — thin shifted-self bright disc clipped to head, paints a translucent white band along the upper-left edge for the "light source from above-left" cue.
  • Primary gloss pip nudged up to rx=4.8,ry=3.6.
  • New secondary catchlight at (-4, -7) — small bright pip near the eye area (anime "double catchlight" tradition).
  • New cheek blush — two soft pink ellipses (rgba(255,140,150,0.28)) on each cheek, clipped to head so they don't bleed past the silhouette.

Attack vectors

  • Right-arm swing range bumped from -1.2 → -0.5 rad to -1.5 → +0.5 rad (a full ~115° arc with proper windup-to-followthrough).
  • Swing curve uses (1 - cos(tπ)) × 1.0 for ease-out feel (slow windup, fast contact, slow follow-through).
  • Spine + head twist amplitudes increased: spine 0.12 → 0.18, head 0.10 → 0.14. Whole body sells the swing.
  • New handR mesh deform on attack — weapon scales up by ~18% at swing peak for "weighty contact".
  • New slash arc trail — translucent white arc swept from the windup angle to the current swing angle, drawn before the weapon. Bright leading-edge inner pass sells the motion direction.

Outlines +1 px

  • Main body STROKE_W: 1 → 2.
  • Eye outline 0.5 → 1.5. Mouth 0.6 → 1.6.
  • Weapon strokes: every 0.5 → 1.5; bow outer rim 2 → 3, bow inner wood rim 0.5 → 1.5.
  • Restores some of the v0.25.135 reduction — outline now reads halfway between the v0.25.134 thick (3 px) and v0.25.135 thin (1 px) versions.

v0.25.136 Platform sync fix — new v2 sprites with no transparent padding

User feedback: "there is a gap between the platform and the character/monster, make it sync, and generate better platform sprites with ludo.ai and implement." Re-generated all 5 themed platform tiles (grass / stone / ice / lava / sand) with explicit "fills the full frame edge-to-edge, no transparent padding" prompt, and switched the bake mode for every platform from grid:1x2 / various to auto — which v0.25.127's both-axes opaque-bound crop strips any residual padding rows automatically.

Root cause of the gap

  • Old floor_wood_v3.webp source had the top plank starting ~6 px below the canvas top (transparent painterly halo above the wood).
  • grid:1x2 bake cropped exactly the top half of the canvas, preserving those transparent padding rows.
  • When scaled to platform h=12, the padding rows squished into "phantom space" above the visible plank → character feet (collision at p.y) appeared 4–6 px above the painted plank top.

Fix

  • 5 new platform sprites in backgrounds/tiles/: platform_grass_v2.webp, platform_stone_v2.webp, platform_ice_v2.webp, platform_lava_v2.webp, platform_sand_v2.webp. Each prompted with "SINGLE horizontal slab that COMPLETELY FILLS THE FRAME edge-to-edge from top to bottom, NO transparent padding above or below" so the baked tile's top edge IS the visible slab top.
  • Every platform bake mode is now auto. _lxBakeSeamlessTile('auto') already crops both horizontal AND vertical opaque bounds (added in v0.25.127), so any tiny residual padding gets stripped.
  • Result: character + monster feet at p.y now sit ON the platform's painted top edge instead of floating 4–6 px above.

v0.25.135 Vector hero — Ivory tone, 0.9× scale, default mode, weapons, eye-tracking, thinner outlines

Stacked user feedback in one ship: "include lighter skin shade, make shading over the head bottom right, and add a light shade add top left, make character slightly smaller (90% of current size), default use drawvectorhero rather than draw cuter hero", "make a layer for weapons based on class", "make character eyes move towards the direction of movement", "for the maincharacter vectors, reduce all outlines by 2 px".

Lighter skin tone

  • New Ivory entry prepended to HERO_VEC_SKIN: light=#fffaf2 / base=#fdf0db / mid=#f1d8bc / deep=#cfae8c — lighter than Porcelain.
  • Existing skinIdx values shift by +1; CHAR_STUDIO.skinIdx default bumped 1 → 2 so new players still default to "Light". Existing saves with skinIdx=1 read as Porcelain (close enough; can re-pick).

Enhanced head shading

  • Bottom-right cel offset bumped 6 → 7 px on the head so the lower-right shadow crescent reads more clearly.
  • Upper-left lit band enlarged from rx=7,ry=5 to rx=10,ry=7 — proper "light from above-left" wash.
  • Glossy white pip moved to (-10, -11) with alpha=0.92 so the shiniest spot sits on top of the lit band.

0.9× size scale

  • Vector hero now renders at 90% of the previous size. Implemented as ctx.scale(0.9, 0.9) right after the world-space anchor + facing-flip, so the rig's rest-pose offsets all shrink uniformly.

Default switched to vector

  • _CHAR_STYLE default flipped from 'sprite' to 'vector'. Players who haven't set a preference now see the vector hero by default.
  • Final fallback in drawPlayer (when neither vector flag nor lookCustom nor HERO sprite is active) now goes to _drawVectorHero instead of drawCuteCharacter — consistent look at every state.
  • Power users can still force ?charstyle=sprite URL flag for the legacy HERO sprite path.

Per-class weapon layer (HERO_VEC_WEAPON)

  • New handR bone (child of armR at offset (0, 10)) anchors the weapon at the front-hand. The weapon naturally inherits the arm's animation rotation + the head/spine bob.
  • Warrior — silver sword with gold crossguard, dark grip, gold pommel; cel shadow on the right edge of the blade + bright highlight on the left.
  • Rogue — short silver dagger with dark leather wrap on the grip.
  • Mage — tall wooden staff with a glowing cyan magic orb on top + radial halo glow.
  • Archer — curved wooden bow with bowstring + leather grip wrap.
  • Default class (no class picked) renders no weapon — clean naked-mannequin silhouette.

Eye tracking

  • Pupil-highlight pip in _drawEye now shifts horizontally based on player movement: +0.7 px when moving forward, -0.7 px when moving backward, mirrored under facing flip. Falls back to a slight +0.6 "looking forward" offset during attack windup.
  • Reads off player.vx + player.attacking; idle eyes stay centred.

Outlines −2 px

  • Main body STROKE_W: 3 → 1.
  • Eye outline: 1 → 0.5. Mouth: 1.6 → 0.6.
  • Weapon outlines: each reduced by 2 px with a 0.5 px floor.
  • Result: a much lighter painterly look — less "thick black sticker" feel, more soft chibi.

v0.25.134 Vector studio (Q) — skin tones + hair picker + 3-tone shading; sprite system removed

User feedback: "make the option to choose skin tone, improve to include 1 more shade, make torso smaller, make ability to choose between different hair options, delete the sprites in the Q UI and replace with this." Wholesale rebuild of the Q-key Character Studio so it drives the vector hero.

Skin tone presets (HERO_VEC_SKIN)

  • 7 tones: Porcelain, Light, Tan, Olive, Bronze, Brown, Deep.
  • Each tone carries 4 levels — light (highlight pip + lit band on the head), base (lit fill), mid (first cel crescent), deep (second deeper cel crescent for the new 3-tone pass).
  • Studio swatches show the base hex; clicking sets CHAR_STUDIO.skinIdx live.

3-tone cel-shading (the user's requested "1 more shade")

  • _drawShaded(path, base, mid, deep, dx, dy) now does TWO shifted-self-clip passes. Pass 1 paints mid in the lower-right crescent. Pass 2 clips again to that crescent, translates further, paints deep. Result: 3 bands with crisp hard-edged boundaries.
  • Head also paints an upper-left SKIN.light band for a 4-tone read overall.

Hair picker (HERO_VEC_HAIR)

  • renderCharStudio calls _drawVectorHero on the studio canvas with explicit _ctx + opts override. Re-renders every requestAnimationFrame tick so the idle bob animates live in the preview.
  • applyCharStudioToPlayer writes player.lookCustom = {skinIdx, hairId} + saveState(). revertCharStudioFromPlayer clears it.
  • drawPlayer routes through _drawVectorHero when player.lookCustom is set (in addition to the existing ?charstyle=vector URL flag).
  • lookCustom added to PLAYER_SAVE_FIELDS so the picks persist across reloads.

Renderer refactor

  • _drawVectorHero(sx, sy, _ctx, opts) now accepts an optional target canvas + opts override (cls, lookCustom, animName, animTime). Internally aliases _ctx || _MAIN_CTX to local ctx so the rest of the function reads naturally without TDZ. _MAIN_CTX added at the top of the script as a stable alias to the main-canvas 2D context.

v0.25.133 Vector hero — unified silhouette + cel-shading + long anime eyes + animated head bob

User feedback: "Make vector for all the classes the same, improve cell shading, make eyes long vertical cute, make torso small, head big, make head bob when move or attack."

Unified silhouette

  • Removed the per-class hat field. No more warrior helmet / rogue hood / mage pointy / archer feather. Every class now shares the chibi anime hairstyle (the v0.25.131 silhouette).
  • Class identity reads off the body palette only: warrior red, rogue indigo, mage blue, archer green, default peach.

Resized rig (smaller torso, bigger head)

  • Head: r=18 → r=20.
  • Torso: ~30 px tall → ~16 px tall; tighter pear with waist pulled in.
  • Arms / legs: ~14 / ~12 tall → ~10 each; stubbier blobs.
  • Head:body ratio closer to a true 1:1 chibi look.

Cel-shading via shifted-self-clip

  • Replaced soft offset-ellipse shadow with proper hand-drawn cel look: fill base → clip to part → translate (dx, dy) → fill SAME PATH in shadow tone. The intersection is the lower-right crescent of the part — crisp hard-edged boundary between lit and shaded regions.
  • Head + torso: 5–6 px shadow offset. Arms + legs: 3 px. Hair: 3 px own pass.

Long vertical anime eyes

  • Dot eyes (1.8 px circle) → tall ovals (rx=2.4, ry=5.2). Solid black with white highlight pip on the upper portion.
  • Universal across all classes (default mannequin now has eyes too).

Animated head bob (new HERO_VEC_BOB table)

  • Per-bone position offsets layered into applyChain() after the rest-pose translate, before rotation.
  • idle — subtle 0.6 px breathing.
  • walk — -|sin(t×2π)|×3 + 1.5: head bobs UP twice per cycle (once per step), visible weight transfer.
  • jump — static -2 px (head leans up during airborne pose).
  • attack — -sin(t×π)×4: head dips down on windup then snaps back.

v0.25.132 Vector hero — chibi mannequin proportions + 3-tone shading + glossy highlight

User shipped a chibi mannequin reference (giant round head, blob torso, stubby teardrop limbs, soft 2-tone peach skin, thick black outline, white glossy highlight on the upper-left of the head) and asked the vector hero to match. Wholesale rebuild of HERO_VEC_PARTS + HERO_VEC_RIG + the renderer's shading model.

New parts (Path2D)

  • head — circle r=18 (was 14) for the big chibi dome
  • torso — pear shape via Q-curves: tapered shoulders at y=-22, widest at the hip line at y=4, rounded bottom at y=8
  • arm — stubby teardrop blob, pivot at top (shoulder), rounded hand at y=14
  • leg — stubby teardrop blob, pivot at top (hip), rounded foot at y=12

Rig anchors (chibi proportions, total height ~70 px)

  • root at feet centre (0, 0)
  • legL/legR at (±5, −12) — hip pivot
  • spine at (0, −12) — torso pivots at hip line
  • armL/armR at (±9, −18) — shoulder pivot
  • head at (−2, −38) — large head sits high; slight x offset for the reference's subtle head tilt

3-tone shading + glossy highlight

  • New _drawShaded(path, base, shadow, dx, dy, sx, sy) helper: fills base → clips to the part → paints shadow as an offset ellipse (lower-right) → strokes outline.
  • New _drawGloss(cx, cy, rx, ry, alpha): soft semi-transparent white ellipse for the glossy chibi reflection. Head gets a prominent pip at (−7, −8); torso/arms/legs get smaller subtler pips.
  • Outline thickness bumped 1.5 px → 3 px to match the bold reference linework. lineJoin/lineCap = round for smooth corners.

Per-class palette additions

  • Default class is now a faceless naked mannequin — body = boot = skin tone, no clothing accent, no eyes/mouth. Identical to the reference frame.
  • Clothed classes (warrior/rogue/mage/archer) keep their bold body colour + accent belt + simple chibi face (eye dots + smile).

New HERO_VEC_PARTS.hair path

v0.25.130 Vector hero renderer — SVG paths + skeletal animation + mesh deformation

User feedback: "improve on Vector Art and SVG, Skeletal Animation and Mesh Deformation." New opt-in renderer draws the hero from Path2D SVG primitives over a parented bone tree, with per-bone rotation curves and scale-based mesh squash/stretch. Default stays the HERO sprite-sheet renderer so existing builds keep their painterly hero artwork — toggle via ?charstyle=vector URL flag or localStorage.setItem('mojiworld_charstyle', 'vector').

Skeletal rig

BoneRest pose (rel. to parent)Parent
root(0, 0)—
spine(0, −26)root
head(0, −32)spine
armL (back)(−9, −22)spine
armR (front)(9, −22)spine
legL (back)(−5, −2)root
legR (front)(5, −2)root

Each bone draws by walking its parent chain root → … → bone, applying every translate → rotate → scale in order. Children naturally inherit parent transforms via ctx.save/restore — no explicit matrix math.

Vector body parts (Path2D from SVG path strings)

  • head — circle, 28 px diameter
  • torso — trapezoidal Q-curve quad with subtle waist taper
  • arm, leg — rounded-bottom rectangles
  • hair — jagged-edge triangle row above the head

Animations

  • idle — spine + head sway at sin(t×2π)×0.012, no limb motion
  • walk — opposing arm/leg swings at ±0.45/0.55 rad, 4× spine bob
  • jump — static "tucked" pose (arms back, legs split) with arched spine
  • attack — one-shot 22-frame swing (right arm sweep −1.2 → 0 rad)

Mesh deformation

  • idle — spine breathes via inverse sx/sy oscillation (compress horizontally as it stretches vertically — classic squash-and-stretch)
  • walk — spine stretches at impact frames (sy = 1 + sin(t×4π)×0.04)
  • jump — static body stretch (sx 0.94, sy 1.08)
  • attack — right-arm extends by 18% in y as it swings; spine snaps to (1.05, 0.98) for the recoil

Class-specific silhouettes

  • Warrior — red body, gold helmet dome on head
  • Rogue — indigo body, dark hood draping over the skin circle
  • Mage — blue body, pointy purple hat with gold star
  • Archer — green body, brown hair + gold feather sticking out the side

Wiring

  • drawPlayer() branches: _CHAR_STYLE === 'vector' → _drawVectorHero(); else the existing HERO sprite path. Block-bubble + nameplate + class-identity HUD all still draw on top.
  • Anchor: feet centred at (sx + player.w/2, sy + player.h). Facing flips via ctx.scale(-1, 1).
  • The face-overlay pass (_drawCuteFaceOverlay) is suppressed in vector mode — the head bone draws its own eyes + mouth.

v0.25.127 Fix character + monsters appearing to float above the ground

User feedback: "the height of the floor is not correct, my character and the monsters appear to have some distance off the ground." Root cause: the ludo-generated grass+dirt source image carried 30-50% transparent padding above and below the actual grass+dirt strip. The auto-bake only cropped the LEFT/RIGHT opaque bounds, not top/bottom — so when scaled to platform height, the empty padding rows squashed into "phantom ground" above and below the visible art. Result: the player's foot line (which collides correctly with p.y) appeared 15–25 px above the visible grass surface.

Fix

  • Extended _lxBakeSeamlessTile() 'auto' mode to also detect the vertical opaque-bounds (yTop → yBot) and crop the source on both axes.
  • Baked tile is now exactly the rectangle of visible grass+dirt content. When drawn into the p.h + grassLift destination region, the top row of the image lines up with p.y - grassLift (i.e. just above the platform's logical foot line, where small grass tufts are supposed to protrude) instead of with empty padding.
  • Net visual change: character + monster sprites now actually stand on the grass instead of floating 15–25 px above it.

v0.25.126 Items / equipment UI mirrored under the U tab

User feedback: "Could you make the item / equipment UI under the U tab as well." Added a 4th tab 🎒 Items to the Character panel (U) alongside Level Up / Boon Loadout / Skills. Same equipment slots row, same inv-tabs (Equip / Use / Etc / Set-Up / Cash), same grid — renders in-place inside the U modal so players can manage gear without bouncing between modals. The standalone B-key inventory still works exactly as before.

Plumbing

  • renderInventory() now takes an optional prefix argument so it can target either DOM host. The B-key call uses the empty default; the U-tab call uses 'u-'.
  • Element lookups (inv-grid, inv-tab-info, inv-tabs, eq-weapon, eq-armor, eq-accessory, consumables) all prepend the prefix.
  • Class-based selectors (.equip-slots, .inv-slot, .inv-tab) scoped to the correct host so the dim/active states don't leak between the two copies.
  • Tab-button onclick + slot onclicks recurse with the same prefix so re-renders stay in the right pane.

v0.25.125 Archer bow overlay — bow now visible across all states, no longer pops in/out

User feedback: "archer sprites does not seem to be synced, please ensure the drawing of the bow is consistent." Root cause: the generic HERO sheets (idle / walk / jump / hit / death / attack) draw the teen with no weapon — only the class-specific teen_archer_shot.webp has a bow rendered into its 4 frames. Result: the archer carried nothing visible during 95% of gameplay, and the bow pop-flashed into existence only during the half-second basic-attack animation.

Fix

  • New procedural bow overlay drawn at the end of _drawPlayerCustomSprite() when player.cls === 'archer' and the active hero animation is not the archer-shot sheet.
  • Reuses the existing _drawCuteBow(P, f, false) renderer (idle hold pose, no nocked arrow) and _weaponPalette() for rarity-aware coloring — equipped bow visuals propagate correctly.
  • Bow positioned at the right-hand grip (~18% width offset, ~50% height up from feet, scaled 0.7×, tilted -0.35 rad). A subtle sin(time * 0.18) * 0.6 bob keeps it sympathetic to walk/idle motion.
  • Detection: hoisted the existing block-scoped frames variable to a new _heroActiveFrames outer let so the bow overlay can compare against HERO.classFrames.archer without re-deriving state. The archer-shot animation is the only state where the sheet already has a bow, so we skip the procedural overlay there to avoid drawing two bows.

States the bow is now visible in

  • Idle — bow held vertically at hip, string straight.
  • Walk / run — bow follows the body with a tiny sympathetic bob.
  • Jump / fall — bow stays in the right hand through the arc.
  • Hit / hit-stun — bow bobs with the recoil pose.
  • Death — bow stays in hand through the death frames.
  • Generic attack (non-archer-shot states, e.g. dash slash) — bow visible.
  • Archer-shot animation — overlay deliberately skipped; the sheet already has a bow drawn into the frames with proper draw-back/recoil.

v0.25.124 DOT tick cadence slowed (40 → 80 frames)

User feedback: "make DOT (damage over time) deal damage more slowly". Burn / poison ticks were every ~40 frames (~0.67 s @ 60 fps); a stack of three sources tagged on a tough mob produced a wall of red numbers every two-thirds of a second. Tick interval doubled to ~80 frames (~1.3 s) so the damage application visibly paces.

What changed

  • polishBurn-DoT tick interval 40 → 80 frames — the only change. Per-tick damage (m.burnDmg) is unchanged, so total burn damage over the duration roughly halves. Affects every DOT source: Grand Hex, fire / elemental arrows, poison-on-hit enhancements, etc.
  • polishDamage numbers spread out — the damage-number stream is half as dense; mob HP bars trickle down at a calmer pace. No change to mob behavior or stagger.

Files

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.124. Single literal change in updateMonsters (40 → 80) plus updated comment block. +5 / -2 lines.

v0.25.123 XP curve very steep from level 15 onwards

User feedback: "make the exp curve very steep starting from level 15 onwards". Repointed the per-level expToNext multiplier so the early game (L1 – L14) keeps its gentle ramp, then a hard wall starts at L15 and ratchets up further at L20 / L30 / L40.

Level bandOld multiplierNew multiplier
1 – 141.201.20 (unchanged)
15 – 191.201.40
20 – 291.201.45
30 – 391.241.50
40+1.281.55

Implication

  • polishL1 – L14 — same pacing as before. First class identity (L1) and the lead-in to first job advancement still arrive at a normal cadence.
  • polishL15+ — the per-level multiplier jumps from 1.20 to 1.40 at the boundary, so a player crossing into L15 sees the next bar take roughly 1.7× longer than the L14→L15 grind. Each subsequent band ratchets up. By L40+ each level needs ~×1.55 of the prior bar — a real wall instead of a slow walk.
  • polishJob / master advancement levels — L25 (job) and L50 (master) are unchanged thresholds; only the EXP cost to reach them shifts upward.

Files

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.123. Single curveMul ladder rewritten in levelUp(). +11 / -10 lines.

v0.25.122 Triple-jump perks no longer wiped on boon equip

User report: "triple jump perk seems to not be functioning". Tracked the bug to _applyEquippedBoons(): it resets every player.mods.* field to 0 before re-applying boon contributions, which wipes the archer class baseline (+1 extraJumps) and the Aerial Mastery tree node (+1 extraJumps). Both are non-boon sources, so the recompute can't see them. Effect: as soon as a player equipped or unequipped any boon, their triple-jump went silent.

Fix

  • bugRe-layer perk bonuses after the boon loop — the recompute now sums archer-class (+1) + Aerial Mastery (+1 if treeUnlocked.a_aerial) + boon contribution (max-of), capped at 3 air jumps so a fully-stacked archer with the tree node + a Triple Jump boon ends at quad jump rather than infinity.
  • polishPersists across re-equips — _applyEquippedBoons is the canonical recompute, so any future boon / perk that touches extraJumps goes through this single layering step.

Files

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.122. ~12-line block added at the end of _applyEquippedBoons just before the multishot cap. +12 / 0 lines.

v0.25.121 Hotkeys — Pg Up / Pg Dn heal 50% HP / MP, Codex moved 1 → Y

Two key-binding changes bundled.

  • featPg Up — heal 50% HP — instantly restores 50% of getMaxHp(). Free, no potion required, no gold deduction. Reads as a "rest" hotkey rather than a potion shortcut.
  • featPg Down — heal 50% MP — instantly restores 50% of getMaxMp(). Same convention as Pg Up.
  • polishR / T preserved — the legacy useQuickPotion('hp' | 'mp') path stays bound to R / T for inventory-based healing. Players who want to manage potion stacks can still do that; players who want a fast rest hit Pg Up / Pg Dn.
  • polishCodex of Shardfall: 1 → Y — the lore map now opens / closes with Y. Frees up the 1 number key for the dev 1+2+3 combo and consistency with future emote/menu numbers. In-modal help text updated.

Files

Cooldown nearly halved (32 → 18 s) so it's a rotation centerpiece rather than a once-per-fight burst. Slam coda fire-time and damage unchanged. Invuln window extended 1300 → 1900 ms to cover the longer chain.

v0.25.117 Archer Z basic locked to single-target (no pierce / explode / split)

v0.25.116 Master-tier ult rebalance — Sky Lance bigger, Grand Hex / Soul Vortex hit harder, Cascade cools faster

Bundled four user-requested ult tunings into one balance pass. Three of the four master-tier ultimates were under-performing on impact-per-cast; the fourth (Prismatic Cascade) was costed too heavily for its damage profile. Numbers chosen so each kit feels like an ultimate rather than a long-cooldown filler.

SkillMasterFieldOldNew

New skill kinds

v0.25.114 Faster boot — reveal gate trimmed from 16 sprites + HERO_READY to 4 critical sprites

User feedback: "make the loading faster". The old loader gated the reveal on 16 sprites + a HERO_READY event (which itself awaited a Promise.all over 10 hero sprites) with an 8 s hard fallback and a 600 ms fade. On a cold cache this was 3-5 s before the world appeared. Trimmed the gate to the 4 assets the first frame actually needs, kicked off background prefetch for the other 12 in parallel, dropped the HERO_READY wait, and shrank the safety net.

What changed

  • featREQUIRED list trimmed 16 → 4 — only the player's idle + walk sheets and the two starting-town NPCs (Elspeth + Brok) gate the reveal. Anything else loads opportunistically.
  • featBackground prefetch — the other 12 sprites (jump / attack / hit / death / 4 class anims / 4 NPCs) get a fire-and-forget new Image(); .src = … at boot so they're warm in the browser cache by the time the runtime tries to draw them. They never block the reveal.
  • featHERO_READY wait dropped — maybeReveal used to hold the overlay until HERO_READY fired (after all 10 hero sprites finished decoding). Now it fades the moment the 4 critical sprites are in. Procedural drawCuteCharacter covers the gap if the hero sheets resolve a frame later — in practice they're usually already cached by the time the camera draws.
  • featHard fallback 8000 → 1200 ms — if a critical sprite 404s or stalls, the overlay still tears down in 1.2 s instead of 8 s, falling back to procedural art.
  • polishFade duration 600 → 220 ms — matches the snappier reveal cadence; the slow fade was bottlenecking even fast loads.

Expected speed-up

  • Cold cache, average broadband: previously ~3-5 s, now 0.5-1.5 s typical.
  • Warm cache: previously ~1.5 s (still gated by HERO_READY's Promise.all), now < 300 ms.
  • Slow / flaky network: previously 8 s hard fallback, now 1.2 s.

Files

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.114. _wireLoadingScreen IIFE rewritten: REQUIRED trimmed, BACKGROUND prefetch added, maybeReveal simplified, fallback + fade timings shortened. +38 / -16 lines.

User feedback: "make it more plush, cute style". Targeted CSS pass on the most-visible modal surfaces — the default .modal shell, inventory tabs, shop rows, shop buttons, and powerup cards. v0.25.112 Mobs flank instead of stacking on the player's pixel

User feedback: monsters cluster at the same pixel location on the player. Cause: every aggroing mob aims for player.x + player.w/2 exactly, so the entire crowd collapses to one stack. Fix: each monster picks a stable per-mob aggro offset (±35..110 px L/R) on first aggro, re-rolled every ~3 s so a long fight has mobs shuffling slots, cleared when the mob drops out of aggro range so re-engagement gets a fresh slot.

What changed

  • featPer-monster m._aggroOffset — randomised ±35..110 px L/R on first aggro. Target X = player.x + player.w/2 + offset, so a wave of three mobs naturally spreads to left, right, and middle slots instead of all converging on one pixel.
  • featRe-roll cadence — m._aggroSettleT ticks every frame; offset re-rolls at > 180 frames (~3 s at 60 fps), so mobs shuffle their flanks during a long fight rather than freezing in formation.
  • polishSettle dead-zone — within 8 px of the chosen slot the mob's vx dampens (× 0.85 / frame) instead of accumulating, so mobs sit at their slot cleanly. Outside the dead zone the original chase-accel kicks in. Within 4 px the facing-flip is skipped so mobs don't oscillate in place.
  • polishCleared on aggro drop — when distToPlayer >= 500 or yDiff >= 200, the offset is wiped (null) so the next aggro round picks a fresh slot.
  • polishAttack ranges unchanged — per-skill attack triggers (typically ≤ 320 px) still fire on a settled mob at ±110 px from the player, so flanking doesn't break melee mob design.

Files

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.112. Regular-AI chase block in updateMonsters (~6 lines) replaced with per-mob target / settle / dead-zone block (~25 lines). One-line offset-clear added to the out-of-aggro branch. +30 / -5 lines.

v0.25.111 Cleaner anime hair — head-hugging dome + swept bangs + ahoge

User feedback: "the shape is bad". The v0.25.71 procedural hair had two structural problems — the silhouette flared 5–8 px past the head edge on each side (read as horns / wings sticking out at ear level), and the five symmetric forelock strands packed across the forehead like comb teeth with no negative space. Fully redesigned both: tighter head-hugging dome with no side flares, and a single big left-sweep bang plus one right counter-strand instead of five.

Shape changes

  • polishSilhouette no longer flares — old ctrl points pushed bezier nodes to sx−5 on the left and sx+38 on the right, both well past the head's vertical edges (sx .. sx+30). New silhouette stays inside those edges with a gentle inward curve on each side; right side rises a touch higher than the left for an asymmetric swept-crown read.
  • polishFive strands → two bangs — replaced the symmetric 5-strand teardrop fringe with a layered bang structure: small right counter-strand in deep tone for asymmetry, large left-sweep bang in lit tone covering most of the forehead, an inner highlight ribbon hugging its lit edge, and a thin centre cowlick at the part line. Same eye-clearance from v0.25.108 (bang tip at sy+11, eye baseline at sy+14).
  • polishTwo flyaway wisps → one ahoge — the v0.25.71 wisp pair (one antenna sticking up, one fin sticking out the right side) read as noise. Replaced with a single curved cowlick spike on top — classic anime "ahoge" charm-piece.
  • polishCrown ribbon tightened — old gloss ribbon wove all the way across the silhouette; new one stays on the un-banged crown only so it doesn't compete with the bang highlight. Same three white sparkles + bright pip kept for catch-light feel.
  • polishInk outline rewritten — traces the new silhouette path. Picked up a third stroke (thin, rgba 0.55) along the lit edge of the main bang for the "drawn-with-a-brush" double-line feel.

v0.25.110 Skill Ranks folded into the Skills tab + projectile-tag bridge for the rank multiplier

The 🎯 Skill Ranks tab introduced in v0.25.109 has been merged into the existing 📖 Skills tab so each skill's keybind, MP / CD / unlock level, description, growth chart, and rank state read as one card. The U panel now has three tabs (Level Up · Boon Loadout · Skills) instead of four. Also fixed: ranks invested in magicBolt / fireball / iceSpike / arrowShot / throwDagger were silently doing nothing because their projectiles tag hits with short tags (bolt / fire / ice / arrow / dagger) that didn't match the SKILL_DEFS id the rank UI lets you invest in. New SKILL_HIT_TAG_TO_DEF_ID bridge resolves that.

UI merge

  • polishOne card per skill — each row in the Skills tab now carries a "RANK" sub-row with the 5-pip strip, a current "+N% dmg" indicator, and the + button. Lv-1→50 growth chart still renders below.

  • polishTab routing — legacy game._uTab === 'ranks' auto-routes to 'skills' in swapPane() so any reload mid-session still lands on the merged view.

Rank multiplier bug fix

  • bugHit-tag ↔ SKILL_DEFS-id bridge — new SKILL_HIT_TAG_TO_DEF_ID table maps the runtime tags hitMonster actually receives back to the SKILL_DEFS ids the rank UI exposes. getSkillRankMul(tag) now tries direct id match first, falls back to the alias map, then returns 1 + rank * 0.08. Pre-fix, ranks invested in magicBolt / fireball / iceSpike / arrowShot / throwDagger applied +0% damage; post-fix they apply the documented +8% / rank.

v0.25.109 Skill Points — per-skill damage rank system + Ability Points relabel

Two currencies now flow from each level-up. The legacy currency (used for tree unlocks + Str/Vit/Agi spending) is renamed to Ability Points — the field player.skillPoints stays put for save compat but every user-facing label now says "Ability Points". A new currency, Skill Points (player.skillRankPoints, player.skillRanks), is granted +1 per level-up and spent in U → 🎯 Skill Ranks to upgrade individual class skills with up to 5 ranks each, where each rank adds +8 % damage to that skill (cap +40 % at rank 5).

What landed

  • featNew currency — player.skillRankPoints + player.skillRanks (map of { skillId → rank }) added to PLAYER_SAVE_FIELDS. Granted +1 in levelUp() right next to the existing ability-point grant.
  • featDamage scaling — getSkillRankMul(skillId) returns 1 + rank * 0.08. Applied inside hitMonster after the global rebalance multipliers so the rank scales with the post-rebalance number. Reactive damage tags (melee · thorns · burn · minion · pet · pack · afterimage) are blacklisted via SKILL_RANK_BLACKLIST so basic-attack / passive damage doesn't double-dip.
  • featSkill Ranks tab — new tab in the U Character panel between Level Up and Boon Loadout. Lists every kit skill with a 5-pip rank track and a + button. Sorted by slot order (D / S / A / E / W / Q / C / X). Reactive skills render dimmed with "reactive · no rank".
  • polishLabel rename — "SKILL POINTS" pill in the Level Up tab is now "ABILITY POINTS". Mobile toast renamed from "+N Skill Point" to "+N Ability Point". Internal field name player.skillPoints kept for save-file compat.

Tuning

  • Cap 5 ranks per skill, +8 % per rank → max +40 % damage uplift on the most-invested skill.
  • Granted at 1 Skill Point per level. Reaching Lv 50 yields 49 points — enough to fully max ~9-10 skills, or spread thinly across the whole kit.
  • Sub-skills only available at job (Lv 25) / master (Lv 50) advancement still appear in the panel and accept ranks once unlocked, since skillsForClass already filters to the current advancement.

Files
