v0.25.16 Phaser 3 migration — Phase 2 (background layer)

Phase 2 of the Phaser migration. The background image layer — every outdoor map's bitmap + haze — now renders through Phaser when the flag is on, via a WebGL-batched TileSprite. The flag-off path is byte-identical to v0.25.15; flag-on users drop the per-frame drawImage × 2 + fillRect sequence in exchange for a single GPU draw call.

🪛 What landed

  • Canvas stacking. Z-index swap: vanilla #game (z:2) now sits over Phaser's #phaser-canvas (z:1). Phaser paints the bg image underneath so monsters, particles, player, and HUD still render on the vanilla canvas as before.
  • LXBackgroundScene replaces the Phase 1 test scene. Preloads all 5 bg PNGs into Phaser's texture cache at boot. A pickBgKey() method mirrors vanilla's _pickBGImage selection rules exactly — explicit mapData.bg override, town → homestead, combat maps → hash-cycle across the other four.
  • TileSprite for tiling. Replaces the vanilla two-image drawImage pattern. WebGL batches arbitrarily-wide parallax scroll into a single draw call. tilePositionX tracks game.camera.x × 0.12 so parallax matches the vanilla factor exactly.
  • Haze overlay. Painted as a Phaser Rectangle at depth 10 with the same rgba(20,24,48,0.18) tint as vanilla's atmospheric haze fillRect.
  • Texture swap on map change. The previous TileSprite is destroyed before a new one is created, so GPU texture slots don't leak across dozens of map loads.
  • Vanilla gate. New helper _phaserHandlingBg() returns true iff (flag on) + (scene ready) + (scene has a texture for this map). When true, drawBackground's very first statement is ctx.clearRect — vanilla leaves the canvas transparent so the Phaser layer underneath shows through. Sky gradient, procedural mountains/pines/flowers/sparkles, haze, and vignette all skipped in that branch.

🎯 Expected wins on the BG layer

Vanilla cost per frame (flag off, bitmap map): 1 full-canvas gradient fill + 2 drawImage tile blits + 1 full-canvas haze fill = 4 full-screen-sized ops. Under HiDPI (2×) that's ~8.6 MP of fill rate per frame just for the bg layer.

Phaser cost per frame (flag on, bitmap map): 1 batched WebGL draw call for the TileSprite + 1 batched draw for the haze Rectangle. GPU batching makes the marginal cost of the tile negligible once the texture is uploaded.

Special backdrops unchanged

Sanctum cosmos, zodiac boss arenas, subway carriage, and the zodiac hub all still render through the vanilla canvas — pickBgKey returns null for those and the vanilla fallback path is untouched. Boss-arena decor also still rides on vanilla (painted on top of the Phaser bg).

📅 Migration roadmap (reminder)

  • ✅ Phase 1. Scaffolding + proof-of-concept (v0.25.15).
  • ✅ Phase 2. Background image layer (this release).
  • Phase 3. Character + nameplate → Phaser sprites.
  • Phase 4. Monsters, projectiles, particles (biggest perf payoff).
  • Phase 5. HUD.
  • Phase 6. Retire the vanilla canvas path.

How to try it

Append ?phaser=1 to the game URL, or run localStorage.setItem('levelx_phaser', '1') in DevTools and reload. On any outdoor map the bg image is now GPU-rendered; the test-scene yellow diamond from v0.25.15 is gone (replaced by the real bg). window.__LX_PHASER.scene.getScene('lx_bg') is the scene object for DevTools debugging.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.16. Three focused edits: #game gets position:relative; z-index:2, #phaser-canvas z-index drops to 1. Phaser bootstrap scene body rewritten into LXBackgroundScene (~55 lines). drawBackground gets a _phaserHandlingBg() early-out gate.
  • No save/network/gameplay/protocol impact. Flag-off path is byte-identical to v0.25.15.

v0.25.15 Phaser 3 migration — Phase 1 (scaffolding)

Phase 1 of a multi-session migration to Phaser 3. No visible gameplay change. Lands the plumbing (CDN load, parent DOM element, bootstrap IIFE, proof-of-concept test scene) so future sessions can incrementally port the render layer (background → characters → monsters → particles → HUD) without another scaffolding pass. Flag-gated — the vanilla canvas build is byte-identical for any user who doesn't explicitly opt in.

🎯 Why Phaser 3?

The vanilla Canvas 2D render layer issues one GPU call per fillRect/arc. On mobile GPUs that's the dominant frame-time cost — v0.25.9 and v0.25.14 were both perf passes patching this. Phaser 3's WebGL batcher collapses hundreds of sprites into a single draw call. Expected mobile FPS win: 2-4× on the same content.

🪛 What landed

  • Flag. window.__PHASER_ENABLED is set at script-eval time from either ?phaser=1 (URL) or localStorage.levelx_phaser=1 (persistent). No visual or cost impact when off.
  • CDN load. Second inline <script> appends a Phaser 3.80.1 CDN tag to <head> only when the flag is on. Zero download cost otherwise.
  • Parent DOM. New #phaser-canvas div sits over the existing #game canvas with pointer-events:none, display:none by default. Becomes visible when the bootstrap flips it on.
  • Bootstrap. _bootstrapPhaser() runs at page load; short-circuits when the flag is off. Polls for the Phaser global every 50 ms, then spins up a Phaser.Game configured with type: Phaser.AUTO (WebGL preferred, Canvas fallback), transparent: true, 960×560 logical size, arcade physics pre-wired.
  • Test scene. Renders a 32-px yellow diamond (generated in-memory — zero asset dependency) plus a "PHASER ON" label in the top-left. Seeing those confirms the entire pipeline works end-to-end.
  • Debug handle. window.__LX_PHASER exposes the Game instance for interactive DevTools inspection and for future migration-step wiring.

📅 Migration roadmap (for reference)

  • v0.25.15 (this release) — Phase 1. Scaffolding + proof-of-concept. Done.
  • Phase 2. Port drawBackground → Phaser scene with the 5 BG images as textures + a Phaser particle emitter for the drift sparkles.
  • Phase 3. Port drawCuteCharacter and the player nameplate → Phaser sprites. Retire _chibiApply / _chibiRestore.
  • Phase 4. Monsters, projectiles, particles. Biggest batching win lives here — boss arenas with 3+ elites currently pay the bulk of the fillrate tax.
  • Phase 5. HUD (HP/MP bars, level-up panel, inventory overlay).
  • Phase 6. Retire the vanilla canvas path; maple_game.html becomes a pure Phaser scene.

How to try it

Append ?phaser=1 to the game URL, or run localStorage.setItem('levelx_phaser', '1') in DevTools and reload. You should see a rotating yellow diamond + "PHASER ON" label in the top-left corner of the game canvas, overlaid on the usual vanilla render.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.15. Two new <script> blocks in <head> (flag eval + CDN loader). New #phaser-canvas parent div next to #game. New _bootstrapPhaser() IIFE + _PhaserTestScene class at the top of the main script (~70 lines). No changes to existing render paths.
  • No save/network/gameplay impact. Flag-off behaviour is identical to v0.25.14.

v0.25.14 Mobile perf pass + dreamier backgrounds

Two-in-one release: a targeted mobile frame-rate pass (DPR cap, halved particle budgets, skip ambient sparkles) and a full replacement of the five pixel-art backgrounds with a more tonally consistent pastel/dreamy set. Mobile fill-rate cost drops by roughly 4×; desktop is unchanged aside from the new artwork.

📱 Mobile perf

  • Cap HiDPI at dpr = 1 on mobile. Single biggest win. Phones commonly report devicePixelRatio of 2-4; the v0.25.2 cap was Math.min(2, dpr), still 4× the fill rate per frame on every Retina-class mobile. The coarse-pointer / narrow-viewport heuristic (same one _isMobileClient uses) now drops to 1. Desktop still caps at 2×.
  • Halved particle / dmg-number / afterimage budgets on mobile. MAX_PARTICLES 500 → 200, MAX_DMG_NUMBERS 40 → 24, MAX_AFTERIMAGES 25 → 12. 500-particle combo bursts were stuttering mobile GPUs during boss phase transitions. 200 still carries the visual read.
  • Skip the drift-sparkle ambient effect on mobile. The 14-18 sparkle-loop in drawBackground ran under globalCompositeOperation='lighter', which forces a full RMW per pixel — particularly expensive on mobile GPUs for pure decorative fidelity. Wrapped in !_IS_MOBILE_AT_LOAD.

🖼️ Background replacement

All five slots swapped for a new painterly pixel-art set that share a pastel/dreamy palette and big cumulus cloud compositions:

  • bg_forest.png — purple & green trees, pink cumulus, boulders, dark grass baseline.
  • bg_valley.png — stone arch bridge + flanking trees + distant misty mountain.
  • bg_meadow.png — teal tree on rocks + pink sunset clouds + flower-speckled grass.
  • bg_misty.png — huge rainbow autumn oak on stacked rocks + moody pastel palette.
  • bg_homestead.png — big oak + giant pink cumulus + red autumn tree (town default).

Selection logic unchanged — town still picks homestead, combat maps still cycle by map-ID hash across the other four, special backdrops (sanctum / zodiac / subway) still ignore the folder.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.14. HiDPI IIFE gets a mobile cap. _IS_MOBILE_AT_LOAD module-level flag feeds three budget constants and the sparkle-loop guard. No save/network/gameplay impact.
  • backgrounds/bg_forest.png, bg_valley.png, bg_meadow.png, bg_misty.png, bg_homestead.png — binary content replaced. Filenames and slot mapping unchanged.

v0.25.13 Five named background slots + map-hash cycle

Expanded the v0.25.12 background system from three slots to six (five named outdoor scenes plus the legacy main slot). Combat maps now deterministically cycle through the loaded outdoor backdrops by hashing their map ID, so each map gets its own visual identity without you having to hand-assign every one.

🖼️ New slots (drop into backgrounds/)

  • bg_forest.png — bright sunny forest framing distant mountains.
  • bg_valley.png — mountain valley with oak + snow peaks + dirt strata.
  • bg_meadow.png — meadow with blossom tree, rocks, big cumulus clouds. New.
  • bg_misty.png — foggy mountain forest with mossy ledges + distant eagle. New.
  • bg_homestead.png — farmhouse on a golden-grass hillside + sky clouds. New.

🎯 Smart selection

  1. Per-map override (highest priority) — any map in the MAPS object can set bg: 'forest' | 'valley' | 'meadow' | 'misty' | 'homestead' to pin a specific scene.
  2. Town default changed — isTown: true now defaults to homestead (farmhouse reads more like a village hub), falling back to valley.
  3. Combat-map cycle — non-town maps run their ID through a cheap string hash and pick one of the loaded outdoor slots. Same map always gets the same backdrop; different maps get different ones. Zero per-map config required.
  4. Unchanged — special backdrops (sanctum, zodiac, subway) still ignore this folder; procedural parallax still kicks in when no slot is loaded.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.13. BG_IMAGES map grows from 3 slots to 6. New _hashStr helper + _BG_CYCLE constant drive the combat-map variety selection. _pickBGImage's town branch switches to homestead-first, and the combat branch now picks by hash instead of a fixed slot.
  • backgrounds/README.md — full rewrite covering the five named slots, the selection rules, sizing guidance, and a worked example of pinning via mapData.bg.
  • No save/network/gameplay impact. All additive — behaviour with zero images present is unchanged from v0.25.11.

v0.25.12 Drop-in background images — forest & valley slots

Expanded the single-image BG_IMG loader from v0.24.1 into a three-slot system. Drop bg_forest.png and bg_valley.png into the new backgrounds/ folder and the game picks them up automatically on the next load — forest for outdoor combat maps, valley for the town hub. If a slot is empty, the procedural parallax from v0.25.11 takes over as the fallback, so the game never looks broken.

🖼️ Slots

  • backgrounds/bg_forest.png — all combat / field / outdoor maps.
  • backgrounds/bg_valley.png — town hub (Everdawn Village).
  • backgrounds/main_bg.png — legacy single-image slot (v0.24.1), ignored if either of the two above is loaded for the current map.
  • Special backdrops (sanctum cosmos, zodiac arenas, subway carriage) never use a bitmap — they keep their authored art.

🧩 How selection works

  1. Map can set an explicit override via mapData.bg = 'forest' | 'valley' | 'main'. Takes priority if that slot is loaded.
  2. Default rule: isTown → valley, everything else → forest, fall back to main.
  3. If no slot is loaded, return null and fall through to the procedural faceted-mountain parallax.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.12. BG_IMG → BG_IMAGES map with _loadBG(path) helper, plus _pickBGImage() resolver. drawBackground's image-path branch calls the resolver instead of checking the single image directly. BG_IMG kept as an alias pointing at BG_IMAGES.main for back-compat.
  • backgrounds/README.md (new) — explains the slot list, sizing guidance (960×560 logical, 16:9-ish), draw order, and which maps use which slot.
  • No save-compat / network / gameplay impact. Fully additive — if you don't drop any images in, the game looks identical to v0.25.11.

v0.25.11 Art pass — faceted mountains, detailed pines, richer sky

Big visual upgrade on the background parallax. The smooth sine-wave mountain silhouettes got replaced with flat low-poly faceted peaks in the "origami mountain" style of modern indie chibi RPGs. Pines got three-tier detail with visible branch silhouettes and split lit/shadow faces. The sky gradient picked up two extra colour stops for painterly atmospheric depth. Matches the art reference shared in-thread.

🏔️ Faceted low-poly mountains (3 layers)

  • Farthest range. Furthest silhouette now renders as angular peaks instead of sine-wave hats. A darker shadow facet overlays the right half of every peak, so each mountain reads as a 3D wedge. Atmospheric perspective preserved (alpha 0.75, sky-blended colour).
  • Distant range. Same faceted rewrite, with the shadow tone mixing the lit colour against a cool indigo (#0a0820 at 35%) for a stronger volume read than the old flat fill.
  • Mid range. Sharpest, closest mountain layer — darkest shadow facet for max foreground pop. Snow/crag caps split into lit + shadow halves instead of floating isoceles triangles, so they match the range's cel-shading language.

🌲 Multi-tier pine silhouettes

Old treeline was two stacked triangles per tree — read as "green pyramid" from a distance. New pines have:

  • A thin brown trunk drawn first (drawn under the branch tufts).
  • Three branch tiers stacked up the stem: widest tier at the bottom, narrowest spire at the top — unambiguously conifer.
  • Each tier split into lit + shadow triangle halves using the same cel language as the mountains. 6 fills per tree × 20 trees = 120 fills per frame, still well under budget.
  • Taller overall (52 + i%3 × 18 vs. the old 44 + i%3 × 14) so trees command more of the foreground silhouette.

🌇 Enriched sky gradient

Sky linear gradient went from 3 stops (top / 0.6 mid / horizon) to 5 stops with _mixHex-blended intermediates at 0.35 (upper-mid) and 0.88 (horizon glow). The 0.88 stop lifts the just-above-horizon band into a painterly warm glow that makes the mountain silhouettes sit against real atmosphere instead of a solid colour bar. Cache still refreshes only on palette change — same perf budget as before.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.11. Three mountain-range draw blocks rewritten in drawBackground (farthest, far, mid). Treeline draw block rewritten for multi-tier pines. Sky gradient cache expanded to 5 stops. No new helper functions — all changes live inside the existing drawBackground body. Special backdrops (sanctum cosmos, zodiac arenas, subway carriage) are untouched — they have their own art and were already at a higher visual fidelity.
  • No save/network/gameplay impact. Pure visuals.

v0.25.10 Zodiac cel-shading polish

A second pass on the shared _zBodyPath helper that renders all 12 zodiac bosses. v0.25.1 introduced the 2-tone cel-shade; this release sharpens the ink, deepens the shadow step, brightens the highlight, and adds a specular pip so bosses read as glossy cel-shaded characters rather than flat-painted cards.

🎨 Six tuning passes

  • Thicker outline, inkier black. Flat 4 px #120615 → scaled max(3.5, r * 0.09) px #0a0310. Big bosses (Taurus, Leo, Aries) now get a proportionally thicker ink so they don't look wiry.
  • Inner ink contour. A second soft stroke INSIDE the silhouette in a fill × 35% black tint, alpha 0.6. Simulates the "paint bleed" next to inked lines in real cel-shaded art — the outline reads as ink on paint instead of a cut-out edge.
  • Deeper second shade. The "deep shadow" cel step mixes the midtone with black at 0.55 instead of 0.45. The three-tier rail (lit / shade / deep) now has real volume instead of two slightly-different mids.
  • Brighter highlight. Upper-left highlight wedge mix 32% → 42% white, alpha 0.9 → 0.95. The lit side actually reads lit now.
  • Specular pip. A small near-white circle (radius scales with r) inside the highlight zone. Classic cel-shading trick for shiny surfaces — bosses now have that "living glass" glossiness.
  • Thicker cel-step rim lines. Boundary stroke 1.2 px flat → max(1.6, r * 0.045). Small bosses keep a delicate 1.6 px rim, big bosses get 3-4 px so the shading transition reads as deliberate cel ink.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.10, rewrite of _zBodyPath's outline / shade / highlight passes. All 12 zodiac signs share this helper and inherit the improved look automatically. Per-sign draw functions (horns, pincers, etc.) untouched. No save-compat impact.

v0.25.9 Perf pass — cached gradients + measureText

Pure performance work, no visual change. Four per-frame hot spots identified from a render-path audit were caching-class wins — gradient rasterization and measureText calls that were being redone every frame despite producing identical results. Under HiDPI (v0.25.2's 2× canvas scaling = 4× fill rate), these adds up to measurable stutter, especially on boss arenas with multiple elites.

🚀 What got faster

  • Vignette gradient cached once. The full-screen radial vignette at the end of drawBackground was rebuilding its gradient object every frame, even though W and H are constants for the life of the page. Now lazily built once into _vignetteGradCache and reused forever. Under HiDPI this gradient fills ~2.15 million pixels per frame — reallocating the gradient object that often was a real cost.
  • Carriage vignette cached too. Same fix for drawCarriageInterior's ambient vignette (cached in _carriageVignetteGradCache).
  • Elite + mini-boss auras → off-screen canvas cache. Both aura types used to build a fresh createRadialGradient every frame for every on-screen elite/miniboss. New strategy: a Map-keyed off-screen canvas cache indexed by (width, height). First time any unique size appears the aura renders ONCE into an off-screen canvas; every subsequent frame just blits via drawImage. Pulse animation moves from varying the gradient radius to modulating globalAlpha (+/- 8-10%) — visually near-identical, hugely cheaper. On maps with 3+ elites on screen the framerate win is noticeable.
  • Nameplate measureText cached. The peer render loop called ctx.measureText(name) once per peer per frame — measureText forces font-metrics recalculation. Same bug on the local _drawPlayerNameTag. Now cached on the peer object (p._nameCache / p._nameTw) and a module-level _playerNameTagCache, invalidated only when the display string actually changes.

Not in this pass

The ambient flora loops (treeline + flowers in drawBackground) and the HiDPI toggle itself were flagged but not changed — they're either cheaper than they look (flora is just 52 small path/fills) or need a settings UI to expose properly. If lag persists on low-end devices, a HiDPI opt-out toggle is the next step.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.9. Four caches introduced (_vignetteGradCache, _carriageVignetteGradCache, _auraCache Map with _getEliteAuraCanvas / _getMiniBossAuraCanvas, and the peer/player nameplate width caches). No rendering output changed; every cache hands the draw call identical pixels to what the per-frame path produced before. No save-compat impact.

v0.25.8 Ballista Siege Volley — 8-shot barrage

The Archer → Sniper → Ballista master signature (G slot) now fires 8 piercing shots instead of 4. Vertical spread tightened so the whole burst fits cleanly inside the player's silhouette; cadence tightened so the barrage still resolves in under half a second. Feels like a wall-of-lead now rather than a slow sprinkler.

🛡️ Siege Volley (Ballista master)

  • Bullet count 4 → 8 — double the payload.
  • Vertical spacing 10 → 7 px — 8 × 7 = 56 px tall, fits just outside the 44 px player envelope so the fan reads as one wide swath, not a scattered column.
  • Cadence 90 → 70 ms — full skill resolves in ~490 ms, still a single burst.
  • Per-bullet stats unchanged — damage (ATK × 3.5 + 25), range, pierce, defBreak all intact. Total skill damage ≈ 2× the old by design; this is a Lv 30 master-tier signature and should feel like one.
  • Tooltip updated to "8-shot piercing barrage; breaks defense." to match.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.8. Two edits: the ballista_volley skill implementation (loop count, y stride, scheduleSkillTimer cadence) and the MASTER_SKILLS.ballista_volley.desc tooltip string. No other skills touched.

v0.25.7 Balance pass — smoother climb, richer loot

Numbers-only rebalance across XP progression, drop rates, chest rewards, and the death penalty. The long L40→50 wall came down, every mob in the world can now theoretically drop a legendary, chests pay 25-50% more mesos, and dying costs 35% of your stash instead of 50%. No mechanics changed — this is purely constants being retuned.

📈 Progression

  • XP curve softened at Lv 30+. Per-level multiplier 1.22 → 1.20 at Lv 30-39 and 1.26 → 1.22 at Lv 40-50. The old 1.26× back-half acceleration compounded into a 2-hour wall between 40 and 50, especially painful across prestige runs. 1.22× is still a clear ramp without feeling like a brick.
  • Global kill XP 1.25 → 1.35. Applied at the kill site, so prestige and combo multipliers still stack cleanly on top. Combined with the curve change this takes about 8% off the L1→50 climb.

💎 Drops

  • Normal-mob drop rate 14% → 18%. Bosses still 100%, elites still 50%. LCK attribute + Scavenger's Eye milestone still multiply on top.
  • Normals can now drop legendaries. Rarity pool went from {common:32, rare:10, epic:2, legendary:0} to {common:32, rare:10, epic:3, legendary:1}. At the new 18% drop rate that's ~0.4% legendary per kill — grind finally has a lottery-ticket feeling.
  • Elites juicier. {common:8, rare:14, epic:5, legendary:1} → {common:6, rare:12, epic:6, legendary:2}. More epics, 2× the legendary weight. Elites should feel like a prize fight — now they do.
  • Boss pool unchanged. Already drops legendaries ~25% of the time; doesn't need a buff.

💰 Chests & Death

  • Wood chests 40-120 → 60-160 (+50% floor / +33% ceiling).
  • Silver chests 200-400 → 260-500 (+30% floor / +25% ceiling).
  • Gold chests 600-1200 → 800-1500 (+33% floor / +25% ceiling). Dawnshard legendaries at the shop cost 7000-8000; the old Gold range meant 7+ Gold chests per shop legendary, disproportionate to how rare Gold chests are.
  • Death meso penalty 50% → 35%. Still stings enough to matter; no longer wipes over a third of your stash per death. XP penalty (0 / 3 / 5 / 8% by level bracket) is unchanged and remains the primary "don't die" deterrent.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.7. Eight surgical constant edits, each in its own commit for easy rollback: _maybeLevelUp curveMul, awardXp xpCurveMul, dropChance base, rollItemDrop rarityWeights (two tiers), openChest rewards table, death meso factor. No code paths moved — purely number tuning.
  • Save-compat: yes. Existing characters inherit the new rates on their next kill / chest / death.

v0.25.6 Codex of Shardfall — press 1 for the lore map

A new in-game lore reader. Press 1 to pause the action and open a tabbed parchment codex with the game's whole setting laid out in one place — the world's backstory, all twelve zodiac bosses, every class/job/master branch, and the legendary Dawnshard regalia. All data is pulled from the live CLASSES / JOBS / MASTERS / ZODIAC_SIGNS constants, so the codex auto-updates when new content lands — no stale copy.

📖 Four tabs

  • The World. Prose intro to the Shardfall (the shattering of the sky twelve ages ago), Everdawn Village (the last lit town and its Bazaar economy), and the expedition's purpose (reclaiming the fallen shards one zodiac at a time).
  • The Twelve Zodiac. 3-column grid card-list of every zodiac boss — glyph, name, element, required level, and a one-line flavour blurb. Pulled from ZODIAC_SIGNS so it stays in sync automatically.
  • The Four Paths. Class → Job → Master tree for all four classes. Each class block shows its tagline and both job branches, with the two master-tier endings listed under each job (color-coded by job/master palette).
  • Relics & Legends. Dawnshard regalia cards (Blade / Aegis / Medallion), the Prestige mechanic, and lore on Lumens — the currency of Everdawn.

⌨️ Keybind

1 toggles the codex open / closed. Guarded against the existing 1+2+3 dev-console combo by requiring that 2 and 3 are NOT currently held when 1 fires, so holding all three still opens the dev console. Toggle pattern matches B / K / U.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.6. New DOM: #lore-modal with .lore-modal / .lore-tab / .lore-card / .lore-path CSS styles. New JS: openLoreMap, closeLoreMap, toggleLoreMap, _renderLoreTab, and the static LORE_WORLD_HTML block. Keydown listener gets the solo-1 toggle.
  • Fully additive — no save-format change, no network protocol change, no gameplay/combat impact. Game pauses while the codex is open.

v0.25.5 Press 0 lets you choose your job path

Small but meaningful dev-shortcut tweak. 0 used to silently auto-pick CLASSES[cls].jobs[0] and the first listed master after boosting to Lv 50 — great if you wanted "any build right now," awful if you actually wanted to test a specific path. It now opens the advancement picker so you choose.

What changed

  • 0 still boosts to Lv 50 — same HP / MP / ATK / DEF / skill-point catch-up as before, so the fully-kitted-out feel is preserved.
  • New: choice cards instead of silent auto-pick. After the boost, resetJobAndMaster clears any current job/master (cleanly un-applying their stats), then openAdvancement fires. The existing card.onclick chain flows you straight into master selection after you pick your job — so a single 0 press gets you both choices offered.
  • Toast updated to "Dev: Lv 50 — pick your job + master path" so the new behaviour is self-announcing.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.5, 0-key handler in the global keydown listener. Auto-pick branch (applyJob(jobs[0]), applyMaster(masters[0])) replaced with resetJobAndMaster() + openAdvancement(). No save-compat impact; existing characters who already advanced keep their picks unless they press 0 again.

v0.25.4 Cuter skies — cute sun, varied clouds, sparkles, flowers

A storybook polish pass on the background parallax. The celestial disc now has a personality (beaming sun by day, sleepy moon by night), every cloud gets one of three cute expressions, pastel sparkles and tiny hearts drift across bright skies, and 4-petal flower tufts sprinkle along the treeline. All additive — zero gameplay impact, pure scene-setting.

☀️ What changed

  • Cute sun face. Bright-map celestial disc now has round eyes with sparkle highlights, pink blush circles, and a beaming smile. Lives inside a new _drawCelestialFace helper so the sun disc itself stays untouched.
  • Sleepy moon. Dark-map moon gets closed-eye arcs (^_^) and a tiny smile painted on the lit crescent, plus soft pink sleep-blush. Makes dungeons feel less lonely at night.
  • Cloud personalities. Previously only ~half of the clouds (even-sized ones) drew faces, and they all had the same smile. Each cloud now picks a stable face variant at buildBackdrop time — classic smile, closed-eye happy (^_^), or heart-eye grin with open-mouth excitement. Dark maps still leave clouds as silhouettes for atmosphere.
  • Treeline flowers. 32 tiny 4-petal blooms tucked between the pines at the treeline base. Bright maps pull from a pink / buttercup / lilac / daisy palette; dark maps use cooler moonlit blue / dusk lilac / mint. Parallax slightly slower than the trees so the flowers read as sitting behind the trunks.
  • Drifting sparkles + hearts. A slow sprinkle of twinkles and tiny hearts floating across the sky. Bright maps: pink / yellow / mint / lilac pastels with occasional heart accents. Dark maps: cooler snowflake-style blues and lavenders. Additive blend gives a soft glow, camera-parallax anchored so they drift with the world.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.4. New helpers: _drawCelestialFace, _drawCloudFace, _drawMiniHeart. buildBackdrop stashes a face variant per cloud. drawBackground draws flowers after the treeline and sparkles after the birds.
  • No save-compat impact, no gameplay change, no network protocol change. Pure visual polish. Skipped for sanctum / subway / zodiac arenas (they have custom backdrops already).

v0.25.3 Chat bubble lift · IGN always below character

Two small nameplate / chat polish passes. The speech bubble that pops above your hero after you send a chat line now sits clearly above the head with breathing room — previously the tail was kissing the hair. And the IGN label is now guaranteed to render below the character even if you never opened the character creator, with the class name used as a graceful fallback.

💬 What changed

  • Local chat bubble lifted. Anchor moved from player.y - 4 to player.y - 34. The bubble now hovers with ~30 px of clearance above the head instead of overlapping the hair.
  • Peer chat bubble matched. Remote players got the same lift — chat from sy - 24 to sy - 54, emote icon from sy - 32 to sy - 72 so the emote still floats above the speech bubble without stacking into it.
  • Peer name tag moved below the feet. Remote players used to show their name + Lv tag above their head; it's now anchored at sy + 58 (below body, matching the local hero's placement). Airspace above peers is now owned by HP bar → chat → emote, which is the classic MMO stack.
  • Local IGN fallback. If player.look.name is empty (fresh character, name input never touched), _drawPlayerNameTag now falls back to the title-cased class — "Warrior", "Mage", "Archer", etc. — so there's always a label below the character.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.3, drawClassIdentityHUD bubble anchor, peer render block (chat + emote + name tag coords), _drawPlayerNameTag fallback. Pure UI positioning; no gameplay, no save format, no network protocol impact.

v0.25.2 Procedural art restore · HiDPI canvas

Rollback of the experimental PNG sprite composite — the procedural Dragon-Quest-style hero (drawCuteCharacter) is back to being the canonical renderer. At the same time the canvas picked up a devicePixelRatio upgrade so the game renders crisp on Retina and other high-DPI displays without changing its on-screen size.

🎨 What changed

  • PNG sprite path disabled. drawLayeredCharacter() now returns false unconditionally, so drawPlayer always falls through to the procedural drawCuteCharacter. The original sprite composite is kept as a block comment for reference — not deleted, just dormant.
  • Boot-time sprite loader silenced. loadCharacterAssets() is commented out in the boot sequence, so the ASSETS map stays empty and no Sprites/character/ PNGs are fetched. Zero network work, zero decoding, zero flicker on first frame.
  • HiDPI canvas. On displays with devicePixelRatio > 1, the canvas's backing buffer is scaled up to W × dpr by H × dpr (capped at 2× to keep fill-rate sane), while the CSS size stays locked at the logical 960 × 560. A matching ctx.setTransform(dpr, 0, 0, dpr, 0, 0) means every existing drawing call still addresses the logical grid — no per-call changes, just sharper pixels.

Why revert the sprites

The PNG composite looked fine in isolation but didn't match the rest of the game's procedural, palette-driven visual identity. The DQ-style cute hero was always the art direction; the sprite experiment was a branch that didn't pan out. Keeping the composite code commented means a future art pass can re-enable it instantly without a diff archaeology session.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — version bump to v0.25.2, HiDPI IIFE added right after the ctx binding, drawLayeredCharacter stubbed with a return false + commented body, loadCharacterAssets() boot call commented.
  • No save-compat impact. No gameplay changes. Pure render / visual.

v0.25.1 Zodiac bosses — 2-shade cel-shade

Every zodiac boss now draws with proper two-tone cel-shading. The shared _zBodyPath helper that renders all 12 signs (Aries ram, Taurus bull, Gemini twins, Cancer crab, Leo sun, Virgo maiden, Libra scales, Scorpio, Sagittarius, Capricorn, Aquarius, Pisces) got four new clipped passes for richer silhouettes.

🎨 What changed in _zBodyPath

  1. Bold outline (unchanged) — 4 px round-joined #120615 stroke for silhouette pop.
  2. Base fill (unchanged) — fully lit tone.
  3. Midtone shadow (unchanged) — existing lower-right diagonal wedge.
  4. NEW — Deep shadow (the "second cel shade") — computed as _mixHex(shade, '#000000', 0.45), rendered as a lower-right triangular band that gives the body weight and grounds it.
  5. NEW — Highlight wedge — upper-left, _mixHex(fill, '#ffffff', 0.32) at 90% alpha. Gives a subtle sheen that makes the ram / bull / lion / etc read as 3D volume rather than flat.
  6. NEW — Cel step rims — thin 1.2 px deep-shade lines along the transition boundaries between the midtone and deep shadow. Crisps up the tonal step so the shade reads as intentional cel-shading rather than an accidental gradient smear.

Why 2-shade matters

Classic cel-shaded art (Dragon Quest, Zelda: Wind Waker, MapleStory itself) uses two discrete shade tones: a midtone and a deep shadow. One shade alone reads as slightly rounded; two tones create visible volume by showing the lit side, the turning edge, and the cast-shadow core. The zodiac bosses are big, slow, dramatic fights — they deserve the extra tonal depth.

Affected

  • All 12 zodiac bosses share _zBodyPath, so every sign picks up the new shading automatically.
  • Zodiac elite / mini-boss variants also benefit (same draw path).
  • Regular mob art is unaffected — this is a zodiac-only helper.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html — _zBodyPath(path, fill, shade, cx, cy, r) rewritten with five sequential clipped passes (outline, base, midtone wedge, deep shadow, highlight + step rims). Same call signature, so the 12 per-sign draw functions need no changes.
  • Save-compat: yes. Pure visual update.

v0.25.0 Backend: Accounts · Passwords · Sessions · Persistent saves

Server-side MMORPG foundations land. The server/ directory gets a full account system — HTTP register/login endpoints, scrypt password hashing, HMAC-signed stateless session tokens, per-account SQLite save persistence, WebSocket auth, and in-memory rate limiting. Dockerfile + Fly.io + Railway deploy configs are wired up. The game client still runs as a guest for now; the client-side login UI + save-sync ships next in v0.25.1.

📚 New: server/auth.js

  • SQLite schema — accounts (id, username, email, password_hash, password_salt, created_at, last_login_at, oauth_provider, oauth_subject) + saves (account_id, data, updated_at) with cascade delete. oauth_* columns wait for Google/Discord wiring without a schema change.
  • Password hashing via Node's stdlib crypto.scryptSync (N=16384, r=8, p=1, 64-byte output) with 16-byte random per-password salt. Verification uses crypto.timingSafeEqual to defeat timing attacks.
  • Session tokens are HMAC-SHA256 signed JSON — <base64url(payload)>.<base64url(sig)>. Stateless: no session table, no DB lookup to verify. Default 30-day TTL, configurable via SESSION_TTL_DAYS.
  • Input validation baked in — username 3-20 chars [a-zA-Z0-9_], password 8-200 chars, optional email with RFC-lite regex.
  • Per-account save blob — 1 MB cap, stored as JSON text in SQLite. getSave(id) / putSave(id, data) round-trip.
  • Uses Node 22+'s built-in node:sqlite — zero native compile, zero extra deps beyond ws.

🌐 HTTP endpoints

MethodPathBodyResponse
GET/ · /health—{ ok, version, rooms, totalPlayers, accounts, saves }
POST/api/register{ username, password, email? }201 { token, user } or 400/409
POST/api/login{ username, password }200 { token, user } or 401
POST/api/logout—{ ok } (advisory)
GET/api/meBearer token{ user } or 401
GET/api/saveBearer token{ data, updatedAt } or 401
PUT/api/saveJSON save + Bearer{ ok, updatedAt }
DELETE/api/accountBearer token{ ok }
ALL/api/oauth/:provider—501 (stub)

🔐 WebSocket auth (optional, guest mode still works)

  • New {t:'auth', token} message promotes a guest socket to an authenticated account. Server replies with {t:'auth_ok', user} or {t:'error', code:'bad_token'}.
  • New {t:'save', data} WS message persists a save blob server-side. Requires a prior successful auth; otherwise replies {t:'error', code:'unauthed'}.
  • welcome now includes an authed boolean so peers can show an account badge if/when we add that.
  • All existing guest behaviour (hello / state / chat / emote / map) unchanged — no breaking change for v0.24.x clients.

🛡️ Safety + rate limiting

  • In-memory per-IP rate limiter: 5 registers/min, 10 logins/min. 429 with a friendly message past the limit.
  • CORS is fully open (Access-Control-Allow-Origin: *) — tighten to your game's origin when deploying publicly.
  • Uniform 401 Invalid credentials on login failure (no username probe surface).
  • SECRET env var becomes mandatory in production — server refuses to boot without it when NODE_ENV=production.
  • Graceful shutdown: SIGTERM/SIGINT closes the SQLite handle before exit.
  • Idle socket sweeper (60s) unchanged.

🚢 Deploy-ready

  • Dockerfile — Node 22-alpine, 58 MB final image, VOLUME /app/data for SQLite persistence.
  • fly.toml.example — one-shot Fly.io config with volume mount, auto-scale-to-zero, /health probe, secrets workflow.
  • railway.json.example — Railway equivalent with Dockerfile build + healthcheck.
  • .env.example — documents every env var with production guidance.

✅ Smoke-tested end-to-end

Before shipping I ran the full register → login → /api/me → PUT /api/save → GET /api/save → wrong password → duplicate register → OAuth stub → validation → unauth → self-delete loop, plus a WebSocket auth/hello/save round-trip, plus rate-limit overflow. All 14 paths responded correctly:

REGISTER 201 OK id=1
LOGIN    200 OK
ME       200 hero123
PUT SAVE 200 OK
GET SAVE 200 {"level":42,"inventory":["sword","potion"],"mesos":5000}
BADLOG   401 Invalid credentials
DUPREG   409 Username or email already registered
OAUTH    501 OAuth not yet implemented
VALIDAT  400 Username too short (min 3)
NOAUTH   401 Invalid or expired token

WS auth_ok  → authed account
WS welcome  → authed: true
WS save_ok  → persisted
RATE 6/7   → 429 Too many registration attempts

🔜 What's NOT in this ship (coming in v0.25.1)

  • Client-side login UI. Register/Login form in the Multiplayer modal, token storage in localStorage, auth-on-WS-connect wiring.
  • Server-side save UI. Manual save button + auto-sync hooks.
  • OAuth flow. Endpoint is a 501 stub; schema is ready.
  • Email verification / password reset. Needs an SMTP provider.
  • Authoritative combat. Still client-side; per-client mob instances. The big milestone.

Touched surface

  • New files: server/auth.js (390 LOC), server/fly.toml.example, server/railway.json.example, server/.env.example.
  • Rewritten: server/server.js (HTTP routing + WS auth + rate limiting), server/package.json (ws only, Node 22+), server/Dockerfile (Node 22-alpine, single stage), server/README.md (full API + deploy guide).
  • maple_game.html — version bump only. Client still runs as guest.
  • Save-compat: yes. No client save format change.

v0.24.3 Typable chat system · 60-char bubbles · Works offline

Chat is now a real in-world feature. Press Enter any time to type a message — solo or multiplayer — and it floats as a speech bubble above your character for 4 seconds. Bubbles hard-cap at 60 characters each, enforced at the input level and on send.

💬 Chat input

  • Press Enter while playing to open the chat input (bottom-left). Previously only worked while connected to a multiplayer server.
  • Press Enter again (or click outside) to send. Press Esc to cancel without sending.
  • Hard cap at 60 chars per bubble — enforced three ways:
    • <input maxlength="60"> stops you typing past 60.
    • _mpSendChat() .slice(0, 60) on send defensively.
    • Server trims to its own 200-char max, but clients never send more than 60 anyway.
  • Control chars (tabs, newlines) are stripped. Blank messages are ignored.

💭 Local chat bubble

  • Always fires — whether or not you're connected. The bubble renders above your character using the same _drawBubble() helper as mobs / NPCs / peers, so the look is consistent.
  • 4 s lifetime, fades out over the last 500 ms.
  • Messages also land in the chat log (bottom-left), tagged as me so your lines are colour-highlighted.
  • New player._chat field initialized on the player literal. Decayed in drawClassIdentityHUD each frame.

🌐 Multiplayer still works

  • When connected, the same Enter flow broadcasts to the room via the existing WebSocket chat message.
  • Server-echoed own messages are now suppressed to avoid a duplicate log entry — the local bubble + log already showed it when you sent.
  • Peer chat bubbles unchanged (still drawn above peer ghosts by _mpDrawPeers).

📢 Surface

  • Bottom controls strip now lists Enter Chat alongside the other toggles.
  • Multiplayer modal hint mentions the 60-char cap and that chat works offline.
  • Input placeholder updated: "Say something… (max 60 chars · Enter send, Esc cancel)".

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: #mp-chat-input maxlength 200 → 60 + new placeholder; player literal gains _chat; Enter gate changed from net.connected to player.cls && player.hp > 0; _mpSendChat() rewrites to cap 60 + always set player._chat + always log + conditionally send over WS; _mpHandle('chat') suppresses own echo; drawClassIdentityHUD adds the local chat-bubble draw + decay next to the emote block; Multiplayer modal + bottom controls copy updated.
  • Save-compat: yes. No schema changes. _chat is runtime-only.

v0.24.2 Dev cheat · Gate levelup · Multishot cap · U-panel Skills tab · F no portal

Quality-of-life patch: press 8 for a dev XP burst, level-ups throttle to one at a time, the Double Shot boon caps at +1, unequipped boons shrink into compact chips, the Skills Reference merges into the U panel with per-slot growth charts, the I key retires, and F stops triggering portals (↑ still does).

✨ Press 8 — dev XP cheat

  • Grants ~40% of next-level XP per press. A few presses crosses a level; combined with the new level-up gate below, this stays grindy even with the cheat.
  • Retired the 💤 sleep emote to free the 8 key. Emotes are now 4 😊 / 5 😲 / 6 😂 / 7 😢.

🚦 One level per trigger

  • Level-up loop changed from while to if — one level per kill / trigger max.
  • Any overflow XP beyond the next level is clamped to 95% of the new expToNext, so huge XP drops don't chain multiple levels but still leave you close enough to trigger again next kill.
  • Level-up logic extracted into _maybeLevelUp() so the press-8 cheat, kill rewards, and future XP sources share the same animation + advancement check path.

🎯 Double Shot capped at +1

  • Boon template max dropped from 2 to 1 — each rolled instance grants exactly +1 projectile.
  • Even if multiple Double Shot boons are equipped, _applyEquippedBoons() hard-clamps player.mods.multishot to 1. No more +3 projectile stacks.

◈ Boon Loadout — compact unequipped chips

  • Equipped boons keep the full card with rich violet border + box shadow + full action row.
  • Unequipped boons collapse to a single-line chip: icon + name + roll + 🎲 reroll + ✕ discard + Equip. Much denser — the whole 25-boon bag fits in the same scroll area.
  • Fewer pixels per boon, more room for the grid.

📖 Skills Reference → U panel Skills tab

  • Added a third tab in the U panel: 📈 Level Up · ◈ Boon Loadout · 📖 Skills.
  • Shows your current class's full binding table (Z/A/X/S/C/D/F/V/G).
  • New: per-slot growth chart. Each row gets a horizontal Lv 1 → 50 track showing:
    • Gold ▼ marker at the slot's unlock level
    • Green "you" marker at the player's current level
    • Green shaded band from unlock onward (available range)
    • Tick labels: Lv 1 · Lv 25 · Lv 50
  • Locked slots (no job / no master yet) grey out with an explanation of what's needed.
  • Old standalone Skills modal path removed; openSkillsReference() now just opens U at the Skills tab for back-compat with any external caller.

⌨ I retired

  • The I key no longer has a binding — the Skills Reference moved into the U panel (same content, better layout, shared tab navigation).
  • Help panel + README updated.

🚪 F no longer enters portals

  • tryInteract() drops the portal fallback. F now only opens chests / picks up drops / casts the job-signature skill. Use ↑ to enter portals.
  • Stops the "I pressed F next to an NPC and got warped somewhere" problem.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: emote map removes 8 → sleep; new 8 branch grants XP burst; _maybeLevelUp() extracted and gated to one level per call with overflow clamp; POWERUPS.multi max 2→1; _applyEquippedBoons multishot clamp; renderBoonPanel splits equipped / unequipped rendering; renderSkillsReference(host) renders inline + adds per-slot Lv 1→50 growth chart; U panel gains Skills tab + tri-pane swap; I-key branch removed; help panel + bottom-bar references updated; tryInteract drops portal fallback.
  • README.md: controls table simplified to merge K/U Character panel.
  • Save-compat: yes. Old characters with multishot > 1 from past saves get clamped to 1 on next _applyEquippedBoons.

v0.24.1 MMORPG balance · Mastery · Cel-shaded UI · Map depth

Retunes the game for MMO rhythm (tiered XP, death penalty, tighter potions, quadratic rerolls), adds a per-mob Mastery grind, a cel-shaded HP/MP/EXP bar refresh, a reorganised Level-Up panel, moves the player nameplate below the character, and drops a new furthest-mountain layer + god rays + cinematic vignette into the map backdrop for cleaner parallax depth.

Retunes the game for a long-haul MMORPG rhythm — steeper endgame XP curve, real death penalty at higher levels, tighter potion economy, quadratic boon rerolls, and a new per-mob mastery grind that rewards farming specific foes. On the UI side, HP/MP/EXP bars get a cel-shaded glow-up and the Level Up panel gets a full layout refresh.

📈 Endgame XP curve (tiered)

  • Lv 1-29: ×1.18 per level (unchanged — same onboarding rhythm).
  • Lv 30-39: ×1.22 per level (noticeably longer).
  • Lv 40-49: ×1.26 per level (real endgame wall).
  • Net effect: Lv 40 → 50 now takes roughly as much XP as Lv 1 → 39 combined. Classic MMO "last ten levels are the grind" feel.

💀 Death XP penalty (Lv 20+)

  • Lv 1-19: no XP loss. Early game stays forgiving.
  • Lv 20-29: 3% of current-bar XP lost on death.
  • Lv 30-39: 5%.
  • Lv 40+: 8%.
  • Capped at the current bar so you never drop below the level. Shown on the death overlay alongside the existing 50% Lumen loss.

💰 Economy tightening

  • Potion prices +40% — healing is now a Lumen decision, not a freebie.
    • Red Potion: 60 → 85 · Orange Potion: 180 → 250 · Pure Water: 500 → 700
    • Blue Potion: 80 → 115 · Mana Elixir: 220 → 310 · Elixir (full): 900 → 1250
  • Boon rerolls are now quadratic — 500 + rerolls² × 200. 1st costs 500, 2nd 700, 3rd 1300, 4th 2300, 5th 3700, 6th 5500. Chasing a god-roll is a meaningful sink.

⭐ Mastery — per-monster farming grind

  • Every kill of a non-boss mob increments player.mastery[type]. Thresholds grant permanent damage bonuses vs that mob type:
    • 100 kills → +1% damage · ★
    • 500 kills → +2% damage · ★★
    • 1000 kills → +3% damage · ★★★
  • Milestones toast with the mob's name when you cross a threshold.
  • Mastery is applied in hitMonster — stacks cleanly on top of boons, buffs, crits, and class-identity multipliers.
  • Saved per character. Builds up over every run, creating long-term "I'm better at fighting Pincers than Rotters" investment.

🩸 Cel-shaded HP / MP / EXP bars

  • Bars got a chunkier silhouette — crisp black outline, inner highlight band on the top 30%, shadow band on the bottom 35%.
  • Fill gradient now uses a stepped two-tone cel shade instead of a soft linear blend. Reads as a toon element, not a window UI.
  • Label text gets an 8-direction outline stroke for contrast on any background.

📊 Level-up panel refresh

  • Big glowing SKILL POINTS pill at the top of the Level Up tab, counter in oversized gold.
  • Each lane card now shows an icon (❤/💧/⚔/🛡/✦/⚡) in the lane's signature colour, clean progress track, and a per-state footer (+ Invest / MAXED / Not enough SP).
  • Hover states — affordable lanes lift + glow in their own colour. Maxed lanes turn green. Locked lanes grey out.
  • Same radar chart + stat summary + Boon Loadout tab underneath; just the lane grid got re-styled.

📛 Player nameplate below the character

  • The MMO-style floating name now sits below the player's feet instead of above the head. Follows the sprite through jumps / movement.
  • The Lv N suffix is gone from the nameplate — level already lives in the top-left HUD, no need to duplicate it in world space.
  • If no name is set, the nameplate doesn't draw at all (used to always show at least the level).

🏔 Map background — deeper parallax

  • New furthest-mountain layer behind everything: muted, barely parallaxes (0.015× camera), paints atmospheric depth on every outdoor map.
  • God rays on bright maps — soft diagonal sunbeams streaming from the celestial disc area. Additive, subtle, gone on moonlit maps.
  • Cinematic vignette — radial darkening toward the corners on combat maps. Focuses the eye on the action and makes the four layers of parallax read cleanly. Disabled in town so the village stays cozy.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: level-up loop tiered curveMul; triggerDeath XP penalty + overlay copy; POTION_ITEMS price +40%; boonRerollCost quadratic; player.mastery field + killMonster tracking + hitMonster bonus + PLAYER_SAVE_FIELDS adds mastery; .bar / .bar-fill cel-shade CSS; .lu-card CSS + renderLevelUp rewrite with icon + colour per lane; _drawPlayerNameTag now renders below the sprite without Lv suffix; drawBackground adds furthest mountain + god-ray + vignette passes.
  • Save-compat: yes. Missing mastery on old saves defaults to {}.

v0.24.0 Multiplayer — real WebSocket server

First step toward a real MMORPG. A Node.js WebSocket server lives in server/; the client gets a 🌐 Multi button, presence tick, ghost-peer rendering, emote relay, and in-world chat. Everyone on the same room name sees each other run around and can chat. Combat / mobs stay per-client for this milestone — that's authoritative-lite, not full MMO.

server/ — Node.js WebSocket relay

  • Single-process server.js using ws. HTTP wrapper so /health returns version + room/player counts for load balancers.
  • Room-based — any unique room id, default lobby. 16 players per room hard cap, 60 s idle kick, 40 ms per-player state-tick floor, 200-char chat cap, control chars stripped.
  • Protocol: hello / state / chat / map / emote (client → server); welcome / joined / left / state / chat / emote / error (server → client). All JSON. Full table in server/README.md.
  • No database, no auth, no persistence — rooms die when the last player leaves.
  • Deployment: Dockerfile included, Fly.io / Railway / VPS instructions in server/README.md. Fly's free tier covers a single small instance.

Client — net module

  • 🌐 Multi button top-right of the HUD opens the multiplayer modal. Fields: server URL, your name, room id. All three persist in localStorage.
  • Presence tick — _mpTick() runs after updatePlayer and sends a state frame every 70 ms (~14 Hz): x/y/vx/vy, facing, map, hp/mp, level, cls/job/master, anim.
  • Peer rendering — _mpDrawPeers() draws each peer in the current map as a translucent violet silhouette with name + level + HP bar above their head. Chat + emote bubbles float above them.
  • Emote relay — pressing 4-8 emotes to everyone in the room.
  • Chat — press Enter while connected to open a bottom-left input. Enter sends, Esc cancels. Messages show as speech bubbles above the sender for 4 s and in a rolling log of the last 30 lines.

What it IS

  • Presence + chat across the room — friends running around in the same map.
  • Per-map scoping — peers on different maps are hidden.
  • Full stat broadcast — HP, MP, level, class, advancement all mirror to peers.
  • Free to run locally or on any tiny VPS / Fly.io / Railway instance.

What it is NOT (yet)

  • Not authoritative combat. Every player instances their own mobs.
  • No shared loot, no trade, no party XP, no PvP.
  • No accounts / persistence. Reconnect = new id.
  • No anti-cheat — server trusts client state. Fine for co-op, not competitive. Server-side combat is the next phase.

Run it

cd server
npm install
npm start
# [levelx-server] listening on port 8080

Click 🌐 Multi in the game, enter ws://localhost:8080, pick a name + room, hit Connect. Share the URL + room with a friend.

Smoke test

  • Verified: client connects, receives welcome with id, second client joins, state frames round-trip, chat echoes to sender, joined/left notifications flow. Console clean of errors.

Touched surface

  • New files: server/server.js, server/package.json, server/Dockerfile, server/README.md, server/.gitignore.
  • maple_game.html: multiplayer modal + button + chat input/log markup + CSS; net module (connect/disconnect/tick/handle/send/chat/emote/draw); closeAllModals includes multiplayer-modal; chat input wired on DOMContentLoaded; _mpTick called in main loop; _mpDrawPeers called in render pass; Enter opens chat when connected; emote keys relay to peers.
  • Save-compat: yes. Multiplayer is opt-in; offline play is unchanged.

v0.23.1 Sniper X/F swap · Piano BGM · Skill-gate tune · Rogue nerf · `-` toggles advance

Combined follow-up patch covering five small adjustments: the Sniper X→F skill swap, piano-classical BGM, skill-unlock levels dropped by 1, rogue Momentum halved, and a new - key to toggle the job-selection page.

🏹 Sniper X / F swap

  • Sniper X (slot s): reverts to MultiShot (the archer default). The old Railshot on X was too punishing at Lv 5 — instant piercing line with escalating damage dwarfed every other class's early game.
  • Sniper F (slot q): now Railshot. Same effect, costs climb to signature tier. MP 16 → 28, CD 1300 ms → 4200 ms.
  • Strafe Volley retired (SKILL_FN kept as dead code; no skill references it).

🎹 Piano-classical BGM

  • Six tracks rewritten as soft chord arpeggios in minor / major keys. Tempos 420-520 ms/beat.
  • All leads + basses switched to sine waveforms for a piano-adjacent fundamental.
  • Each note now layers a quiet (~22%) octave overtone for a warm "bell" body that pushes sine closer to a real piano partial.
  • Envelope changed to piano mode: 20 ms attack, slow decay to 38% of peak across the note body, soft release past the end — legato / sustain-pedal feel.
  • Track volumes trimmed ~15% so the music sits behind SFX.

📉 Skill unlock levels — all −1

Each skill-slot gate moved down one level so unlocks land on clean multiples of 5.

  • X 6 → 5, S 11 → 10, C 16 → 15, D 21 → 20, F 26 → 25 (aligned with 1st advancement), V 31 → 30, G 50 → 49.
  • Job advancement stays at Lv 25, master at Lv 50 — unchanged. The slot-level changes just bring the availability in at the "0-of-5" boundary instead of "1-of-5".

🗡 Rogue Momentum halved

  • Momentum's damage-bonus cap dropped from +100% → +50% (formula: 1 + m/200 instead of 1 + m/100).
  • Build rate / decay rate unchanged; only the output multiplier is halved.
  • Rogue base crit (25%) + crit damage + mobility still make them a glass-cannon class; this just prevents the 2× Momentum × full-crit combos from one-shotting zodiac bosses.
  • Class-select identity tooltip updated to reflect the new cap.

⌨️ - toggles the job / master selection page

  • Press - any time (with a class picked) to open the advancement modal. Press again to close.
  • If you don't have a job yet, this presents the 1st-advancement picker. If you already have a job + master, it lets you re-pick both so commitments aren't permanent.
  • Separate from 0, which remains the Lv-50 dev max-out cheat.

🗝️ N also opens treasure chests

  • N is now a context-aware interact key: chest → NPC → Codex.
    • If you're standing on a treasure chest, N opens it.
    • Otherwise, if an NPC is in range, N starts their dialog.
    • Otherwise, N opens the Codex.
  • The in-world chest prompt now reads [N] Open.
  • F still works for chests via the legacy tryInteract path, so muscle memory holds.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: SLOT_LEVEL_REQ values −1 across the board; SKILLS.deadeye removed + SKILLS.snipe_railgun moved to slot q with MP/CD bumped; MUSIC_TRACKS rewritten with piano flag + sine waveforms; music._tone piano-mode envelope + octave overtone; _computeClassSkillMul rogue branch changed to 1 + m/200; CLASSES.rogue.identity.desc updated; keydown handler adds - branch for advancement toggle.
  • Save-compat: yes.

v0.23.0 Skill cadence · Epic class-select · Balance pass

Two small follow-ups. The Sniper's X goes back to the archer default (MultiShot) because Railshot was too strong for an early-cadence slot; Railshot is promoted to the F job-signature slot, displacing Strafe Volley. Separately, the map BGM gets a soothing piano-classical rework — all tracks use warm sine fundamentals with a quiet octave overtone, slower tempos, and longer legato envelopes.

🏹 Sniper X / F swap

  • Sniper X (slot s): reverts to MultiShot (the archer default). The old Railshot on X was too punishing — instant piercing line with escalating damage at Lv 6 dwarfed every other class's early game.
  • Sniper F (slot q): now Railshot — same effect, but the cost / cooldown climb to the job-signature tier. MP 16 → 28, CD 1300 ms → 4200 ms. Still powerful, but budgeted like Shadow Strike / War Cry / Smoke Bomb.
  • Strafe Volley is retired (the SKILL_FN stays in the file as dead code; no skill definition points to it any more).
  • Net effect: Sniper's early game plays closer to the base archer feel, then Lv 26 unlocks the screen-clearing Railshot as their defining signature.

🎹 Piano-classical BGM rework

  • All six tracks rewritten as gentle chord arpeggios in minor / major keys:
    • Town — C-major pastoral lullaby at 480 ms/beat
    • Forest — A-minor → C-major overworld at 440 ms/beat
    • Mushroom — D-minor contemplative at 520 ms/beat
    • Boss — C-minor dramatic but calm at 420 ms/beat
    • Zodiac — A-minor → C-major cosmic at 500 ms/beat
    • Tower — G-major ascending reverent at 460 ms/beat
  • Sine waveforms everywhere for lead + bass — the piano fundamental. Square / sawtooth / triangle retired from music (still used for SFX).
  • Quiet octave overtone layered on every piano note at ~22% amplitude — gives the sine a warm "bell" body closer to a real piano partial.
  • Longer envelope — 20 ms attack, slow decay to 38% of peak over the note body, soft release past the note end. Creates the legato, sustained feel of a pianist holding the sustain pedal.
  • Tracks opt in via piano: true on the track object. SFX unaffected — only music._tone() checks the flag.
  • Volumes trimmed ~10-20% across the board so the music sits behind sound effects without competing.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: SKILLS.deadeye removed, SKILLS.snipe_railgun slot moved from s to q with MP/CD bumped; MUSIC_TRACKS fully rewritten with piano: true + sine waveforms + chord-arpeggio phrasing; music._tone gained a piano-mode envelope + octave overtone.
  • Save-compat: yes. Sniper characters that had Railshot bound to X will find it on F after load; MultiShot takes X automatically via skillBySlot's class fallback.

v0.23.0 Skill cadence · Epic class-select · Balance pass

Major progression + balance rework. Skills unlock every 5 levels instead of all at once. Job advancement moves to Lv 25, master to Lv 50. The class-select page is fully reskinned with animated cosmos rays, per-class glow, and dramatic taglines. Mage basic spells get proper recast cadence, rogue F goes purple-and-black, and every skill takes a global 20% haircut for balance.

📜 Skill cadence — one slot every 5 levels

  • New constant SLOT_LEVEL_REQ:
    • A Block/Parry — Lv 1 (always)
    • Z basic — Lv 1
    • X skill 2 — Lv 6
    • S skill 3 — Lv 11
    • C skill 4 — Lv 16
    • D skill 5 — Lv 21
    • F job signature — Lv 26 (also requires job advancement)
    • V job ultimate — Lv 31 (also requires job)
    • G master signature — Lv 50 (also requires master)
  • Advancement levels: 1st job → Lv 25 (was 10). Master → Lv 50 (was 20).
  • isReady(id) now checks the slot's level requirement. The skill bar greys out gated slots and shows "Lv N" in the MP line until unlocked.
  • The Warrior charge-hold, archer hold-to-draw, and the poll-cast loop all pass through isReady so level-gated slots don't fire.
  • 0 dev key now snaps you to Lv 50, auto-advances to the first job + first master, and grants the missed HP/MP/ATK/DEF and 49 SP. Use for quick testing.

📈 XP curve + rewards

  • XP growth softened from ×1.30 per level to ×1.18 per level. Reaching Lv 50 is now realistic under the 5-level cadence.
  • Monster XP rewards globally +25% to keep the climb from feeling longer than the old Lv 1 → 30 experience.
  • Prestige offer bumped from Lv 50 → Lv 60 since 50 is now the master gate.

⚔ Epic class-select page

  • Backdrop: radial purple gradient with a slowly spinning conic-gradient ray field (cs-rays) and twinkling star-dust layer (cs-stars).
  • Title: "⚔ THE SHARDFALL EXPEDITION ⚔" subline in letter-spaced violet, plus a pulsing gold "Choose Your Hero" headline that breathes every 2.4 s.
  • Per-class colour variables (--cls-color, --cls-glow, --cls-shadow) drive a radial-gradient wash that fades in on hover + a hover scale-lift + class-coloured box-shadow.
  • Dramatic taglines under each class name:
    • Warrior — "Strike first. Strike hard. Bear the burden."
    • Rogue — "The shadow falls before the blade."
    • Mage — "Speak the word. Reshape the world."
    • Archer — "A breath. A heartbeat. An arrow."
  • Advancement levels surfaced in the header copy ("First Advancement at Lv 25, Mastery at Lv 50") so players know the new pacing up front.
  • Modal grows up to max-height: 94vh with inner scroll to accommodate the longer content on smaller viewports.

◈ U-key panel: tabbed layout

The combined Level Up + Boon Loadout panel was too tall to fit on a typical viewport. Now split into two tabs inside the same modal:

  • 📈 Level Up — SP radar + lane grid + current-stats summary. Radar dropped 280 → 220 px, lane grid is now 2-column, stats inline.
  • ◈ Boon Loadout — equipped slot row + inventory grid + reroll/discard controls. Same UI as before, now on its own tab.
  • Tab state (game._uTab) persists across opens.
  • Modal body has max-height: 88vh + scroll fallback so even monster-sized inventories fit.

🔮 Mage base CDs

  • Z Magic Bolt — 210 ms → 300 ms
  • X Fireball — 800 ms → 1 000 ms
  • S Ice Spike — 650 ms → 2 500 ms
  • Cleaner cadence distinction between the three basics — bolt spam, fireball punch, ice spike as a deliberate cast.

💜 Rogue F recoloured (purple + black)

  • Shadow Strike (ninja F): pink/magenta particles swapped to #1a0230 deep black, #7722aa royal violet, and #b866ff amethyst.
  • Smoke Bomb (assassin F): cloud recoloured from grey to #0c0118 / #5a1a8a / #9a66cc. Plays as an obsidian smoke rather than dust.
  • Matches the rogue class fantasy — proper assassin palette.

⚡ Nightreaper G — Blink Barrage (rework)

The old Ricochet Daggers was serviceable but not memorable. The new master signature is the signature zip-zap.

  • Scan all visible mobs, mark up to 14. Rogue dissolves, then blink-strikes each mark at 65 ms cadence — blindingly fast.
  • Each strike ignores DEF, always crits, deals ATK × 2.2 × critDmg, and leaves a 10-point violet afterimage trail showing the path between strikes.
  • Alternates flanks (left / right) of each target for readable rhythm.
  • 2.4 s invulnerability blanket across the entire barrage — no interrupt damage.
  • Finale: a twin-crossed slash (violet + deep purple) + 240 px shadow nova at the landing point, 650 ms stun on everything caught, +18% max HP heal on exit.
  • MP 25 → 55, CD 6.5 s → 15 s. Fits the master-ultimate cost bracket (Voidrift / Divine Aegis / Gale Storm).
  • Whiffs cleanly with partial MP refund if nothing's on screen.

💢 Global damage balance knob

Added a single tuning constant in hitMonster so the whole roster can be rebalanced at once.

  • GLOBAL_SKILL_DMG_MUL = 0.80 — blanket 20% nerf on all non-basic skill damage.
  • GLOBAL_ULT_DMG_MUL = 0.75 — additional 25% trim on master ults (they stack with the skill nerf, netting 60% of the old damage).
  • ULT_SKILL_TAGS set lists which skill tags are considered ultimates (earthbreaker, deathBlossom, phantom_nova, sage_meteor, arrowRain, etc).
  • Basic attacks (melee / arrow / dagger / bolt) keep full damage — their tempo is already balanced by the new cooldown cadence.
  • Thorns / burn DoT also pass through unmodified.
  • Monsters got a +25% HP bump in v0.20 + new slower class-identity gating; the 20%/25% nerfs are calibrated so skill-to-basic damage ratios stay roughly where they were, just with less one-shot-ultimate drama.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: new SLOT_LEVEL_REQ / JOB_ADVANCE_LEVEL / MASTER_ADVANCE_LEVEL / GLOBAL_SKILL_DMG_MUL / GLOBAL_ULT_DMG_MUL / ULT_SKILL_TAGS constants; isReady() + slotLevelReq(); hitMonster() nerf block; level-up loop bumps to 25/50 + new 1.18× curve; mob-kill XP gets +25% multiplier; 0 keydown branch rewritten as Lv-50 cheat; openLevelUpPanel() split into tabs; CLASSES gets tagline field on each class; renderClassCards() wires per-class CSS vars; SKILLS.magicBolt / fireball / iceSpike cooldowns; SKILLS.nightreaper_mark rename + stat tweak; SKILL_FNS.shadowStrike + smokeBomb recolours; SKILL_FNS.nightreaper_mark full rewrite; skill-bar _sbBuild + live renderer show level locks; class-select HTML + CSS.
  • Save-compat: yes. Existing characters see the new skill cadence immediately based on their current level.

v0.22.0 MapleStory nostalgia pack — Emotes · Chat · Tabs · Music

Four features pulled straight from the MapleStory feel-book: emote speech bubbles on number keys, idle chatter over mobs and NPCs, a proper five-tab inventory, and synthesized chiptune music per map. All Web-Audio / Canvas — still single-file, still no binary assets.

😊 Emotes (4-8)

  • 4 😊 smile  ·  5 😲 shocked  ·  6 😂 laugh  ·  7 😢 cry  ·  8 💤 sleep
  • Pops a rounded speech bubble above the player's head for ~2 seconds with a tiny pointer tail.
  • Fades out over the last 400 ms.
  • Doesn't pause the game, doesn't cost MP, doesn't interrupt combat. Pure flavour.

💬 Chat bubbles — mobs + NPCs

  • Every monster rolls a chatter timer every 8-25 seconds with ~40% chance to speak. Bubble sits for 2.2 s. Per-type phrase pools (snails go "zzz..." / "slippery!", zombies "braiiins" / "ughh", wraiths "oooo~" / "fade...", etc).
  • NPCs idle-chatter every 12-30 seconds with their role-specific lines (Elspeth: "Fresh potions!", Brok: "Clang! Clang!", Amnesiac: "...who...", Sage Mira: "The boons await", etc).
  • NPC chat hides when the player stands next to them — the [N] Talk prompt takes priority.
  • Bubbles draw outside the squash/stretch transform so they stay upright when the mob wobbles.
  • Shared _drawBubble() helper powers emote + mob + NPC bubbles with a consistent pill + tail look.

🎒 Inventory tabs (5-tab layout)

  • ⚔ Equip — weapons, armour, accessories. The default tab. Click items to equip/unequip.
  • 🧪 Use — potions and throwables. HP/MP potions now display as stacked icons with ×N counts in the top-right of each cell. Click to consume.
  • 📦 Etc — crafting materials and quest items. Empty for now; populates as future drops land.
  • 🪑 Set-Up — chairs, mounts, pets. Reserved bucket for future features.
  • ✨ Cash — cosmetic-only items. Reserved for event rewards.
  • Active tab highlighted in gold. Equip slots dim to 55% opacity on non-Equip tabs (still visible — you know what's worn).
  • Item classification helper _itemTab(it) routes existing inventory items into the right bucket based on slot, type, and a few opt-in fields (cosmetic, chair, etc).
  • Active-tab state (game._invTab) persists while the modal is open so you don't get bounced back to Equip after clicking a potion.

🎵 Web-Audio music per map

Short looping monophonic-lead + monophonic-bass chiptunes synthesized in Web Audio. Zero sample files, zero download cost.

  • 6 tracks, one per map archetype: town, forest, mushroom, boss, zodiac, tower.
  • Each track defines lead + bass patterns as [note, beats] tuples with per-track tempo (180-300 ms per beat) and waveforms (triangle / square / sawtooth / sine).
  • Short envelope on each note — quick attack, gentle decay, soft release — for a gameboy-advance chip feel.
  • Scheduler uses audio.ctx.currentTime with a 600 ms look-ahead; re-arms every 150 ms. Seamless loop at the end of the pattern.
  • loadMap(id) automatically swaps to the new track. Maps starting with zod_* all share the Zodiac mystical-triangle theme.
  • M mute / unmute now also pauses the music cleanly. Unmuting resumes the last-played map's track.
  • Music fails gracefully if the audio context isn't yet initialised (browser autoplay policy) — first user gesture activates it.

Track vibes at a glance

  • Town — C-major pastoral triangle lead over sine bass. Warm, friendly, Henesys-adjacent.
  • Forest — D-minor adventurous square lead, driving tempo. Classic overworld.
  • Mushroom / Fungal — A-minor sawtooth lead, sparser bass. Slightly eerie, inviting-creepy.
  • Boss — C-minor square lead over sawtooth bass. Fast tempo, tense. Reserved for Jelly King / Momma Shroom / Aetherion / Gravitos arenas.
  • Zodiac — A-minor triangle lead over sine bass. Mystical, contemplative. Every zodiac arena.
  • Tower — C-major ascending square over triangle bass. Climbing rhythm, carriage-of-ascension feel.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: player literal gains _emote; keydown handler gets the 4-8 emote block; _tickClassIdentity decays the emote timer; drawClassIdentityHUD renders the emote bubble; new _mobChatTick / _drawMobChat helpers + MOB_CHAT_LINES + NPC_CHAT_LINES pools + _drawBubble shared renderer; updateMonsters calls _mobChatTick; monster render loop calls _drawMobChat; drawNPCs gets NPC chatter + near-player suppression; inventory HTML gets a 5-button tab bar + #inv-tabs / #inv-tab-info elements + .inv-tab CSS; renderInventory() rewritten as a tab-filtered renderer; _itemTab(it) classifier; new MUSIC_TRACKS + MAP_MUSIC + _mapTrackId + music object with play / stop / _schedule / _tone; loadMap calls music.play; audio.toggleMute pauses/resumes music.
  • Save-compat: yes. No schema changes. game._invTab defaults to equip on load.

v0.21.2 Class Identity unlocked from Lv 1

Charge & Release (Warrior), Momentum (Rogue), Chain Cast (Mage), and Rooted Fire (Archer) are now available the moment you pick a class — no more waiting until Lv 10 to feel your class's signature mechanic.

What changed

  • _classIdentityActive() now returns true as soon as player.cls is set, instead of requiring both player.cls and player.job. The charge-hold, momentum gauge, chain-cast detection, and archer draw/steady all light up immediately.
  • Mage crit CDR refund (every crit shaves 150 ms off all other cooldowns) no longer gates on job advancement either — base Mages can start feeling the rotation pressure from their first kill.
  • Class-select cards — the identity block on each class card dropped the "From Lv 10:" prefix so the pitch reads as a day-one feature.

Why

The Lv 10 gate was originally a design hedge — we wanted the job-advancement to feel like a meaningful milestone. In practice it made the first 10 levels feel generic: all four classes basically chose which basic animation to watch. Opening the mechanics from Lv 1 means a fresh Warrior can hold a skill and feel the charge ring; a Rogue sees their momentum bar climb; a Mage gets rewarded for cycling through basic skills; an Archer learns to plant their feet before a shot. The learning curve matches the moment-to-moment gameplay.

Balance note

No damage numbers were adjusted. The charge at +100% is still +100%; momentum still caps at +100%; chain still empowers to 1.5×; archer draw still caps at +140% with full Steady. Mobs haven't been re-tuned — the difficulty bump in v0.20 already assumed these mechanics were in play.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: one-line change in _classIdentityActive(), one condition removed in hitMonster (mage CDR refund gate), four description strings in CLASSES.
  • Save-compat: yes. No schema changes.

v0.21.1 Modal toggle — press same key to close

Every pop-up panel is now dismissible three ways: the same key that opened it, the ✕ button, or Esc. Previously only B (inventory) and Esc closed — pressing K/U/I/N/? again did nothing.

What changed

  • K / U — toggle the Level Up panel.
  • I — toggle the Skills Reference card.
  • N — toggle Codex (or the NPC dialog when one is in range).
  • ? / / — toggle the Help panel.
  • B already toggled (via toggleModal); unchanged.
  • Esc and the ✕ close buttons continue to close via closeAllModals(); unchanged.

Bonus: variant swap on shared modal

The Level Up panel and Skills Reference share the same attributes-modal container. The new toggleSharedModal(id, variant, openFn) helper tracks which variant is currently rendered via modal.dataset.variant:

  • Press K with nothing open → opens Level Up (variant lp).
  • Press I while Level Up is showing → content swaps to Skills Reference (variant skills).
  • Press K again → swaps back to Level Up.
  • Press the key that matches the CURRENT variant → closes the modal.

No accidental close when you're swapping between the two panels.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: new toggleModalOrOpen() + toggleSharedModal() helpers next to toggleModal(); keydown branches for K/U/I/N/? updated to call the toggles.
  • No changes to closeAllModals(), the ✕ buttons, or Esc handling — those paths already worked.
  • Save-compat: yes. No schema changes.

v0.21.0 Accuracy · Archer Z aim · MISS rolls

Three linked combat changes. The Archer's Z basic no longer auto-repeats on hold — each press fires one arrow, and damage scales with Steady Aim so patient shots hurt. A new Accuracy stat drives a real miss-roll against monster Evasion, and the gap between the two matters: if your accuracy is too far below a target's evasion, you'll watch "MISS" float over their head.

🏹 Archer Z — aimed single shot

  • Edge-triggered. Holding Z no longer auto-spams arrows. Each arrow is one press. The auto-cast poll skips arrowShot for archers; a dedicated keydown handler fires on the down-edge only.
  • Steady Aim now empowers the shot. Standing still builds Steady stacks (0 → +40%). Each Z press consumes most of the stacks for a bigger arrow: +damage, faster velocity, less drop, brighter tracer. Fire-and-reposition.
  • High-Steady shots (≥ 35% stacks) get a louder flash + extra muzzle sparks so you can see the "aimed shot" land.

◎ Accuracy & Evasion

A new combat axis. Basic attacks (sword / arrow / dagger / bolt) now roll against a monster's evasion — if your accuracy is too low, the attack misses outright and floats "MISS" in grey.

  • getAccuracy() — class-based floor plus AGI, equipment, and boon contributions:
    • Archer: 130 base (highest — class fantasy)
    • Rogue: 110 base
    • Warrior: 100 base
    • Mage: 90 base (weakest basic-hit accuracy — mages lean on AOE)
    • +1.5 per AGI point, +steady×0.9 (archer only), + equipment accuracy, + Eagle Eye boon
  • Hit-chance formula: chance = clamp(0.15, 1, 1 − (evasion − accuracy) / 150). If accuracy ≥ evasion you always hit; each 150 points of gap drops hit chance by 100% (floored at 15% so high-evasion foes aren't un-hittable).
  • Skill AOEs always connect — only melee / arrow / dagger / bolt tags roll accuracy. Earthbreaker, Meteor Shower, Aegis, Bloodwave, etc. bypass the check so big MP/CD casts never whiff to RNG.
  • Thorns and burn DoTs also bypass accuracy.
  • U panel now shows your Accuracy value next to the other derived stats.

Monster Evasion table

Every monsterType now declares an evasion value. Elite variants +20%, mini-bosses +40%. Tower floors add up to +100% evasion at high floors.

MobEvasionNotes
Slippy (snail)40Slow, easy target
Jelly (slime)50Bounces a bit
Shroom55Pops spores
Horncap75Fast-ish
Sunbun85Hoppy
Stumpy60Slow but tough
Rotter100Mid evasion
Pincer (scorpion)130Speed 1.7 — very elusive
Wrappy (mummy)90Shambles
