Gravitos (hyperboss)210Even light falls
Zodiac bosses140 + order×8Aries 148 → Pisces 244

🦅 New boon — Eagle Eye (Accuracy)

  • Rolls +15 to +45 Accuracy per boon. Rerollable like any other.
  • Maps to the new player.mods.accuracy stat. Summed across equipped boons.
  • Essential if you're fighting zodiac bosses or hyperbosses on a low-AGI warrior / mage.

Balance implications

  • A warrior with default 5 AGI has 107 accuracy. Hits snails always. Hits Pincer (ev 130) at ~85% rate. Hits Pisces (ev 244) at ~15% (miss floor). Needs Eagle Eye boons or high-AGI AP investment to reliably land basics on endgame zodiac bosses.
  • An archer with 30 AGI + full Steady + 1 Eagle Eye boon can push accuracy to ~220, reliably landing on Pisces.
  • Skills (powerStrike, groundSlam, all job / master ults) are untouched — they still always connect. Only the basic-attack chip damage respects evasion.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: new getAccuracy() helper next to getEvasion(); new _rollAccuracyHit() + BASIC_HIT_SKILLS set; miss check at top of hitMonster; monsterTypes gain evasion field; zodiac registration loop adds evasion; spawnMonster scales instance evasion for elite / mini-boss / tower; player.mods gains accuracy; POWERUPS gains acc (Eagle Eye); renderLevelUp shows Accuracy in the stats line; poll loop skips archer slot-d auto-cast; keydown handler adds archer Z edge-trigger; arrowShot SKILL_FN gains Steady damage scaling + cash-out.
  • Save-compat: yes. Existing characters gain accuracy on next getAccuracy() call. Missing evasion field on monsters defaults to 40 (snail-tier) via fallback.

v0.20.1 Sniper F → Strafe Volley

Sniper's job signature (F) was "Deadeye" — a single guaranteed-crit piercing shot. It's now Strafe Volley: a sideways hop + three piercing arrows fired in rapid succession on different vertical lanes.

Strafe Volley

  • 3 piercing arrows fired at 0 ms / 60 ms / 120 ms — reads as a rhythmic bang-bang-bang burst.
  • Lane stagger: Arrow 1 angles high, Arrow 2 flies dead-straight, Arrow 3 angles low. Covers grouped enemies at different heights.
  • Sideways hop on cast: the sniper strafes backwards away from the facing direction with a small vertical lift. Gives the "strafe-fire" silhouette. Skipped if the cast came from a hold-to-draw release (the draw flow already positions the archer).
  • 260 ms invulnerability during the volley so you don't eat a swing to the face mid-burst.
  • Damage: 1.55× ATK + 12 per arrow. Three arrows = ~4.65× ATK total — comparable to the old single Deadeye but spread across 3 hits for cleave potential.
  • MP 22 → 26, CD 3.5 s → 3.8 s (tiny uptick for the added utility).
  • Works with the archer's hold-to-draw — hold F, charge the draw, release to fire the empowered volley.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: SKILLS.deadeye rename ("Deadeye" → "Strafe Volley") + MP/CD tweak, SKILL_FNS.deadeye rewritten as a 3-arrow staggered volley with sideways strafe hop + muzzle flashes per arrow.
  • Keeps the skill id deadeye for save-compat — no schema change.

v0.20.0 Archer charge · Boon bag cap · Harder mobs

Four linked changes tightening the economy and class balance. The Archer now holds to draw (like the Warrior), the Warrior's full charge loses its free crit, the Boon bag caps at 25 so overflow has to be discarded, and every combat mob tier got a difficulty bump to catch up with stronger players.

🏹 Archer — hold-to-draw

  • Holding a skill key now charges a draw meter (same timing as the Warrior — ~0.75 s to full) while the archer's feet are forced still. Release fires the skill.
  • Damage scales multiplicatively with hold time: tap = 1×, half-hold = 1.5×, full draw = 2×. Steady Aim stacks (max +40%) still add on top, so full draw at max Steady caps at +140% damage.
  • No more auto-root on skill cast. Tap-fired skills keep the archer mobile. The old 0.4 s post-cast freeze was removed — if you want bonus damage, commit to the hold.
  • Visual: green-tinted charge ring (vs the Warrior's orange), foot-bracket indicators at the ground, "🏹 LOOSE" prompt at 100%.

⚔ Warrior — full-charge crit guarantee removed

  • Full-charge releases still double damage (up to +100%) but no longer auto-crit. Crits are earned through Crit %, Sharp Eye boons, Crit Damage stacking, and skill tree nodes.
  • This was a small but meaningful nerf — a full charge on a class with 5 stacked boons was hitting for absurd numbers with the free crit. Stays impactful, no longer silly.

◈ Boon bag cap at 25

  • New cap: BOON_INVENTORY_CAP = 25. You can own at most 25 rolled boons. Equip cap of 5 is unchanged.
  • Bag-full behaviour: when the bag is full, orb pickups / Sage buys / level-up rewards toast "Boon bag full — discard one first (press U)" and the new boon is not consumed. You don't lose the opportunity — you just can't hoard indefinitely.
  • Loadout UI now shows N / 25 in bag with a color that shifts orange → red as you approach the cap, plus a "Bag 100% full" footer when at cap.
  • Discarding already existed per-boon (red Discard button with confirm dialog). No UI changes needed — just make room.

💢 Difficulty rebalance

Class identity multipliers and stacked boon rolls pushed player power too high — fights outside bosses felt trivial at Lv 20+. Monster tiers rebalanced to restore tension:

TierHPATKExamples
1 (early)+15%+10%Slippy · Jelly · Shroom
2 (mid)+25%+15%Horncap · Sunbun · Stumpy
3 (late)+35%+20%Rotter · Wrappy · Bones · Pincer · Spook
Bosses+30%+15%Jelly King · Momma Shroom · Aetherion · Gravitos
Zodiac+30%+15%All 12 zodiac bosses
  • XP / Lumen drops scale up alongside HP so grind time stays roughly constant despite tankier foes.
  • Elite / mini-boss multipliers (×3 / ×5 HP, ×1.5 / ×2 ATK) unchanged — they compound on top of the new base stats automatically.
  • Player-side damage math untouched — you keep every multiplier you had; fights just aren't over in one charged Power Strike anymore.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: monsterTypes (all tiers + zodiac registration), _computeClassSkillMul (warrior no-crit, archer charge formula), tryStartWarriorCharge / tryReleaseWarriorCharge renamed to tryStartClassCharge / tryReleaseClassCharge with back-compat aliases, _tickClassIdentity (archer root-during-hold), drawClassIdentityHUD (archer charge ring + foot brackets), acquirePowerup (bag cap gate), renderBoonPanel (N/25 header), CLASSES identity copy.
  • New constant: BOON_INVENTORY_CAP = 25.
  • Save-compat: yes. Existing characters retain all boons in their bag (no saved characters had more than 25).

v0.19.1 Bloodlust rework · Phantom ultimate

Two skill surgeries. Bloodlust stops being a passive ring and becomes an active amplifier for basic attacks. Phantom's ultimate goes from a single teleport-slash to a cinematic chain-execution on up to 6 marked targets.

🩸 Berserker — Bloodlust (nerfed + reworked)

The old 10 s auto-shockwave ring felt "cast and ignore" — you popped it and the game played itself for 10 s. Now the buff rewards active swinging.

  • No more auto-shockwave ring. The 400 ms projectile ring-of-10 that auto-fired for 10 s is retired.
  • Z basic attacks launch forward shockwaves while Bloodlust is active. Every basic swing spits out a getAtk() × 0.9 + 4 shockwave that pierces in the facing direction. Player-driven damage, not passive.
  • Duration trimmed 15 s → 12 s. On-cast heal / MP refund trimmed 25% → 20%. Cooldown shortened 20 s → 18 s to compensate.
  • Net effect: Bloodlust damage now depends on how fast you're swinging. Rewards aggression; no free DPS from standing still.

👻 Phantom — Voidrift Execution (new ultimate)

The old Dimensional Cut was one teleport-strike for ATK × 4 — punchy but short. The rework turns it into Phantom's signature multi-target execute.

  • Marks up to 6 nearest enemies in 900 px. Each mark gets a floating violet sigil.
  • Chain-teleports through every mark at 110 ms intervals — rogue flashes from target to target on alternating flanks, leaving a shadow trail.
  • Each strike ignores DEF, always crits, and hits for getAtk() × 3.2 × critDmg. Execute fodder: dead targets are skipped so the chain doesn't waste on corpses.
  • Final mark triggers a shadow nova at the rogue's landing point — 220 px radius, ATK × 2 + 20 to every mob caught, 700 ms stun, violet explosion rings + radial spokes.
  • Survival reward: +15% max HP heal after the nova fires. 2.2 s invulnerability blanket during the full chain.
  • If no enemies are in range → whiffs gracefully with a 30 MP refund instead of consuming full cost.
  • Cost rebalanced: MP 30 → 55, CD 7.5 s → 14 s. Bigger, slower, defines the class.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: SKILLS.bloodlust def (duration / CD / desc), SKILLS.phantom_cut def (name "Voidrift Execution" / MP / CD / desc), SKILL_FNS.bloodlust simplified, SKILL_FNS.slash gains the Bloodlust shockwave rider, SKILL_FNS.phantom_cut rewritten as a 6-strike chain + nova, old _bloodstorm tick in updatePlayer reduced to a back-compat drain.
  • No gameplay data lost on old saves — player._bloodstorm still exists but emits nothing.
  • Save-compat: yes.

v0.19.0 Equippable Boons + Lumen Rerolls

Power-ups, Sage Mira's purchases, and every other boon source now drop rolled instances that the player has to equip. Up to 5 boons can be active at once; the rest wait in inventory. Each boon has a rolled stat value within a range — spend Lumens to reroll for better stats.

What changed

  • Boons now roll stat values. Every boon template (Iron Muscles, Lifesteal, Sharp Eye, etc.) has a [min, max] range. Acquisition rolls once; e.g. Iron Muscles rolls +8% ATK to +22% ATK. What you get is random, but you can reroll.
  • Equip cap of 5. You own as many boons as you want; only 5 can be active at a time. Orb pickups / level-up picks / Sage buys auto-equip when a slot is open and sit in inventory otherwise.
  • Press U for the new Loadout panel. Shows 5 equipped slots at the top, full inventory below. Each card has Equip / Unequip / Reroll / Discard buttons. Rerolls cost 500 Lumens base (+250 per previous reroll on the same boon) and shuffle the roll within the boon's range.
  • Old saves migrate automatically. Legacy player._powerups (array of boon ids) gets converted on load: each old powerup becomes a rolled instance with a median roll, auto-equipped up to the 5-slot cap. No player action needed.
  • Sage Mira's shop still sells a random boon for 1 500 Lumens — but now the boon drops into inventory instead of auto-applying. Spend more Lumens to reroll it if the stat is bad.
  • Level-up boon picks show the actual rolled value on each card so the choice isn't blind. Pick the one whose roll landed best in the range.

Under the hood

  • POWERUPS is now a data schema (stat, min, max, fmt, scale). The old apply() functions were removed — stats are derived via scale(roll) and summed in _applyEquippedBoons().
  • player.boons holds instances {id, roll, rerolls}; player.boonsEquipped is an array of inventory indices (max BOON_EQUIP_CAP = 5).
  • player.mods is now purely derived — _applyEquippedBoons() wipes it and re-sums every equipped boon's contribution, gated by stat key. Called on equip, unequip, reroll, discard, and on load.
  • Helpers: rollBoonInstance, getBoonDef, formatBoon, boonRerollCost, equipBoon, unequipBoon, rerollBoon, discardBoon, _migrateLegacyPowerups.
  • UI: new renderBoonPanel() slots into openLevelUpPanel() below the radar chart. Equipped-slot grid (5 cells) + inventory grid (auto-fill) with inline Equip / Unequip / Reroll (cost pill) / Discard buttons.
  • Save: boons and boonsEquipped now in PLAYER_SAVE_FIELDS. Legacy _powerups kept in save list so migration has something to read; it's deleted by the migrator.

Balance notes

  • Old cap was 8 total / 3 same-type, all always-active. New cap is 5 active with no same-type limit (you can equip three Iron Muscles if you have three of them — just takes three of your five slots).
  • Reroll curve: first reroll 500💰, second 750💰, third 1 000💰, fourth 1 250💰, etc. No upper bound — chasing god-rolls is an intended Lumen sink.
  • Legacy saves get median rolls ((min+max)/2) so post-migration power is close to pre-migration with no RNG penalty on existing players.

v0.18.0 Class Identity — four distinct playstyles

Every class now plays meaningfully differently after job advancement (Lv 10+). Existing skills stay the same — a new mechanical layer wraps around them so how you cast starts to matter as much as what you cast.

⚔ Warrior — Charge & Release

  • Hold a skill key to charge. A ring fills around the warrior over ~0.75 s. Release fires the skill with up to +100% damage.
  • At 100% charge: guaranteed crit + hit-stop + screen shake + orange particle burst. Toast reads "⚔ EMPOWERED".
  • Quick-tap (<120 ms) casts at minimum charge — normal damage.
  • Charge cancels if you get stunned or die. Auto-cast polling is suppressed while a key is held, so you don't accidentally spam the skill.
  • Applies to every warrior skill except basic attack — X S C D F V G all support charging.

🗡 Rogue — Momentum

  • Moving builds a gauge (0-100). Running full-tilt fills it in ~1 s. Standing still drains it faster than it builds.
  • Skills spend most of the gauge (−60) for up to +100% damage. A full-gauge cast is a massive burst.
  • Visible as a thin purple bar above the rogue that brightens to pink near 100%.
  • Rewards hit-and-run / corridor-running play. Standing still to channel skills gives 0 bonus.
  • Quick-dash, rush, and dodge roll all count as movement for gauge purposes.

🔮 Mage — Chain Cast

  • Cast two DIFFERENT skills within 1 s → the second one deals 1.5× damage. A floating "⌬ CHAIN" indicator appears above the mage after the first cast so you know the window is live.
  • Every crit shaves 150 ms off every other skill's cooldown. Mage perks already give 30% CDR; this stacks on top — critting into a rotation feels like the cooldowns evaporate.
  • Gated to once per frame so a single AOE tick can't reset everything.
  • Rewards spell-rotation play instead of spamming one nuke.

🏹 Archer — Rooted Fire

  • Casting a skill freezes the archer in place for ~0.4 s (forces vx = 0, gravity still applies). In exchange you get +25% damage.
  • Standing still builds Steady Aim — stacks climb +0.25/frame up to +40% damage. A "◎ AIM +N%" label appears above the archer.
  • Moving horizontally at any speed breaks Steady instantly.
  • Skill damage formula while rooted: base × (1.25 + steady/100). Max boost: +65%.
  • Rewards planting your feet and actually aiming — suits the class fantasy of a sniper who can't move-and-shoot.

How it works under the hood

  • New module CLASS IDENTITY near castSkill. Each class has a _tickClassIdentity pass per frame and a _computeClassSkillMul hook called before every skill effect runs.
  • Central damage multiplier on player._classSkillMul with a 2-second expiry window, so delayed projectiles / tethered volleys from the same cast still pick up the bonus.
  • Applied in hitMonster for non-melee / non-thorns / non-aegis hits.
  • All four states (_warCharge, _momentum, _steady, _rootedTimer, _mageLastCastT) are cleared on death, respawn, loadMap, and loadState. No leaking between runs.
  • Class-select cards gained a new purple ◈ Identity block under the perk describing the mechanic.
  • Save-compat: yes. No schema changes. An existing Lv 20 character gains their mechanic immediately on load.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: CLASSES (identity copy), player literal (init fields), castSkill (pre-cast hook), hitMonster (multiplier + mage crit refund), updatePlayer (tick + charge polling suppression), keydown/keyup (warrior start/release), triggerDeath + respawnAtTown (state clear), render pass (drawClassIdentityHUD), class-select card markup.
  • Version bumped to v0.18.0.

v0.17.3 Talk moves to N

Small but annoying conflict: F used to be both "Talk to NPC" and "Job signature skill" (slot Q). Pressing F next to an NPC would open their dialog and cast a skill in the same frame. Talk is now on N; F is reserved for chest / pickup / Job signature.

What shipped

  • N is the primary Talk key. If an NPC is within 60 px of the player, N opens their dialog; otherwise it opens the Codex (achievements + bestiary). Context-aware — one key, two meanings, no conflict.
  • F no longer doubles as Talk. Still opens chests, picks up drops, and casts the Job Signature (Q-slot) skill — which was the original intent of the key. Pressing F near an NPC will continue to talk via the existing tryInteract chest/portal/NPC fallback, so muscle memory isn't broken, but the primary affordance is now N.
  • In-world prompt updated. Floating NPC label now reads [N] Talk instead of [F] Talk.
  • Help panel + Skills Reference updated. The ? Menus & Items column now lists N Talk to NPC / Codex and F Open Chest / Pickup. The I-key Skills Reference card describes the new context-aware N binding.
  • Mobile deck button repurposed. The 💬 bubble button at the bottom-right of the mobile controller now dispatches N instead of F, so mobile players get the same context-aware Talk / Codex behaviour.
  • README Controls table now documents N = Talk / Codex and F = Open chest / Pickup, with a footnote explaining the context-aware behaviour and the legacy F talk fallback.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: keydown handler for N (context branch), drawNPCs prompt label, help panel markup, Skills Reference row for N + F, bottom-bar controls pill, mobile deck button, version bump to v0.17.3.
  • README.md: Controls → UI & utility section updated.
  • No game logic changes beyond the keybind remap. Save-compat: yes.

v0.17.2 Onboarding hotfix

Six small fixes pulled out of a headless-browser playthrough. All new-player friction — wrong docs, invisible zodiac portal, hostile entry spawns, dailies that require items a fresh character doesn't have.

What shipped

  • README keybind table rewritten to match KEY_TO_SLOT. Previously said D was basic attack — actually Z is basic attack and D casts War Cry (7 s CD). Every skill key was shifted. The table is now split into Movement / Combat / UI sections with an explanatory line about the left-hand cluster layout (Z X S C D F V G).
  • Zodiac Sanctum visual cue. The Zodiac portal shares an x-coord with The Amnesiac, so its purple swirl was completely hidden behind the cottage. Added a floating 8-point zodiac sigil (pulses, rotates, orbits 3 sparkles) above the Amnesiac's cottage roof, plus a "ZODIAC SANCTUM" banner that appears when the player is within 200 px. Portal hitbox unchanged — the sigil is pure visual advertisement.
  • HUD label LP: → SP:. Matches the standard MMO convention for Skill Points. Tooltip added so players know what it spends on. Carried through to the Level-Up panel copy and the Skills Reference card.
  • Stuck input on map change. loadMap now clears game.keys and player.lastTapKey. Previously, if a key was physically down during a portal transition, its keyup often never reached the window after the swap — leaving game.keys['arrowup'] true, which caused ghost movement / repeated portal attempts / phantom skill casts on the new map. Paired with cancelPendingSkillTimers() from v0.17.1 — same principle, clear transient state on transition.
  • Forest entry safe zone. On combat maps, mobs that spawned within 240 px of the entry point are now pushed deeper into the map (max 320 px clearance). Fixes the Lv 1 "lose 40% HP before the first swing" issue in Emerald Thicket where the default entry x=160 overlapped a 5-mob cluster. Boss arenas and the tower are exempt — they deliberately spawn close.
  • Daily Challenge pool gated by level. Added minLv on each challenge. Lv 1-5 rotates through three beginner-friendly ones (Defeat 10 enemies, Visit 3 different maps, Talk to 3 different NPCs); Lv 6+ unlocks the old kill 50 / combo 30 / open 3 chests set; Lv 15+ unlocks enhance an item / reach Lv 25. Tracking for visit/talk uses per-day sets so revisits don't re-count. Fixes the Lv 1 "Enhance any item once" first-impression where new players have no weapon and no enhancement stones.

Touched surface

  • README.md: Controls section rewritten into Movement / Combat / UI tables.
  • maple_game.html: HUD SP label, drawNPCs (zodiac sigil), loadMap (input clear + forest entry buffer + visit tick), openChest + openNPC (daily hooks), DAILY_CHALLENGES + _pickDailyChallenge + tickDaily.
  • Version bumped to v0.17.2.
  • No combat-math changes. No skill-tree changes. Save-compat: yes.

v0.17.1 Code-health hotfix

Five surgical bug fixes pulled out of a 3-agent parallel audit. No gameplay changes — purely stops ghost effects from lingering past death, kills an infinite-buff exploit, and flattens the per-frame particle cost.

Bugs fixed

  • Ghost Bloodlust / Aegis / Clones after death. triggerDeath() and respawnAtTown() now null out player._bloodstorm, player._bloodstormNextTick, player._aegis and player._clones. Dying mid-ultimate no longer leaves shockwaves / hovering orbs / shadow clones firing on the corpse through the death screen.
  • Mute state desync. audio.muted is now the single source of truth. saveState() mirrors it into game.muted only at serialize-time; toggleMute() no longer writes to two places. Reload-while-muted no longer drifts.
  • Infinite-buff save/reload exploit. loadState() now zeros every player.buffs.* timer and every transient combat flag (invulnerable, rushTimer, dodgeTimer, _aegis, _clones, _pendingTimeouts) after the Object.assign. Previously: pop Bloodlust → refresh browser → 15 s buff persists forever.
  • Queued skill ticks surviving the player. New scheduleSkillTimer() + cancelPendingSkillTimers() wrapper. All 29 setTimeout call-sites inside SKILL_FNS now register their id into player._pendingTimeouts. Death, respawn, and map transitions clear the queue. A 7-strike volley mid-cast no longer keeps detonating on an empty arena after you die or portal out.
  • Per-frame particle O(n²). The particle / damage-number update loops previously did splice(i, 1) per expired entry — O(n²) in bursty frames. Replaced with a single-pass write-index compactor (O(n)). The overflow-cap still drops oldest-first via splice(0, excess), but only in frames that actually overflow.

Touched surface

  • maple_game.html: audio block, player literal, loadState / saveState, triggerDeath / respawnAtTown, loadMap, updateParticles, SKILL_FNS (29 setTimeout swaps).
  • Version bumped to v0.17.1.
  • No asset, controls, or balance changes. Save-compat: yes.

Documentation shareable

Gaming-psychology audit + phased roadmap

Added GAMING_AUDIT.html — a self-contained, dark-themed audit doc designed to be shared with collaborators. Covers a 12-lever psychology scorecard, cross-confirmed gap analysis from three parallel codebase audits, and a ROI-ranked roadmap (Phase 1 quick wins · Phase 2 structural · Phase 3 big bets) with code anchors into maple_game.html. The doc is an audit only — no gameplay changes yet.

Auto-pull SessionStart hook

Added .claude/hooks/session-start.sh + .claude/settings.json so every Claude Code session begins with a git fetch origin and a fast-forward / rebase of the current branch onto origin/main. Prevents drift against a human collaborator's pushes. Opt out per-session with CLAUDE_DONT_PULL=1. Always exits 0 so it never blocks a session; handles dirty tree, detached HEAD, fetch timeout, and rebase conflicts gracefully.

Mobile-branch hooks — auto-rebase before push + zone guard (branch mobile-ui-pass only)

Two new PreToolUse / PostToolUse hooks scoped to the mobile-ui-pass branch so the mobile UI pass can run in parallel with gameplay work on main without late-stage merge pain:

  • Pre-push auto-rebase (.claude/hooks/mobile-pre-push.py). When Claude is about to run git push on mobile-ui-pass, the hook fetches origin/main and rebases first. Blocks the push with a clear conflict list if the rebase collides; exits clean (hook skipped) if the working tree is dirty or the branch is already up-to-date.
  • Zone guard (.claude/hooks/mobile-zone-check.py). After every Edit / Write / MultiEdit on maple_game.html, the hook computes the changed hunks' line ranges and flags any that fall outside the mobile "safe zones" (7–10, 33, 65–322, 472–593, 1135–1155, 1464–1500, 3317–3744). Warning only — never blocks. Safe-zone list documented in CLAUDE.md.

Both hooks no-op on branches other than mobile-ui-pass, so they're safe to keep registered in .claude/settings.json.

How to try it

git fetch origin main
git switch main
open maple_game.html

Or drop the file into any static server / preview. No install step.

Verification checklist

  1. Save. Pick a class, reach level 2, kill a mob, refresh. Expect Welcome back! toast + same level / mesos / map (you'll land in town).
  2. Audio. Hit a mob → tick. Land a crit → bright two-tone. Level up → 3-note rise. M toggles mute.
  3. Daily. Banner top-right shows progress. Complete the challenge → reward toast.
  4. Codex. Press N — 12 achievements, live kill count, best combo. Kill the first mob → First Blood unlocks.
  5. Respec + Reset. Open attributes (U). Respec refunds AP + wipes milestones. Reset (red button) wipes the whole save.
  6. Prestige. Dev console (hold 1+2+3) → set level 50 → kill a mob → ascend prompt. After: L1 with permanent ×1.3 XP / ×1.3 DMG.
  7. Combos. Farm a weak mob past 50 / 100 / 150 hits — three escalating buffs.
  8. Juice. A 500-damage crit should be visibly huge; rare drops glint, legendary drops explode. Aetherion and Gravitos phase shifts hit-stop the frame.
